</s>
<s> Đến thăm , không cần tìm hỏi tôi cũng nhận ra cái khoảng tối đen giữa những căn nhà sáng_rực ánh điện , nhấp_nháy đèn màu , là nhà chị .
</s>
<s> Đốm sáng duy_nhất là một cây nến cháy leo_lét , hắt quầng sáng vàng_vọt xuống trang nhật_ký chị đang nắn_nót viết .
</s>
<s> Khi sáng , lúc gặp chị ở sân tòa_án , thất_thần với quyết_định phúc_thẩm bắt_buộc phải trả lại nhà cho chủ , tôi đã không_thể tưởng_tượng được căn nhà mà chị bảo là mồ_hôi_nước_mắt của hai vợ_chồng lại thê_thảm đến thế .
</s>
<s> Nhìn bên ngoài có_thể thấy cái đà ngang đã nứt võng xuống như sắp gãy đôi .
</s>
<s> Nhìn bên trong không thấy gì ngoài sự bề_bộn , rách_nát .
</s>
<s> Ấy vậy_mà căn nhà ấy chị cũng không được trú_chân nữa , nhưng câu_chuyện của chị lại còn buồn hơn cả căn nhà .
</s>
<s> Chị Hòa có năm con thì cả năm chỉ có lớn mà không có khôn .
</s>
<s> Vừa rẽ vào ngõ đã gặp mấy người có dáng_vẻ đàn_ông , đàn_bà ngồi ngẩn_ngơ , lê_la với mấy cái chai , mảnh nhựa nhặt được .
</s>
<s> Đấy là con của chị đang đợi mẹ về cho ăn , chờ mẹ về cho tắm .
</s>
<s> Ông chồng vì quá thất_vọng với những núm ruột của mình đã bỏ vợ , bỏ con .
</s>
<s> Một_mình chị Hòa vào bệnh_viện làm_thuê , đi lượm ve_chai , lên tận Nông_trường Lê_Minh_Xuân nuôi vịt , trồng rau_muống ... để có tiền mua gạo .
</s>
<s> " Chỉ mong có được chén cơm , phải tự_nguyện cắt điện , cắt nước vì không có tiền trả " .
</s>
<s> Những tâmsự thật đắng lòng : " Hằng với Ti gây_lộn , làm khổ mẹ quá .
</s>
<s> Mình điên hay con mình điên ?
</s>
<s> Khóc mãi , khóc suốt đêm cũng không hiểu được điều gì sẽ xảy đến ngày_mai ...
</s>
<s> Mình ăn , ở sao cũng được , chỉ cầu_mong con mình có chén cơm , có chỗ chui_ra_chui_vào tránh nắng_mưa ... " .
</s>
<s> Khách đến , chị tìm một băng ghế đặt trước cửa nhà vì bên trong không có chỗ nào để ngồi .
</s>
<s> Chị kể về lần phải chạy xuôi_ngược khắp xóm vay tiền để đăng tin " tìm trẻ lạc " .
</s>
<s> Thành_phố giải_phóng , nhà thay_đổi chủ , gia_đình chị vẫn lầm_lũi sống cho đến khi chủ mới hoàn_tất thủ_tục chủ_quyền , bắt_đầu đòi nhà .
</s>
<s> Xin hợp_thức_hóa thì đuối lý , muốn mua lại thì không tiền , ra tòa hai lần chị thất_thểu ra về với vai_trò người thua cuộc .
</s>
<s> Chị Hòa đã gửi rất nhiều những lá đơn xin một căn nhà tình_thương , nhưng chị chỉ nhận lại nhiều quyết_định cưỡng_chế thi_hành án .
</s>
<s> Một trong những lá đơn của chị đã đến với chúng_tôi .
</s>
<s> Chúng_tôi đang suy_nghĩ , biết thế , chị lại quay sang an_ủi chúng_tôi : " Thôi , thế_nào chị cũng tìm được cách , như thuê một mảnh ruộng trồng rau nuôi mấy đứa .
</s>
<s> Mưa từ trên trời mưa xuống mà ... " .
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Đổi lòng hoạn_thư : Từ cuộc điện không lời thoại .
</s>
<s> Lần đầu_tiên công_ty thám_tử được tiếp một khách_hàng có thái_độ vui_vẻ , nhẹ_nhàng như chị Thư .
</s>
<s> Bởi chuyện của Thư cũng rất nhẹ_nhàng và chẳng nên chuyện tí nào .
</s>
<s> Phía sau chuẩn_mực .
</s>
<s> Đó là cách đây ba hôm , khoảng 8 g 30 tối , hai vợ_chồng Thư đang đọc sách và xem tivi thì chuông điện_thoại reo .
</s>
<s> Nhưng khi chị thưa thì đầu dây bên kia có tiếng " dạ " đứt_quãng rồi im_lặng không trả_lời .
</s>
<s> Giọng khó đoán nam hay nữ , trẻ hay già .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ họ không nhầm máy vì sau mấy lần Thư hỏi thì người đó mới dập máy .
</s>
<s> Chỉ thế thôi .
</s>
<s> Thư muốn các thám_tử theo_dõi xem anh Nhu , chồng chị , có bồ_bịch hay quan_hệ bí_ẩn nào không .
</s>
<s> Thư đoán là không , bởi 20 năm từ khi yêu nhau đến khi thành vợ_chồng , Nhu chưa bao_giờ có tình_ý thậm_chí thái_độ cợt_nhả với người đàn_bà nào .
</s>
<s> Nhu là một nhà_khoa_học có chí , có tài , nổi_tiếng chung_thủy , chỉn_chu , nghiêm_túc và mẫn_cán trong gia_đình , cơ_quan và khu_phố .
</s>
<s> Vợ_chồng chị cũng chưa từng một lần mặt_nặng_mày_nhẹ với nhau .
</s>
<s> Hạnh_phúc ấy Thư xứng_đáng được hưởng vì chị là một cán_bộ nhà_nước , có trình_độ .
</s>
<s> Gái Hà_Nội nhưng chữ công_dung_ngôn_hạnh ít người bì kịp .
</s>
<s> Dường_như chị đến công_ty thám_tử là để tham_quan .
</s>
<s> Thám_tử Toàn được giao ảnh , địa_chỉ nhà , cơ_quan anh Nhu để theo_dõi .
</s>
<s> Toàn thật nhàn vì Nhu cứ ăn sáng ở nhà với vợ xong mới đến cơ_quan .
</s>
<s> Tám ngày liền như_vậy , hợp_đồng của Thư tưởng như chấm_dứt thì buổi chiều định_mệnh ập đến .
</s>
<s> Ban_đầu là một đoàn khách của cơ_quan Nhu đến .
</s>
<s> Nhu đi cùng đoàn tiếp khách .
</s>
<s> Nửa bữa , Nhu xin_phép về trước .
</s>
<s> Toàn theo Nhu đến ngã ba và định bỏ về thì anh giật_mình : Nhu không rẽ về nhà .
</s>
<s> Người đàn_ông đó bất_ngờ phóng như ma đuổi , len_lách vào các ngõ tắt , đường ngang với thái_độ bất_thường .
</s>
<s> Nơi Nhu dừng xe là một quán nước gần công_viên Lênin .
</s>
<s> Chừng 5 phút thì một cô gái trẻ , ăn_mặc gọn_gàng , bịt khăn , đội mũ đi vượt lên phía trước và hơi ngoái đầu ra_hiệu với Nhu .
</s>
<s> Nhu phóng xe lên , rồi cả hai hối_hả tiến ra ngoại_ô .
</s>
<s> Toàn lập_tức chạy vào đăng_ký thuê phòng .
</s>
<s> Anh phát_hiện : chiếc chìa_khóa cô gái cầm theo mang số 205 .
</s>
<s> Lửa hận .
</s>
<s> Bình_thường thì các thám_tử tránh thông_báo tức_thời địa_chỉ của đối_tượng cho thân_chủ trong những vụ ngoại_tình như_thế_này .
</s>
<s> Nhưng vì Toàn tin Thư là người dịu_hiền , có văn_hóa và đủ bản_lĩnh kiểm_soát hành_vi , cảm_xúc của mình nên đã báo cho Thư .
</s>
<s> Thư hơi hụt giọng nhưng vẫn ôn_tồn hứa với Toàn sẽ không đến nhà_nghỉ đó và cũng không nặng_lời với chồng .
</s>
<s> Chị đi một_mình và tiến thẳng vào lễ_tân xin thuê phòng .
</s>
<s> Thư lên phòng 205 gõ_cửa và nói vọng vào với Nhu là vợ đến .
</s>
<s> Cô gái lao vào trốn trong buồng tắm .
</s>
<s> Nhu mặt cắt không còn hạt máu đổ gục cả thân_xác to_lớn xuống chân vợ .
</s>
<s> Thư kéo ghế ngồi điềm_tĩnh đến lạnh người .
</s>
<s> Mắt Thư sắc buốt như dao , mặt tím thâm lại trong hai hàm_răng nghiến bạnh quai_hàm .
</s>
<s> Cái duyên_dáng , nhu_mì bỗng tiêu_tan thay bằng những tiếng rít ghê như rắn .
</s>
<s> Chị gọi cô gái trong buồng tắm ra , nói ăn_mặc chỉnh_tề và ngồi xuống cạnh Nhu .
</s>
<s> Thư yêu_cầu hai người viết giấy nhận tội quan_hệ bất_chính , vi_phạm Luật hôn_nhân gia_đình .
</s>
<s> Họ khai : cô gái tên Liên , 25 tuổi , chưa chồng , gia_đình ở Hà_Nội , trình_độ đại_học , đang làm_việc tại một cơ_quan_hành_chính .
</s>
<s> Họ đã quan_hệ với nhau năm năm nay và hoàn_toàn vì tình_yêu .
</s>
<s> Cả hai cam_kết chấm_dứt quan_hệ vĩnh_viễn .
</s>
<s> Họ cùng phải ký và điểm_chỉ vào bản nhận tội .
</s>
<s> Xong việc Thư đạo_diễn cho hai người ôm nhau tình_tứ , cúi đầu nhận tội và cùng ký giấy , điểm_chỉ để Thư chụp ảnh .
</s>
<s> Gấp tờ giấy , cất máy_ảnh , Thư điềm_nhiên xuống lễ_tân trả tiền và tươi_cười nói là người mình hẹn không đến được .
</s>
<s> Thám_tử Toàn ở phòng bên cạnh chứng_kiến từ đầu đến cuối và không_thể phản_ứng gì .
</s>
<s> Nhưng mọi chuyện không dừng ở đó .
</s>
<s> Một người đàn_ông đến công_ty thám_tử hỏi xem có phải vợ mình đã thuê công_ty này theo_dõi ông_ta không !
</s>
<s> Người đàn_ông này chính là Nhu , chồng Thư .
</s>
<s> Nhu kể : sau sự_cố đó cuộc_sống gia_đình vẫn bình_yên .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện không hề rò_rỉ ra ngoài .
</s>
<s> Nhưng Thư không_thể lấy lại được thăng_bằng và Nhu biết vợ mình đang âm_thầm tìm cách trả_thù Liên .
</s>
<s> Nhất_là Liên lại sắp lấy chồng ...
</s>
<s> Nguyên_tắc của công_ty là tuyệt_đối giữ bí_mật cho khách_hàng và không bao_giờ chống lại khách_hàng .
</s>
<s> Vì_vậy Toàn cũng không xác_nhận Thư đến thuê thám_tử và cũng không ký hợp_đồng với Nhu .
</s>
<s> Cuộc thương_thảo chấm_dứt .
</s>
<s> Nếu có một hậu_quả không lành nào đó xảy ra , Toàn sẽ thấy mình có lỗi bởi anh đã cho Thư biết địa_chỉ của nhà_nghỉ mà Nhu - Liên đang ở .
</s>
<s> Công_ty thám_tử chấp_nhận cho Toàn đơn_phương theo_dõi Thư để hóa_giải nguy_cơ xấu .
</s>
<s> Ngày_mai Toàn phải là người tháo ngòi_nổ của quả bom này sao cho không một ai phải mang thương_tích .
</s>
<s> Kỷ_niệm 59 năm ngày thành_lập Công_an nhân_dân .
</s>
<s> Họ đã sống vì sự bình_yên của nhân_dân .
</s>
<s> Và họ đã góp_phần không nhỏ cho sự bình_yên của TP này .
</s>
<s> Những chuyện " nhỏ " ...
</s>
<s> Để giới_thiệu Trần_Ngọc_Đoàn - 27 tuổi , trinh_sát của phòng cảnh_sát hình_sự , anh Thành_Bỉ dẫn_chương_trình giao_lưu đã mở_đầu : " Có một vụ án vào một thời_khắc anh phải có_mặt ngay để phá_án , nhưng cũng vào thời_khắc ấy cha của anh đang thập_tử_nhất_sinh , cần có_mặt anh bên cạnh và anh đã phải gác chuyện riêng ... " .
</s>
<s> Cả hội_trường đã chìm trong im_lặng .
</s>
<s> Đoàn cũng xúc_động không kém khi anh bồi_hồi kể lại thời_khắc của vụ án ấy .
</s>
<s> Đoàn đã vào vai một thanh_niên ăn_chơi để tiếp_cận với khoảng 20 gái mại_dâm .
</s>
<s> Nhưng chứng_cứ thu_thập được vẫn còn mỏng , phải làm_sao để bắt quả_tang việc giao_nhận tiền giữa các " trùm " trong đường_dây này .
</s>
<s> Đêm ấy , mọi việc đã được sắp_xếp ...
</s>
<s> Trong khi đang dồn hết_mình cho việc phá_án thì cha của Đoàn phải vào bệnh_viện cấp_cứu vì cao huyết_áp .
</s>
<s> " Tôi vào bệnh_viện trong tâm_trạng rất lo_lắng .
</s>
<s> Nếu ở lại với cha thì cơ_hội phá_án sẽ qua đi , còn đi phá_án nếu chẳng may ...
</s>
<s> Tuy_nhiên , cha tôi đã động_viên và tôi gác chuyện riêng lên_đường " , Đoàn bộc_bạch .
</s>
<s> Ngay trong đêm ấy , Đoàn cùng đồng_đội đã bắt quả_tang và đưa hàng chục tên tội_phạm ra ánh_sáng .
</s>
<s> Đoàn bảo : " Đây chỉ là một chiến_công nhỏ so với các bậc đàn_anh trong phòng cảnh_sát hình_sự , nhưng đã động_viên tôi rất nhiều " .
</s>
<s> Cũng với suy_nghĩ ấy , Phạm_Ngọc_Thăng - điều_tra_viên trẻ của phòng cảnh_sát điều_tra - kể về những cuộc đấu_trí căng_thẳng và phức_tạp khi đối_diện với những thủ_đoạn tinh_vi , xảo_quyệt của bọn tội_phạm , để tìm cho được chứng_cứ trong vụ phá đường_dây làm giấy_phép lái_xe giả .
</s>
<s> " Công_việc chỉ luôn đối_diện với hồ_sơ , giấy_tờ và tội_phạm , anh có cảm_thấy buồn không ? " , anh Thành_Bỉ hỏi .
</s>
<s> Thăng chững_chạc trả_lời : " Khi đã khoác trên mình màu áo công_an nhân_dân thì không phải là vui hay buồn nữa mà là nghĩa_vụ và trách_nhiệm , thậm_chí là niềm tự_hào trong công_việc " .
</s>
<s> Giống như điều Thăng vừa tâm_sự , chiến_sĩ đội cảnh_sát chống tội_phạm ma_túy LBKT Công_an quận 1 RBKT 24 tuổi Đặng_Văn_Cự cũng từ niềm tự_hào của màu áo công_an nhân_dân , đã không ít lần được khen_thưởng đột_xuất vì phá vỡ nhiều tụ_điểm mua_bán cái_chết_trắng .
</s>
<s> " Tham_gia bắt tội_phạm ma_túy , anh có cảm_giác thế_nào khi chứng_kiến những người cùng trang_lứa phạm_tội ? " , một bạn trẻ hỏi .
</s>
<s> " Tôi thấy đau_lòng .
</s>
<s> Số bạn trẻ vướng vào ma_túy đã tự làm mất đi tuổi_trẻ của mình " , Cự nói .
</s>
<s> Nghệ_sĩ hài Trung_Dân đặt câu hỏi với trung_úy Trần_Thanh_Nguyên , đội_trưởng đội cảnh_sát phòng cháy chữa_cháy LBKT Công_an Bình_Thạnh RBKT : " Để cứu người , cứu tài_sản , ngoài trách_nhiệm phải có lòng dũng_cảm nữa .
</s>
<s> Bạn đã lăn_xả thế_nào khi một vụ cháy xảy ra ? " .
</s>
<s> Nguyên kể về vụ cháy tại khoa thí_nghiệm Trường đại_học y_dược TP_._HCM .
</s>
<s> Hôm đó , Nguyên cùng một đồng_đội đi làm một nhiệm_vụ khác thì bất_ngờ thấy khói bốc lên cao ở khu_vực Trường đại_học y_dược .
</s>
<s> " Linh_tính nghề_nghiệp mách_bảo tôi chắc cháy lớn nên chúng_tôi phóng ngay đến hiện_trường " .
</s>
<s> Nguyên phân_công anh bạn đồng_nghiệp ở vòng ngoài bảo_vệ , còn mình leo lên lầu của khu_vực cháy để cứu người và chữa_cháy .
</s>
<s> Nguyên vừa trấn_an vừa hướng_dẫn những sinh_viên còn kẹt trên lầu đi xuống .
</s>
<s> Sau đó xé áo bịt mũi và miệng để vào sát ngọn lửa .
</s>
<s> Khói mịt_mù , Nguyên phải dùng tay và chân đập bể các cửa_kính cho khói thoát ra ngoài ...
</s>

</s>
<s> Mối quan_hệ đôi bên bây_giờ tồn_tại bởi hai sợi dây .
</s>
<s> Thứ nhất : tình_cảm hai người đang êm_đẹp và không ai có_thể tự tuyên_bố cắt bỏ mà không có tác_động lớn nào xen vào .
</s>
<s> Thứ hai , dù_sao Lan cũng đang trông vào trợ_cấp của Nam .
</s>
<s> Nhi muốn họ lìa nhau theo ý của chị : tuyệt_đối không đi_lại với nhau và đứa con của Lan sẽ không được công_nhận trước pháp_lý là con của Nam .
</s>
<s> Tức_là mẹ_con Lan không được đòi tài_sản thừa_kế từ Nam .
</s>
<s> Thêm nữa , nếu câu_chuyện này kết_thúc mà không ảnh_hưởng đến tình_cảm vợ_chồng Nhi thì càng tốt .
</s>
<s> Qua phân_tích , Thắng thấy cần loại_bỏ Nam khỏi kế_hoạch này và chỉ tấn_công vào Lan .
</s>
<s> Phương_pháp này sẽ dễ thành_công và êm_đẹp nhất .
</s>
<s> Màn_kịch của Thắng với Lan vẫn tiếp_diễn .
</s>
<s> Sau cú sốc biết Lan quan_hệ với Nam , Thắng khuyên Lan nên chấm_dứt .
</s>
<s> Lý_do : Nam không_thể cưới Lan .
</s>
<s> Lan còn trẻ , đẹp và hoàn_toàn có_thể lấy chồng tử_tế , tự làm để nuôi gia_đình và làm_giàu .
</s>
<s> Lan không_thể dựa mãi vào Nam vì Nam có_thể không có điều_kiện chu_cấp cho cô đến hết đời , Nam có_thể lại vướng vào hàng chục cô khác , đó là chưa kể vợ Nam có_thể biết .
</s>
<s> Lan cũng không_thể trông_chờ việc con mình hưởng thừa_kế của Nam vì từ nay đến đó biết_bao đổi_thay , biến_cố .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa cơ_hội để lấy chồng , có vốn , hoàn_lương ngày_một xa dần .
</s>
<s> Việc Thắng có lấy Lan hay không sẽ bàn sau khi Lan quyết_định từ_bỏ Nam .
</s>
<s> Lúc này Lan thật_sự hoang_mang .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa , Lan cũng không muốn phá vỡ hạnh_phúc gia_đình họ thì chắc_chắn cô ấy sẽ bù_đắp tiền cho Lan khôi_phục cuộc_sống ...
</s>
<s> Lan không ngăn_cản .
</s>
<s> Sau đó Thắng không nhắc gì đến câu_chuyện đó .
</s>
<s> Lan sốt_ruột gặng hỏi .
</s>
<s> Thắng nói : " Cô ấy rất hào_phóng và thông_cảm .
</s>
<s> Nhưng cô ấy đòi một_số điều_kiện " .
</s>
<s> Lan hỏi : " Điều_kiện gì ? " .
</s>
<s> Đã đến lúc Thắng lật bài : " Thật_ra anh là em họ chị Nhi .
</s>
<s> Chị ấy định xử em theo luật giang_hồ nhưng anh đã nói hết về em .
</s>
<s> Chị ấy rất độ_lượng và thông_cảm .
</s>
<s> Chị chấp_nhận chúng_ta thương_lượng với nhau " .
</s>
<s> Cụ_thể : Nhi sẽ không trả_thù , bêu_xấu và không đòi lại những tài_sản mà Nam cho Lan .
</s>
<s> Nhi cho Lan số tiền khá lớn để tự lo cuộc_sống mới .
</s>
<s> Đổi lại , Lan phải chấm_dứt tuyệt_đối mối quan_hệ với Nam , phải chuyển đến một tỉnh khác để sinh_sống .
</s>
<s> Lan phải viết giấy thừa_nhận đứa con của mình không phải là con Nam vì nó được sinh ra trước ngày Lan đến Hà_Nội , nó mang họ bố và không trùng với họ của Nam .
</s>
<s> Tất_cả chuyện này đều phải tuyệt_đối giấu Nam .
</s>
<s> Tiền sẽ được chuyển cho Lan từng phần , phụ_thuộc vào tiến_độ thực_hiện " dự_án " trên .
</s>
<s> Trong hai tuần suy_nghĩ và tham_khảo những người xung_quanh , Lan đã nhận thấy tính ưu_việt của kế_hoạch trên .
</s>
<s> Còn Nhi , để hạnh_phúc gia_đình " kiên_cố " từ bên trong , chị bắt_đầu trau_dồi kiến_thức về các loại rượu bổ và nước_hoa ...
</s>
<s> Mọi người đều thán_phục tài_nghệ của thám_tử Thắng , nhưng cũng phải thừa_nhận thuận_lợi ở đây là Nhi có tiền và Thắng ... già_đời .
</s>
<s> Còn nhân_vật của sự_kiện ngày_mai thì rất non_trẻ , cũng chẳng có tiền .
</s>
<s> Cô chỉ là một nữ_sinh trung_học và mất_tích đã 10 ngày nay .
</s>
<s> Quái_vật trên sông Đồng_Nai .
</s>
<s> Tình_trạng tận_thu cát sỏi lòng_sông Đồng_Nai đã làm cạn_kiệt nguồn tài_nguyên cát và nghiêm_trọng hơn là sự tác_động gây sạt_lở hàng trăm ngàn mét_vuông đất .
</s>
<s> Thế nhưng , đi dọc theo sông Đồng_Nai chúng_tôi chứng_kiến tình_hình khai_thác cát vẫn còn nóng_bỏng ...
</s>
<s> Có thời_điểm trên 50 cần cạp , hàng trăm ghe bơm hút cát thoải_mái cả ngày lẫn đêm trên một đoạn sông Đồng_Nai dài khoảng 60 km .
</s>
<s> Khi lòng_sông hết cát , lực_lượng khai_thác cát kéo vào mép bờ sông tiếp_tục khai_thác khiến hai bờ sông bị sạt_lở .
</s>
<s> Thậm_chí nhiều cù_lao , di_tích lịch_sử ... bị thu_hẹp dần nhưng chẳng ai phòng_chống sạt_lở , ngăn_chặn tình_trạng khai_thác cát bừa_bãi .
</s>
<s> Người dân hai bên bờ kêu_gào không thấu , khiếu_nại tập_thể cũng không giải_quyết được gì .
</s>
<s> Thậm_chí lực_lượng khai_thác cát còn hăm_dọa đưa cần_cẩu vào giật sập nhà dân nên đã xảy_ra nhiều trận chiến .
</s>
<s> Người dân trong bờ ném đá , làm giàn ná bắn đá tấn_công bọn khai_thác cát .
</s>
<s> Bọn " giặc cát " trên sà_lan đáp trả bằng cách tiến lại gần bờ quăng gàu khai_thác cát , giật lở bờ sông , phá sập nhà dân ...
</s>
<s> Từ thị_trấn Uyên_Hưng , huyện Tân_Uyên LBKT Bình_Dương RBKT chúng_tôi xuôi dòng Đồng_Nai , vòng qua cù_lao Bạch_Đằng .
</s>
<s> Dọc theo sà_lan là một_số ghe đang chờ ăn cát .
</s>
<s> Từ sáng sớm đến 12 g trưa , chiếc xáng cạp đã móc được hai sà_lan cát .
</s>
<s> Chiếc cần_cẩu trên sà_lan mỗi lần cạp 1 m3 cát .
</s>
<s> Người dân cho biết chiếc cẩu cạp này của Công_ty Xây_dựng Bình_Dương " núp_bóng " khai_thác cát dưới danh_nghĩa một dự_án nạo_vét dòng sông .
</s>
<s> Trên từng cây_số .
</s>
<s> Cách khu_vực cầu Hóa_An khoảng 300 m là ba cần_cẩu đang tiến_hành cạp cát ở khu_vực giữa sông trên một đoạn gần 1 km , theo một cán_bộ phòng khoáng_sản Sở Tài_nguyên - môi_trường tỉnh Đồng_Nai , hiện_nay toàn_bộ dự_án khai_thác cát đều bị ngưng cấp phép .
</s>
<s> Thỉnh_thoảng cần_cẩu lại thả xuống dòng sông một mẻ vừa cạp lên .
</s>
<s> Cách đó khoảng 70 m chiếc sà_lan cạp cát số LA 3636 - vừa cạp đầy một sà_lan cát , rồi lại tiếp_tục ăn cát cho sà_lan mới .
</s>
<s> Trên sà_lan lúc này có khoảng 40 m3 cát và ba người luôn túc_trực để tách bùn và cát .
</s>
<s> Từ đoạn cầu Hóa_An chạy xuôi về khu_vực cầu Ghềnh khoảng hơn 1 km , chúng_tôi gặp hai sà_lan số SG 0104 LH và một cần cạp không số cũng đang miệt_mài khai_thác cát .
</s>
<s> Theo người dân khu_vực , hai chiếc sà_lan này nằm một chỗ hốt cát đã hai năm nay .
</s>
<s> Đây là bọn khai_thác cát lậu có " tai_mắt " khắp nơi , toàn_bộ hoạt_động đều ngưng lại ngay_tức_thì khi có một cú phone báo_động .
</s>
<s> Nhiều năm nay , từ công_an xã đến huyện , tỉnh đều biết rõ bọn chúng nhưng chẳng làm gì được để ngăn_chặn những con quái_vật ăn cát ngày_đêm , suốt năm này qua năm khác !
</s>
<s> Chạy dọc sông Đồng_Nai có hàng trăm bãi cát sẵn_sàng thu_gom cát 24 / 24 giờ , lúc nào những bãi đó cũng có dày_đặc sà_lan chở cát , ghe hút cát đang neo chờ đưa cát lên bờ .
</s>
<s> Di_tích lịch_sử rồi ... sẽ biến mất .
</s>
<s> Cù_lao Rùa được xem là một di_tích văn_hóa - lịch_sử của tỉnh Bình_Dương , vậy_là trong khoảng ba năm nay hàng trăm ngàn mét_vuông đất cù_lao đã bị cuốn_trôi , sạt_lở .
</s>
<s> Nguyên_nhân chính là do khai_thác cát bừa_bãi .
</s>
<s> Tuyến đường giao_thông ấp 3 , xã Thạnh_Phước , huyện Tân_Uyên LBKT Bình_Dương RBKT năm_ngoái xe_tải có_thể chạy được , vậy_mà từ đầu năm đến nay đã bị sạt_lở và biến_mất .
</s>
<s> Ông Nghĩa nói : " Chỉ cần một cơn mưa nhỏ đủ thấm đất là con đường này lại biến mất ngay " .
</s>
<s> Như_vậy là chỉ trong hai năm , phần đất_liền cù_lao Rùa giáp với mé sông đều bị sạt_lở ăn sâu vào ít_nhất 30 m .
</s>
<s> Mới đây người dân cù_lao Rùa đã kiến_nghị tập_thể lên Thủ_tướng Chính_phủ nhằm chấm_dứt khai_thác ở quanh cù_lao này .
</s>
<s> Còn khu_vực cù_lao Phố LBKT TP Biên_Hòa RBKT cũng trong tình_trạng sạt_lở tương_tự .
</s>
<s> Từ bến đò Kho kéo dài đến cầu Rạch_Cát đều bị sạt_lở .
</s>
<s> Nhiều đoạn bờ sông hiện đang chờ đổ ập xuống bởi hàng chục hàm_ếch ăn sâu vào đất_liền .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người dân phải tự cứu mình bằng cách thả đá , xây_dựng bờ kè , cắm cọc cừ , chặn bao cát ... tránh sạt_lở .
</s>
<s> " Tôi sẽ làm tất_cả vì công_lý " .
</s>
<s> Nỗi đau da_cam lên_tiếng .
</s>
<s> Phạm_Ngọc_Khang bị teo cơ nằm một chỗ , đến 10 tuổi thì chết .
</s>
<s> Phạm_Ngọc_Khang nay đã 30 tuổi , hai tay hai chân bị teo cơ co rút , đi_đứng không vững " .
</s>
<s> Lá thư còn kèm theo một tấm ảnh của Phạm_Ngọc_Khải , 25 tuổi , ngồi trên xe_đẩy , hình_ảnh một chàng thanh_niên với thân_hình quắt_queo trong căn nhà đơn_sơ ...
</s>
<s> Có thư được gửi trực_tiếp đến ông , có thư được gửi qua các hội chữ_thập_đỏ địa_phương , tập_hợp lại giờ đã thành một chồng dày .
</s>
<s> Cả nước VN có hàng ngàn , hàng vạn con_em đang ngày_đêm đau_đớn và những gia_đình chịu bao cảnh mất_mát , đau_thương , trong đó có một phần nhỏ_bé của gia_đình cháu .
</s>
<s> " - Nguyễn_Thị_Viện mở_đầu lá thư của mình gửi từ xã Việt_Hùng , huyện Trực_Ninh , tỉnh Nam_Định như vậy .
</s>
<s> Bố Viện là bộ_đội lái xe_tăng của đoàn 375 , bị nhiễm chất_độc da_cam và đã qua_đời vì ung_thư .
</s>
<s> Viện bị bại_liệt nửa người .
</s>
<s> Chị của Viện bị bại_liệt toàn_thân .
</s>
<s> Hai chị_em hiện sống với người mẹ già trong căn nhà như Viện mô_tả là " dột_nát nắng_mưa trên mảnh đất eo_hẹp cơ_cực " .
</s>
<s> Từ xã Bình_Đào , huyện Thăng_Bình , Quảng_Nam , bà Mai_Thị_Lý viết thư đặt câu hỏi : " Khi chúng_tôi chết đi , ai sẽ là người nuôi_nấng , chăm_sóc con_cái chúng_tôi trên cuộc_đời này ? " .
</s>
<s> Những năm chiến_tranh , gia_đình bà đã cùng người dân trong vùng phải thường_xuyên di_chuyển trong rừng_núi , thung_lũng để tránh địch phát_hiện , nhưng chất khai_quang không buông_tha họ .
</s>
<s> Bốn lần mang_thai và sinh_nở trong thời_bình , hai cháu đầu chết khi chưa tròn 10 tuổi .
</s>
<s> Cháu thứ ba không điều_khiển được mình , cháu thứ tư bị hội_chứng Down .
</s>
<s> Bà viết : " Trong những lúc tuyệt_vọng nhất , tôi đã tự đặt câu hỏi : Tại_sao nỗi bất_hạnh không buông_tha gia_đình mình ?
</s>
<s> Nguyên_nhân nào và nó từ đâu đến ? " .
</s>
<s> Các nạn_nhân không đơn_độc .
</s>
<s> Qua hình_ảnh và câu_chuyện của những nạn_nhân , ông bị " sốc " với những gì nghe thấy .
</s>
<s> Ông nói : " Tôi đã bị xúc_động mạnh .
</s>
<s> Cảm_giác mất_mát và tức_giận tràn_ngập trong tôi .
</s>
<s> Có hàng ngàn nạn_nhân như_vậy ở Đà_Nẵng .
</s>
<s> Sau đó ông đã gửi tới văn_phòng đại_diện Thông_tấn_xã VN tại Washington bức thư kêu_gọi nạn_nhân chất_độc da_cam lên_tiếng .
</s>
<s> Ông nói : " Chính_phủ Mỹ phải có trách_nhiệm đáp_ứng những yêu_cầu về y_tế cũng_như xã_hội của những công_dân VN từng là nạn_nhân của chất_độc này , cũng_như xử_lý những thảm_họa môi_trường do họ gây ra " .
</s>
<s> Theo tôi , những công_ty đó phải gánh cả trách_nhiệm pháp_lý và lương_tâm đối_với các nạn_nhân ở VN " .
</s>
<s> Những lá thư đầy tình_cảm và nỗi đau sau đó đã tới_tấp bay về .
</s>
<s> Vừa trở_về Mỹ sau chuyến công_tác dài ngày định_kỳ tại VN , giáo_sư Kenneth gửi email cho các đồng_sự ở VN khẳng_định : " Có những người bạn khắp thế_giới đang quan_tâm và lo_lắng cho họ " .
</s>
<s> Nỗ_lực của tôi và của những người VN , người Mỹ trong chương_trình sẽ tiếp_tục " .
</s>
<s> Thay những giọt nước_mắt bằng những nụ cười .
</s>
<s> " Cuộc chiến_tranh tại VN đã khiến tôi tự nhận_thức rằng mình cần phải có trách_nhiệm với vùng_đất này " - ông tâm_sự .
</s>
<s> Các dự_án của Quỹ Quảng_Nam - Đà_Nẵng đặt ra mục_tiêu mỗi năm giúp_đỡ được 500 gia_đình người nghèo , cung_cấp học_bổng , các phương_tiện y_tế cho trẻ_em , người khuyết_tật ở Đà_Nẵng và một_số chương_trình nhỏ hỗ_trợ nạn_nhân chiến_tranh .
</s>
<s> Nỗi đau hậu_chiến và những đổi_thay của VN đã được giáo_sư Kenneth viết trong cuốn sách Bệnh_nhân phong và thần_kinh : một người Mỹ tại VN ngày_nay LBKT Lepers and lunacy : an American in Vietnam today RBKT dày 246 trang vừa được Nhà_xuất_bản BookSurge phát_hành tại Mỹ và đang được Công_ty văn_hóa tổng_hợp Phương_Nam dịch ra tiếng Việt .
</s>
<s> Ông nói : " Khi nhìn những cảnh nghèo_khó và đớn_đau do chiến_tranh để lại , tôi không_thể không lên_tiếng .
</s>

<s> Bác_Hồ ủng_hộ quyết_định của tôi ... " .
</s>
<s> Riêng bà Raymonde_Dien luôn ôm hôn những người bạn Việt : " Tôi sung_sướng khi cuộc chiến_tranh của Pháp tại VN đã chấm_dứt , nhưng không may cho các bạn lại tiếp_tục cuộc kháng_chiến trường_kỳ đối_với quân_đội Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Họ đã để lại hậu_quả quá lớn bằng chất_độc da_cam / dioxin hủy_diệt .
</s>
<s> Hiện_giờ chúng_tôi vẫn đấu_tranh để chống lại , tố_cáo di_hại của chất_độc da_cam ...
</s>
<s> Nhân_dân VN đang khắc_phục hậu_quả chiến_tranh .
</s>
<s> Hậu_quả nghiêm_trọng là hậu_quả chất_độc da_cam .
</s>
<s> Tháng 3 - 2005 chúng_tôi cùng Hội Hữu_nghị Pháp - Việt sẽ tổ_chức hội_thảo quốc_tế về chất_độc da_cam .
</s>
<s> Cho đến giờ có nhiều cá_nhân và tổ_chức đăng_ký tham_gia với chúng_tôi .
</s>
<s> Tôi rất tự_hào là người bạn của VN .
</s>
<s> Hành_động của chúng_tôi đòi quyền công_bằng cho người dân VN bị nhiễm chất_độc da_cam đã diễn ra từ nhiều năm qua .
</s>
<s> Tại Pháp , nhiều cá_nhân , hội đã tham_gia cuộc vận_động của chúng_tôi chống chất_độc da_cam tại VN .
</s>
<s> Chúng_ta phải đứng lên tố_cáo để buộc các công_ty phải khắc_phục hậu_quả khi đã sản_xuất ra chất_độc để quân_đội Mỹ rải xuống mảnh đất của người VN làm ảnh_hưởng đến bao thế_hệ ... " .
</s>
<s> Đến VN lần này , hai người như đang trở_lại ngôi nhà của mình .
</s>
<s> Nguyên đại_sứ đầu_tiên của VN tại Pháp , ông Võ_Văn_Sung , đã nhấn_mạnh : " Hai bạn là người Pháp rất VN " .
</s>
<s> Có_mặt tại buổi giao_lưu , cô Trần_Tố_Nga LBKT nguyên là hiệu_trưởng Trường Marie_Curie RBKT nói : " Năm tôi 8 tuổi , mẹ tôi đã nói với tôi tấm_gương của ông Henri_Martin và bà Raymonde_Dien là hai anh_hùng dũng_cảm đấu_tranh cho dân_tộc VN , và từ đó hai tấm_gương này theo tôi mãi trong cuộc_đời .
</s>
<s> Giờ đây tôi được gặp hai người bằng xương bằng thịt tại đây , tôi rất hạnh_phúc và xin_phép cho tôi được ôm hôn hai cô chú " .
</s>
<s> Ông Võ_Văn_Sung cho biết : " Phong_trào nhân_dân Pháp ủng_hộ VN chống chiến_tranh xâm_lược của thực_dân Pháp và Mỹ rất sôi_nổi .
</s>
<s> Có được sự đấu_tranh mạnh_mẽ của nhân_dân Pháp lúc đó , hai người bạn của chúng_ta là tia lửa đầu_tiên và giữ ngọn lửa ấy trong suốt cuộc đấu_tranh đó " .
</s>
<s> Ông Henri_Martin đã gửi thông_điệp đến các bạn trẻ VN : " Các bạn hôm_nay đón_tiếp chúng_tôi như những người bạn thân_thiết .
</s>
<s> Tình hữu_nghị hai nước Việt - Pháp đã có từ rất lâu_đời , từ khi tôi chưa chào_đời .
</s>
<s> Từ những năm 1920 khi Bác_Hồ là người tham_gia sáng_lập Đảng Cộng_sản Pháp .
</s>
<s> Tôi chỉ là người phát_triển thêm tình hữu_nghị đó " .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người đã xúc_động : " Chúng_ta phải đặt tên VN cho hai người bạn của chúng_ta là Hồ_Henri_Martin và Hồ_Raymonde_Dien " .
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Đòi lại một cuộc_đời : Đứa con bị đánh_cắp .
</s>
<s> Chuyến bay sang châu_Âu phải hoãn lại do thời_tiết xấu .
</s>
<s> Hằng mệt_mỏi quay về nhà .
</s>
<s> Xuống xe , chị ngạc_nhiên thấy cổng biệt_thự không khóa .
</s>
<s> Theo lịch , hôm_nay người giúp_việc về quê ; Tùng , con_trai chị , đi học .
</s>
<s> Trong sân hai chiếc môtô cỡ lớn dựng ngỗ_ngược bên thềm .
</s>
<s> Lần theo vết giày hằn trên thảm_đỏ , Hằng lên tới phòng con_trai .
</s>
<s> Cửa khép hờ vẳng tiếng thều_thào , chửi tục và sặc_sụa mùi khét .
</s>
<s> Hằng ghé_mắt và choáng_váng muốn đổ gục xuống thềm : thằng Tùng - đứa con_trai duy_nhất của chị - đang gí mũi hít thứ khói trắng bốc lên từ mảnh giấy kẹo cao_su do một thằng tóc đỏ như ma_trơi đưa sát mặt .
</s>
<s> Tùng lim_dim nuốt khói , uống một ngụm coca rồi nằm vật ra nền thọc tay vào bụng gãi_gãi .
</s>
<s> Thằng thứ ba ấn vào miệng Tùng điếu thuốc_lá cháy đỏ .
</s>
<s> Biệt_thự , đôla , bất_động_sản , công_ty ... - những thứ làm thiên_hạ phải khuất_phục chị , nay đã thành vô_nghĩa .
</s>
<s> Hằng đến công_ty thám_tử với yêu_cầu " đòi lại đứa con " cho chị .
</s>
<s> Chàng thám_tử thư_sinh .
</s>
<s> Cuộc họp bất_thường của Công_ty điều_tra & bảo_vệ V được giám_đốc Vinh mở_đầu bằng câu giới_thiệu : nhiệm_vụ lần này sẽ lớn gấp nhiều lần về thời_gian , độ công_phu cũng như chi_phí .
</s>
<s> Chỉ duy_nhất một người nhận nhiệm_vụ và đó phải là một người điềm_tĩnh , hiểu_biết xã_hội , sống nghiêm_túc , kỷ_luật , biết tiếng Anh ... nhưng lại có tính_cách , kiến_thức và lứa tuổi của một sinh_viên ; đặc_biệt phải là một tấm_gương mẫu_mực trong cuộc_sống .
</s>
<s> Các thám_tử ngỡ_ngàng hơn khi người được chọn là một sinh_viên vừa ra trường mới vào làm_việc được ba tháng .
</s>
<s> Đó là Tuấn , chàng thư_sinh người Hà_Nội lành như ngụm nước mưa .
</s>
<s> Ấp_úng trong phòng giám_đốc , Tuấn không biết cần hỏi gì cho đủ .
</s>
<s> Giám_đốc Vinh vỗ vai nói : " Tất_cả những điều tôi nói trong cuộc họp là đúng .
</s>
<s> Nhưng thật_ra cậu chỉ cần thực_hiện nhiệm_vụ là làm một người bạn tốt , làm một thanh_niên có chí_hướng là đủ " .
</s>
<s> Năm ngày liền Tuấn nằm lì một chỗ nghiên_cứu , tìm_hiểu về lý_lịch , tính_cách , sở_thích , những mối quan_hệ , nơi lui_tới ... của một người trạc tuổi mình .
</s>
<s> Mẹ Tùng chấp_nhận mặc_cả của con_trai là mua cho nó một chiếc @ .
</s>
<s> Đổi lại Tùng phải học tiếng Anh để sắp tới du_học ở Úc .
</s>
<s> Nếu Tùng học được hai tuần nghiêm_túc thì mẹ mua xe .
</s>
<s> Sau hai tháng học tử_tế mẹ sẽ chính_thức sang_tên xe cho Tùng .
</s>
<s> Tốt_nghiệp khóa học sẽ còn nhiều phần_thưởng nữa , thậm_chí là xe_hơi .
</s>
<s> Chịu được bốn ngày thì Tùng quá_sức định phá " hợp_đồng " với mẹ , nhưng đúng hôm đó lại nhìn thấy con @ đẹp như công_chúa cứ lượn_lờ ngay ngoài ngõ , đành cắn_răng chờ 10 ngày nữa .
</s>
<s> Chiều đó mẹ Tùng nói : " Sợ con buồn , mẹ gặp được một cậu con_trai người bạn cũng đang tìm thầy học tiếng Anh .
</s>
<s> Hai đứa nếu hợp thì học chung " .
</s>
<s> Tùng OK - đánh_bạn với thằng nào cũng được , có xe tính sau .
</s>
<s> Bảo_mẫu kiểu ... thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Thám_tử Tuấn trong vai Hải xuất_hiện bên Tùng một_cách lãnh_đạm .
</s>
<s> Hải học nghiêm_túc , kiệm_lời , ít giao_lưu .
</s>
<s> Khi được hỏi thì khá ân_cần .
</s>
<s> Khi Tùng định lấn_át , Hải điềm_nhiên nhìn thẳng vào mặt Tùng tỏ_vẻ cứng_rắn nhưng không thách_thức , không thù vặt .
</s>
<s> Hải bày cho Tùng cách học , cách truy bài khá thú_vị và hiệu_quả .
</s>
<s> Tóm_lại Tùng thấy Hải vô_hại , dễ gần và có_ích trong chừng_mực nào đó .
</s>
<s> Buổi học bớt nặng_nề với Tùng .
</s>
<s> Hai ngày nữa mẹ Tùng sẽ mua xe .
</s>
<s> Biết Tùng sắp trốn học gặp bọn Thắng " trắng " , Hùng " mặt đá " để khoe và tư_vấn , Hải bám theo .
</s>
<s> Vừa đánh xóc_đĩa ở ngõ rắn_lục LBKT ngõ Chợ - Khâm_Thiên , Hà_Nội RBKT ra thì Tùng thấy Hải đang chằm_chằm nhìn cậu .

<s> Hải cười , khẽ gật và ghé vào quán nước ngồi tỉnh_bơ .

<s> Hôm đó về nhà Tùng rất ngán mẹ biết tin này .
</s>

</s>
<s> Mất uy_tín với đồng_bọn ...
</s>

<s> Hải vẫn bình_thản như không .
</s>
<s> Mẹ Tùng vẫn mua xe như cam_kết .
</s>
<s> Tùng thầm nể Hải .

<s> Hải và chị Hằng tìm mọi cơ_hội để xây_dựng tình_cảm cho hai thanh_niên .

<s> Thỉnh_thoảng học khuya , Hải ngủ lại với Tùng .
</s>
<s> Có bữa mẹ Tùng mời cả thầy_giáo và hai thằng cùng ăn tối .
</s>
<s> Có hôm Hải rủ Tùng đi câu , dã_ngoại , chơi thể_thao ...
</s>
<s> Tất_cả những hành_động này Hải đều báo_cáo với công_ty .
</s>
<s> Hải âm_thầm tìm_hiểu những điều thú_vị , những kiến_thức bổ_ích trong các hoạt_động đó để bồi_bổ cho Tùng .
</s>
<s> Ví_dụ : đi câu thì Hải kể cho Tùng nghe tích Lã_Vọng câu cá , thơ câu cá của Nguyễn_Khuyến , những bậc anh_hùng ở_ẩn buông câu quên đời ...
</s>
<s> Đánh bóng_bàn thì luyện mắt tinh_anh như_thế_nào ?
</s>
<s> Đời tư vận_động_viên bóng_bàn giỏi nhất Trung_Quốc ra_sao ? ...
</s>
<s> Khi dã_ngoại thì đến chùa , đình , danh_lam nào Hải cũng có những mẩu chuyện sâu_sắc hay dí_dỏm để kể .
</s>
<s> Hải từng bước lấp đầy khoảng_trống thời_gian , không_gian và tình_cảm của Tùng .
</s>
<s> Một hôm biết Tùng sắp sẵn kế_hoạch trốn học đến gặp bọn Thắng " trắng " , Hải kéo Tùng đi ăn nem ở phố Cầu_Gỗ .
</s>
<s> Nguyên_nhân : chúc_mừng Tùng đạt điểm cao ở học_phần 1 .
</s>
<s> Tùng sửng_sốt và thấy một niềm hạnh_phúc chưa bao_giờ cậu có .
</s>
<s> Hải ý_tứ nói : là thằng con_trai muốn thể_hiện sức_mạnh thì cần tránh bị coi_thường , nhất_là về đầu_óc .
</s>
<s> Đã chấp_nhận học thì đừng để thầy chê ...
</s>
<s> Hôm đó Tùng không đi chơi .

<s> Tùng khó_chịu nhưng cũng rất xấu_hổ và quyết_tâm nhịn .

<s> Hôm Tùng nhận giấy_tờ xe mẹ trao , công_ty thám_tử lập một kế_hoạch công_phu với sáu vai_diễn đón tại đầu đường Thanh_Niên cắt Yên_Phụ .

<s> Tùng liên_hoan , kẹp thêm ba tên côn_đồ phóng như xé gió .

<s> Đang hùng_hổ thì không ngờ đó là bọn du_đãng toàn thằng to như con tượng , xăm trổ đen người , ùa ra xâu_xé .

<s> Lũ bạn hảo_hán của Tùng bỏ chạy hoặc câm_như_hến .

<s> Bất_ngờ Hải đến , chắn ngang mặt lũ cô_hồn .

<s> Không nhiều lời , bọn chúng rút tuýp_nước , vỏ_chai vồ lấy Hải .

<s> Như phim Hong_Kong , Hải tung chân đá lật hàm , đấm móc ngược chấn_thủy , hạ hai đối_thủ trong vòng 3 phút .
</s>
<s> Lũ côn_đồ gầm lên hô nhau rút phóng_lợn LBKT dao chọc_tiết lợn RBKT , mã_tấu lao đến .
</s>
<s> Thằng mặt lợn , mắt trâu , to như hộ_pháp nhăn_nhó , oằn người kêu_la ầm_ĩ .
</s>
<s> Cả bọn tráo mắt đứng khựng lại .
</s>
<s> Hải điềm_tĩnh tra chìa_khóa , nổ xe đưa Tùng về .

<s> Từ đây mọi việc_làm , suy_nghĩ bình_thường của Tùng , Tùng đều có thói_quen xem_xét lại ...
</s>
<s> Tùng luôn nhìn thấy những cái mốc phấn_đấu ngay phía trước và tự_tin mình đủ sức ...
</s>

</s>
<s> Đã làm_chủ được tình_hình và mọi diễn_tiến đều thuận_lợi thì bất_ngờ Hải bị lật_tẩy chân_tướng .
</s>
<s> Mọi kế_hoạch và thành_quả có nguy_cơ đổ_vỡ , Hải và tất_cả thành_viên tham_gia lâm vào tình_thế cam_go ...
</s>
<s> Kết_quả cuộc thi phóng_sự - ký_sự 2004 của báo Tuổi_Trẻ .
</s>
<s> Ban giám_khảo công_bố cuộc thi phóng_sự - ký_sự 2004 như sau : Giải nhất : không có .
</s>
<s> Hai giải nhì : Nàng_tiên nhỏ trong gia_đình " cái_bang " LBKT của Tiến_Dũng RBKT , Tường_trình từ nghĩa_trang vòng_hoa trắng của Nguyễn_Lê_Nguyên .
</s>
<s> Ba giải ba : Tôi đi buôn ngựa của Võ_Văn_Thành , Cái học của gia_đình người Cil của Tiến_Đạt , Dựng lều trọ học của Hà_Hữu_Đồng .
</s>
<s> Hai " kỹ_sư " chân_đất .
</s>
<s> Hai nông_dân dáng người nhỏ_nhắn một người tóc bạc trắng , chỉ còn một con mắt và một cánh_tay ; một người trạc ngũ_tuần có đôi tay chai_sần - ngồi thu mình im_lặng ở một góc phòng họp của ủy_ban tỉnh vì không chịu được ... máy_lạnh .
</s>
<s> Trưa .
</s>
<s> Anh Lộc bảo : " Phải đích_thân tui làm chứ không dám nhờ người khác , làm không đạt yêu_cầu , mới xài mấy bữa bị gãy , mất uy_tín " .
</s>
<s> Mới ngồi nói_chuyện với anh chục phút mà đã có ba bốn người tới tìm anh để đặt_hàng mua kéo .
</s>
<s> Đưa tôi một thanh kim_loại dài chừng 2 m sơn màu đỏ dựng ở góc nhà , anh Lộc bảo : " Đây là kéo cắt tỉa của tui làm , chú mang ra vườn cắt thử coi .
</s>
<s> Muốn cắt cành , cắt trái gì cũng được " .
</s>
<s> Tôi đưa lưỡi kéo lên chùm cam_sành tìm cuống của trái cam đèo_đẹt nhất và bóp nhẹ vào thanh kim_loại nhỏ - ở phần cuối cây kéo tương_tự như sử_dụng bình tưới hoa kiểng - đang nằm gọn trong lòng bàn_tay .
</s>
<s> " Bựt " , trái cam rơi đánh bịch xuống đất , gọn và dễ hết_sức ! ...
</s>
<s> Hèn_nào , chỉ mới hơn một năm mà anh đã sản_xuất hơn 1_._000 cây kéo phục_vụ nhà_vườn các tỉnh Tiền_Giang , Bến_Tre , Vĩnh_Long , Đồng_Tháp .
</s>
<s> Anh Lộc cho biết cách đây mấy ngày cây kéo " độc_quyền " này vừa lên xe_đò ra miền Đông làm nhiệm_vụ ... hái mãng_cầu .
</s>
<s> Anh nói : " Nhà tui có tám công vườn trồng cam , quít , bưởi .
</s>
<s> Muốn hái trái bệnh trên cao phải bắc thang đôi rất cực , còn kéo giật dây của Đài_Loan sản_xuất thì không tỉa được mấy trái đèo trong chùm nhiều trái .
</s>
<s> Cực nhất là mùa thu_hoạch , cầm kéo ngắn hái từng trái mất biết_bao_nhiêu thời_gian , công_sức , trừ chi_phí không còn lợi bao_nhiêu , nên tui nghĩ phải làm ra một cái kéo đa_năng " .
</s>
<s> Nghĩ là làm , anh Lộc bắt_đầu thức đêm nghiên_cứu bằng phương_pháp của nông_dân : không có bản_vẽ , đồ_nghề cũng không .
</s>
<s> " Tui lấy giấy cạctông cắt hình lưỡi kéo đủ kiểu , giống kéo cắt vải có , giống lưỡi câu cũng có ... " .
</s>
<s> Nhưng anh lại trăn_trở : " Phải _làm_sao cho cán kéo dài ra 2 - 3 m mà vẫn cắt như kéo thường mới ăn " .
</s>
<s> Một hôm đi sớm anh thấy người_ta mở cửa sắt và ... một ý_nghĩ lóe lên trong đầu anh Lộc .
</s>
<s> Đạp xe chạy ngược về nhà , anh lấy giấy cắt hình lò_xo xếp theo nguyên_tắc đóng mở của cửa sắt .
</s>
<s> Thấy kéo bằng giấy hoạt_động theo đúng ý_đồ của mình , anh Lộc bắt_đầu đi mua sắt thép và ra tiệm hàn nhờ người_ta thao_tác giùm các chi_tiết kéo theo mô_hình bằng giấy .
</s>
<s> Ba ngày sau , cái kéo đầu_tiên dài 1 m thành hình .
</s>
<s> Đem ra vườn cắt thử , thấy sướng tay , anh ở ngoài vườn cắt tỉa suốt ngày quên cả cơm_nước .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người hàng_xóm nghe tin tới xem và đặt_hàng ngay .
</s>
<s> Đến mùa thu_hoạch , nhà_vườn chỉ cần gắn thêm túi vải vào kéo LBKT có gắn sẵn khung sắt RBKT sẽ thu_hoạch nhanh gấp vài chục lần hái trái bằng ... các loại kéo khác .
</s>
<s> Máy gom lúa của lão_nông lớp 5 trường làng .
</s>
<s> Năm 1972 , trong lúc làm_cỏ ruộng chuẩn_bị sạ lúa thì một quả mìn phát_nổ làm anh nông_dân Huỳnh_Văn_On LBKT sinh năm 1952 RBKT vĩnh_viễn mất đi một cánh_tay trái và con mắt phải .
</s>
<s> Bị thương_tật nặng , anh Tư_On không_thể tiếp_tục nghề thợ_máy ôtô đã bỏ công đi học ở tận Sài_Gòn , mà phải sống lây_lất bằng nghề ... sửa máy_cày ở quê_nhà - chợ Mỹ_Phước_Tây , huyện Cai_Lậy LBKT Tiền_Giang RBKT .
</s>
<s> Năm 1992 vợ_chồng con_cái anh Tư đùm_túm nhau về khai_hoang , lập_nghiệp ở vùng đất đầy cỏ_năng thuộc ấp Long_Phước , xã Mỹ_Phước_Tây .
</s>
<s> Anh Tư bảo ở xứ " khỉ_ho_cò_gáy " này tới mùa thu_hoạch tìm nhân_công khó như hái sao trên trời vậy .
</s>
<s> Cả mẫu ruộng mà không có người phụ cắt , gom lúa để phóng thì coi như cả nhà phải ăn ngủ ngoài đồng suốt mấy ngày trời .
</s>
<s> Tới mùa mưa làm không kịp thì coi như gặp tai_họa lớn .
</s>
<s> Sau nhiều vụ lúa vất_vả chỉ vì chuyện gom lúa LBKT vùng này đã có vài máy cắt giải_quyết rất nhanh nhu_cầu thu_hoạch của nông_dân RBKT , anh Tư bực_mình ở miết ngoài hè - nơi chứa đồ phế_liệu máy_móc mà anh gọi là xưởng - để tìm cách làm máy gom lúa cho vụ tới .
</s>
<s> Đó là thời_điểm cuối vụ đông_xuân 2003 .
</s>
<s> Anh thật_thà : " Tui chẳng biết vẽ mà cũng chẳng quen chuyện vẽ_vời như mấy ông kỹ_sư .
</s>
<s> Nói thiệt , hồi đó mới học đến lớp 5 trường_làng chứ mấy , nay chữ_nghĩa đã " đội_nón " ra đi gần hết rồi .
</s>
<s> Trong đầu tui nghĩ ra được cái gì là tui làm cái đó trước .
</s>
<s> Mấy anh ở Sở Khoa_học - công_nghệ tỉnh lên bảo tui cho coi bản_vẽ để giúp làm hồ_sơ dự thi sáng_tạo gì đó , tui cũng nói thật trong nhà tui kiếm tờ giấy trắng còn khó nữa , nói chi là bản_vẽ " .
</s>
<s> Để " chế_tạo " ra máy gom lúa , đầu_tiên anh Tư nghĩ : muốn gom được thì phải ... xúc nó lên .
</s>
<s> Ý_tưởng về một dàn xúc dần thành_hình trong đầu anh Tư .
</s>
<s> Lấy mấy cây sắt phi 8 hàn lại thành những mũi chĩa nhọn , tiếp đó anh sai thằng út_Vinh chạy tới mấy nhà_máy xay xát tìm xin cho được mấy sợi dây trân cũ LBKT dây băng_tải khổ lớn RBKT về cắt ra xếp gần với nhau cho rộng bằng với chiều_cao cây lúa đã cắt .
</s>
<s> Hệ_thống này được nối với động_cơ máy xới tay bánh trục .
</s>
<s> Khi máy xới vận_hành , hệ_thống dây trân này sẽ xoay theo .
</s>
<s> Máy gom lúa của anh Tư ban_đầu chỉ có vậy .
</s>
<s> Gắn hệ_thống này vô máy xới tay chạy thử , anh lại nghĩ : " Phải có cái rơmooc chứa lúa " .
</s>
<s> Máy gom lúa của anh Tư ra_đời sau gần ba tháng miệt_mài chế_tạo .
</s>
<s> Cha con anh hớn_hở trông đến ngày thu_hoạch lúa để đưa máy xuống ruộng .
</s>
<s> Nhưng chỉ mới chạy được chục thước , cha con anh Tư đã méo_mặt vì lúa chẳng chịu chạy ra sau cái rơmooc mà cứ xoay tít quanh mấy sợi dây trân rồi rơi xuống ruộng .
</s>
<s> Và sau gần một năm chỉnh sửa , máy gom lúa của anh Tư đã hoàn_thành khi những đồng_tiền cuối_cùng trong gia_đình cũng hết .
</s>
<s> Với hai nhân_công vận_hành , chiếc máy này gom được 2_,_5 ha / ngày với tiền công 200_._000 đồng / ha , trong khi đó nếu thuê nhân_công gom thì phải mất 300_._000 - 900_._000 đồng / ha tùy thời_điểm .
</s>
<s> Dù vậy anh Tư vẫn chưa hài_lòng : " Tui đang nghiên_cứu làm dây_chuyền gom lúa , phóng lúa và rải rơm trên khắp mặt ruộng luôn mà chỉ cần hai người vận_hành " - anh Tư quả_quyết .
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Đòi lại một cuộc_đời : Chàng du_học_sinh bí_ẩn .
</s>
<s> Theo kế_hoạch , những ngày đầu cả hai luyện tiếng Anh trước khi thi vào đại_học .
</s>
<s> Hải sẽ học cùng lớp , ngồi cùng bàn , ngủ cùng phòng và ăn cùng mâm với Tùng .
</s>
<s> Tác_chiến ở xứ người .
</s>
<s> Mọi hoạt_động và mối quan_hệ xã_hội của Tùng đều diễn ra bên Hải .
</s>
<s> Điều này tuy thuận_lợi trong việc nắm_bắt Tùng song cũng hết_sức nguy_hiểm vì dễ sơ_suất .
</s>
<s> Nếu Tùng phát_hiện Hải thì hậu_quả vô_cùng tồi_tệ .
</s>
<s> Tùng sẽ thấy bị khinh_thường , sẽ không tin ai và không nghe ai .
</s>
<s> Tùng sẽ thất_vọng hơn khi niềm_tin lớn nhất bị sụp_đổ .
</s>
<s> Công_ty thám_tử và mẹ Tùng cũng không hẳn yên_tâm khi bản_thân Hải cũng chỉ là một thanh_niên mới lớn , chưa va_vấp xã_hội nhiều , chưa sống tự_lập và xa nhà bao_giờ .
</s>
<s> Không loại_trừ việc Hải cũng có_thể sa_ngã .
</s>
<s> Vì_vậy mỗi ngày Hải phải gửi về công_ty một bản báo_cáo ngắn thông_qua thư_điện_tử .
</s>
<s> Việc này cần cẩn_trọng vì Hải không_thể dùng máy_tính trong phòng hay máy_xách_tay của Tùng .
</s>
<s> Ra ngoài một_mình nhiều thì dễ bị lộ .
</s>
<s> Tuy_vậy , mọi việc bước_đầu đúng như kế_hoạch .
</s>
<s> Tùng vui , ổn_định tâm_lý , bỏ thuốc_lá , quên hẳn ma_túy , không ham những thói xấu trước đây và học khá tiến_bộ .
</s>
<s> Hải rủ Tùng tham_gia các nhóm học tin_học , triết_học và âm_nhạc .
</s>
<s> Thời_gian chính là đi học và lên thư_viện .
</s>
<s> Đôi bạn hòa_đồng với các học_sinh nước_ngoài khi du_lịch , chơi thể_thao .
</s>
<s> Tùng thật_sự tự_tin và phấn_khích .
</s>
<s> Những lá thư Tùng gửi về cho mẹ khoe những tiến_bộ của mình , Hải đều được chị Hằng gửi lại cho xem .
</s>
<s> Mọi việc ổn .
</s>
<s> Riêng việc gửi báo_cáo quá nguy_hiểm nên công_ty chấp_nhận năm ngày Hải gửi một lần .
</s>
<s> Công_ty cũng không ngừng nhắc_nhở Hải cần tỉnh_táo , khôn_khéo với Tùng và với cả bản_thân mình .
</s>
<s> Hết tháng thứ ba , công_ty thám_tử cử người bay sang tận nơi , trong vai một người VN đi công_tác muốn tìm_hiểu việc du_học để đưa con sang .
</s>
<s> Ông đã trực_tiếp " nghiệm_thu " và công_tác tư_tưởng cho Hải .
</s>
<s> Thêm những tín_hiệu đáng mừng : Tùng và Hải cùng đủ điểm dự thi đại_học .
</s>
<s> Tùng kết_thân với một cô bạn_gái người Hàn_Quốc học rất giỏi ...
</s>
<s> Khi thám_tử bị điều_tra .
</s>
<s> Nhân niềm vui đó , Hải quyết_định dành ngày cuối tuần đi bơi và mua_sắm .
</s>
<s> Tùng hào_hứng thêm khi gặp những đoàn khách du_lịch đến từ Hà_Nội .
</s>
<s> Đang trò_chuyện , chợt một thanh_niên trong đoàn khách hét toáng : " Ơ , Tuấn , mày sang đây làm gì ? " .
</s>
<s> Người đó cứ xoắn lấy Hải , luôn mồm gọi là Tuấn và hỏi_han đủ điều rất lạ .
</s>
<s> Rằng : ra trường mày làm ở đâu ?
</s>
<s> Mấy lần đi qua Bưởi vào nhà tìm nhưng bố_mẹ mày nói mày đi làm xa ...
</s>
<s> Người khách đó có vẻ rất hiểu gia_đình Hải nhưng tất_cả những điều anh ta nhắc đến đều khác với những gì Hải kể với Tùng .
</s>
<s> Nhìn Hải lúc đó rất bối_rối .
</s>
<s> Sau một hồi ngập_ngừng , Hải tìm cách bỏ đi .
</s>
<s> Chiều về hai người không nói_chuyện nhiều .
</s>
<s> Rất thân nhau , Hải thường ăn ngủ ở nhà Tùng nhưng Tùng không thấy Hải mời đến nhà bao_giờ .
</s>
<s> Hải học giỏi nhưng không hiểu sao thi đại_học trong nước không đỗ .
</s>
<s> Nhà Hải không nghèo nhưng sao không mắc điện_thoại ?
</s>
<s> Hóa_ra Hải còn có một cái tên nữa .
</s>
<s> Nhà Hải không phải như địa_chỉ Tùng biết .
</s>
<s> Hải đã ra trường hai năm , đã đi làm .
</s>
<s> Và đặc_biệt là thái_độ lúng_túng của Hải khi bị nhắc đến những thông_tin này ...
</s>
<s> Con_người này là ai ?
</s>
<s> Ở bên mình nhằm mục_đích gì ? ...
</s>
<s> Bản báo_cáo của Hải làm sửng_sốt ban lãnh_đạo công_ty thám_tử và chị Hằng .
</s>
<s> Tất_cả có_thể đổ xuống sông , thậm_chí còn tồi_tệ hơn khi chưa thực_hiện .
</s>
<s> Rất may Hải đã ứng_biến tốt : Hải bị gọi là Tuấn vì ở gần nhà có hai ông già đều tên Hải nên mọi người gọi sang tên đệm .
</s>
<s> Hải và bố_mẹ ngày trước ở chung với ông_bà trên đường Bưởi và người bạn nọ quen_biết Hải trong thời_kỳ Hải ở đó .
</s>
<s> Hải thi đại_học không đỗ và có học trường trung_cấp du_lịch .
</s>
<s> Ra trường đã đi làm nhưng có người_nhà ở nước_ngoài tài_trợ nay du_học ...
</s>
<s> Hai kịch_bản mới phải thực_hiện .
</s>
<s> Tại ký_túc_xá , Hải vẫn tỏ ra rất bình_thường sau cuộc gặp người bạn lần trước .
</s>
<s> Tùng cũng tỏ ra rất bình_thường để âm_thầm theo_dõi Hải .
</s>
<s> Hải vẫn giữ nguyên thói_quen ra ngoài một_mình như trước đây đi gửi thư về công_ty .
</s>
<s> Một lần Tùng nói : " Em đi chơi cùng cô bạn người Thái_Lan , tối muộn mới về " .
</s>
<s> Bắt xe_buýt đi một vòng , Tùng lập_tức quay lại ký_túc_xá trong trang_phục khác .
</s>
<s> Đầu đội mũ sụp vành , đeo kính đen , đi xe_đạp địa_hình và mua sẵn bánh , sữa để mai_phục .
</s>
<s> Trời gần tối , Hải đi bộ ra phố .
</s>
<s> Tùng bám theo .
</s>
<s> Hải vào siêu_thị ăn kem và mua hai đĩa_nhạc .
</s>
<s> Tối , Hải vào thư_viện đọc sách Chiến_tranh và hòa_bình đến khuya thì về phòng .
</s>
<s> Vài lần Tùng theo_dõi , Hải giữ nguyên kịch_bản trên .
</s>
<s> Một hôm Hải dựng cảnh : đang mở hộp_thư riêng thì một người bạn cùng lớp LBKT khi nhận được tín_hiệu Hải báo RBKT lao vào phòng kéo Hải xềnh_xệch ra ngoài vì một nữ sinh_viên ăn_mặc như ngoài bãi_biển .
</s>
<s> Lập_tức Tùng copy thư trong email của Hải vào đĩa_mềm và chuồn ra ngoài đọc .
</s>

</s>
<s> Trước_mắt , Thanh cứ theo_dõi Hùng .
</s>
<s> Thanh bám sát .
</s>
<s> Hùng xách cặp lên tầng và vào một lớp_học tại_chức buổi tối .
</s>
<s> Lớp tại_chức buổi tối khá lộn_xộn và ít biết mặt nhau .
</s>
<s> Đóng vai một sinh_viên , Thanh gặp lớp trưởng xin photo danh_sách , địa_chỉ , nghề_nghiệp và số điện_thoại của cả lớp .
</s>
<s> Còn quãng thời_gian Hùng ở Đức ?
</s>
<s> Đã cách 10 năm về trước , hơn_nữa không biết Hùng ở thành_phố nào , đi diện gì và ở bao_lâu .
</s>
<s> Thanh quyết_định khai_thác ở chính anh ta qua một kịch_bản : Hùng đến chơi , điện_thoại nhà bà Loan đổ chuông .
</s>
<s> Người đầu dây bên kia xin gặp bà Loan .
</s>
<s> Nói_chuyện một lúc , bà quay sang Hùng và bảo : " Bạn cô LBKT thám_tử Thanh RBKT có con_trai đang ở Đức .
</s>
<s> Nó gặp nhiều khó_khăn .
</s>
<s> Hùng vui_vẻ cầm máy nói_chuyện rất tự_tin .
</s>
<s> Hùng tư_vấn nhiều điều bổ_ích và còn đề_nghị viết thư giới_thiệu con ông khách với bạn Hùng ở Berlin .
</s>
<s> Qua câu_chuyện , Thanh biết Hùng đã ở Berlin từ năm 1988 - 1993 và chuyên buôn_bán .
</s>
<s> Cộng_tác_viên của Thanh ở Berlin tìm đến khu_vực xưa Hùng cư_trú .
</s>
<s> Thật lạ là không ai biết Hùng .
</s>
<s> Thậm_chí cả những người Hùng nhắc đến tên và nói là bạn cũng không biết Hùng .
</s>
<s> Một buổi sáng rất sớm , Thanh đóng vai một người bạn làm_ăn của Hùng thời bên Đức nay về nước , được bạn_bè cho số điện_thoại của Hùng nên gọi .
</s>
<s> " Hùng đấy à ?
</s>
<s> Tao là Mạnh " Quảng_Ninh " ở Berlin với mày đây mà ... " .
</s>
<s> Thanh thao_thao về quá_khứ , tình_hình buôn_bán và hẹn gặp Hùng .
</s>
<s> Hùng nói_năng rất cảnh_giác và cuối_cùng anh ta hỏi : " Thế sao mày biết tên thật của tao ? " .
</s>
<s> Thanh nói đổ đi rồi lảng_tránh bằng hẹn_hò .
</s>
<s> Như_vậy là Hùng có ở Đức nhưng bằng một cái tên khác .
</s>
<s> Qua tìm_hiểu , Thanh mới biết thời_kỳ đó phần_lớn dân VN sang Đức từ một nước châu_Âu khác .
</s>
<s> Ở đó , nhiều người Việt có giấy_tờ xuất_cảnh sang Đức nhưng khi họ quay về thì giấy này có_thể bị bán lại cho người muốn sang .
</s>
<s> Rất nhiều người Việt đã có_mặt ở Đức bằng thứ giấy có tên người khác , dán ảnh mình như vậy .
</s>
<s> Hùng có_thể là một trường_hợp .
</s>
<s> Bài_học của mẹ vợ .
</s>
<s> Thanh trình_bày toàn_bộ kết_quả cho bà Loan và nhận_xét : Hùng là một người tốt , có bản_lĩnh và nay là cán_bộ trẻ có năng_lực .
</s>
<s> Riêng việc học đại_học tuy thiếu chính_xác một_chút LBKT vì đang học chứ không phải đã tốt_nghiệp RBKT , nhưng có_thể thông_cảm .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa bà cũng cần phải hợp_lý_hóa việc vì_sao bà biết những thông_tin Hùng nói_dối .
</s>
<s> Khá đau_đầu , Thanh mới soạn xong một kịch_bản đẹp như mơ cho bà Loan .
</s>
<s> Thông_thường tối thứ_bảy , mẹ_con bà Loan ăn cơm sớm để Hùng đến đón Nụ đi chơi .
</s>
<s> Tuần này bà Loan cố chùng_chình ăn muộn .
</s>
<s> Hùng đến và tất_nhiên phải chờ ở phòng khách .
</s>
<s> Năm phút sau Thanh vào nhà với vai một nhân_viên cùng cơ_quan bà Loan đến chở bà đi thăm người ốm .
</s>
<s> Thanh bắt_chuyện với Hùng và nói : " Tôi trông ông quen_quen ? " .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ vì lịch_sự Hùng cũng nói : " Tôi cũng thấy hình_như gặp ông ở đâu " .
</s>
<s> Thanh vỗ đùi đánh đét rồi hô váng nhà : " Thôi chết rồi !
</s>
<s> Cùng câu_lạc_bộ " trốn học " với nhau rồi !
</s>
<s> Ông là Hùng , lớp tại_chức K7 thương_mại đúng không ?
</s>
<s> Tôi ngồi ngay đằng sau ông .
</s>
<s> Ông đã biết hôm_qua lớp trưởng đọc danh_sách những đứa hay nghỉ học có_thể không được thi chưa ?
</s>
<s> Có cả ông đấy ! " .
</s>
<s> Hùng giật_mình : " Sao tôi không biết ông nhỉ ? " .
</s>
<s> " Thì cả ông lẫn tôi cùng chuyên bỏ học nên sao ông biết được tôi ! " .
</s>
<s> Cùng lúc bà Loan ngậm tăm chậm_rãi đi xuống .
</s>
<s> Hùng ngồi im , mặt đỏ như gấc .
</s>
<s> Thanh đập vai Hùng hét to : " Cô ơi , hóa_ra con rể tương_lai của cô đang học cùng lớp tại_chức với cháu .
</s>
<s> Cùng câu_lạc_bộ " trốn học " với nhau " .
</s>
<s> Bà Loan rành_rẽ : " Mày chỉ huyên_thuyên , anh Hùng tốt_nghiệp đi làm mấy năm rồi " .
</s>
<s> " Khổ quá , ông này còn mượn cả vở cháu .
</s>
<s> Anh_em vừa nhận nhau , còn hẹn hôm nào đến xin thầy cho thi lại đây này ! " .
</s>
<s> Thanh quay sang Hùng : " Ông quê đâu nhỉ ?
</s>
<s> À , tôi còn có danh_sách lớp đây này " .
</s>
<s> Nói rồi Thanh giở danh_sách lớp đọc vanh_vách tên_tuổi , địa_chỉ , điện_thoại của Hùng .
</s>
<s> Hùng thảm_hại như bánh_đa gặp nước .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ đã thấy đủ , bà Loan xách túi đi ra với cả ban_nhạc trong lòng .
</s>
<s> Như dự_đoán của Thanh , mấy hôm sau Hùng gặp bà Loan thưa chuyện .
</s>
<s> Bà yêu_cầu Hùng kể hết những chuyện gì chưa đủ , chưa đúng để bà kiểm_nghiệm và chỉnh_sửa .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ sau lần đó Hùng lễ_độ và khéo xử hơn .
</s>
<s> Bà Loan cũng hiểu Hùng hơn .
</s>
<s> Bà hài_lòng và hả_dạ nên đám cưới Hùng và Nụ đã cử_hành cuối mùa_đông năm ấy .
</s>
<s> Cuộc tình đã được " gói lại " bằng một đám_cưới vui_vẻ .
</s>
<s> Nhưng cuộc_sống không phải lúc_nào cũng kết_thúc có đầu có đuôi như thế , nhất_là khi chuyện vợ_chồng " nhà người_ta " lại đầy phức_tạp với không ít xung_đột , mâu_thuẫn ...
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện truy_tìm kẻ khủng_bố hạnh_phúc gia_đình bằng điện_thoại vì_vậy đã được giao cho thám_tử Cường - một người đàn_ông đã có vợ , khéo_léo và tinh_tế ...
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Khủng_bố bằng điện_thoại : Thả mồi .
</s>
<s> Ngày chủ_nhật đẹp trời , hai vợ_chồng Thu - Thọ ríu_rít sửa_soạn cho bữa tiệc cuối tuần .
</s>
<s> Bỗng điện_thoại_di_động của Thu có tin nhắn .
</s>
<s> Đem máy cho vợ , tiện tay Thọ bấm đọc .
</s>
<s> Những mẩu tin quái_ác .
</s>
<s> Tin viết : " Em thật quá_đáng , dù chúng_mình không còn gì với nhau nữa thì cũng phải nói một lời rõ_ràng .
</s>
<s> Mặt Thọ sa_sầm , giọng lạnh như băng : Em làm gì quá_đáng mà để người_yêu giận này ! " .
</s>
<s> Bỏ con cá làm dở , Thu đọc mẩu tin , mặt tái_mét , tay run như người cảm lạnh .
</s>
<s> Chị bối_rối trước ánh mắt xoáy như mũi khoan của chồng và nói : Em cũng không biết số này của ai .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ là nhầm " ...
</s>
<s> Thọ không nói thêm nhưng lấy bút ra ghi lại số máy này .
</s>
<s> Bữa cơm kết_thúc chóng_vánh .
</s>
<s> Thu đi nghỉ , còn Thọ thở_dài rồi âm_thầm ra box điện_thoại công_cộng gọi vào số máy bí_ẩn kia .
</s>
<s> Anh bấm máy , chuông đổ nhưng không có người nhận .
</s>
<s> Ba lần thay số gọi nhưng máy di_động kia vẫn im_lặng .
</s>
<s> Thọ về .
</s>
<s> Những lần sau anh gọi lại thì số máy này tắt .
</s>
<s> Gia_đình Thọ lại trôi theo cuộc_sống đầy lo_toan , bận_rộn .
</s>
<s> Rồi anh cũng quên dần mẩu tin nhắn khó_chịu kia .
</s>
<s> Nhưng thật tai_ác , khoảng hai tháng sau cũng đúng lúc đang ăn cơm thì điện_thoại của Thu lại có tin nhắn .
</s>
<s> Thọ đọc : Sao em bỏ hẹn mà không báo gì cho anh , làm anh chờ cả buổi .
</s>
<s> Chán thật ! " và cũng của số máy lần trước .
</s>
<s> Thu một lần nữa hốt_hoảng . bối_rối và chị lại nói không biết .
</s>
<s> Thọ khẳng_định đây không_thể là nhầm số được .
</s>
<s> Thọ nói : Đây chỉ là những lần tôi biết , còn những lúc vắng mặt tôi thì " nó " giận_hờn trách_móc cô bao_nhiêu lần ? " .
</s>
<s> Lúc này Thọ mới nhớ ra : Tại_sao những lúc ở nhà cô thường tắt máy ?
</s>
<s> Có phải là cô biết " nó " sẽ nhắn cho cô ? " .
</s>
<s> Trước những câu hỏi của chồng , Thu không có lời giải_thích thuyết_phục .
</s>
<s> Hai vợ_chồng lời_qua_tiếng_lại khá căng_thẳng .
</s>
<s> Đến lúc này buộc Thu phải nói thật : Từ hai tháng trước ngày Thọ đọc được tin nhắn lần đầu , Thu liên_tục bị một số máy lạ nhắn vào máy với những lời_lẽ yêu_đương đắm_đuối .
</s>
<s> Đủ giận_hờn , khen_gợi , hẹn_hò , trách_móc , nghi_ngờ ...
</s>
<s> Thu cho rằng có kẻ nào đó trêu_chọc hay chơi_xỏ mình nên mặc_kệ .
</s>
<s> Chị cũng nghĩ chẳng nên cho chồng biết , chỉ tổ bực_mình và khó_chịu ...
</s>
<s> Thọ hỏi Thu có nghi ai thì Thu nói không ai có dấu_hiệu khả_nghi .
</s>
<s> Nhiều lần Thu đã nhờ người gọi vào số máy đó nhưng vẫn không có người nghe ...
</s>
<s> Hai vợ_chồng quyết_định sát_cánh chống " tin_tặc " .
</s>
<s> Không phải chờ lâu , ngay hôm sau Thu đã mang về cho Thọ một tin : " Hôm_qua anh đã quyết_định quên chuyện chúng_mình mãi_mãi và không bao_giờ nhắn_tin làm_phiền em nữa , nhưng sáng nay thấy em mặc màu đỏ quá đẹp khiến anh không_thể cầm_lòng .
</s>
<s> Đến nước này thì không_thể chịu_đựng hơn được nữa .
</s>
<s> Kẻ nhắn_tin đó lại còn luôn theo sát vợ Thọ hằng ngày .
</s>
<s> Hắn là ai và muốn gì ?
</s>
<s> Tại_sao địa_chỉ hắn nhắn_tin là vợ Thọ chứ không là người khác ?
</s>
<s> Sau nhiều đêm trằn_trọc , vợ_chồng Thọ tìm đến các thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Đồng_minh cũng là đối_thủ .
</s>
<s> Nghe xong câu_chuyện , thám_tử Cường hỏi hai vợ_chồng liệu có khả_năng vợ hoặc chồng bị cạnh_tranh địa_vị hay quyền_lợi với người khác trong cơ_quan hay gia_đình nội ngoại không .
</s>
<s> Họ cho biết : Thọ làm ở công_ty nhà_nước với chức_vụ nhân_viên bình_thường , làm_công ăn lương và không mâu_thuẫn với ai .
</s>
<s> Thu làm ở công_ty khác và cũng không có đặc_quyền_đặc_lợi gì nên không mâu_thuẫn với ai .
</s>
<s> Hai gia_đình nội ngoại của họ đều không có tranh_giành thừa_kế hay chuyện gì khác ...
</s>
<s> Như_vậy lý_do phá_hoại hạnh_phúc , quấy_rối cuộc_sống vì thù_hằn tiền_bạc hay địa_vị là thiếu căn_cứ .
</s>
<s> Qua nghiên_cứu nội_dung những mẩu tin và thông_tin từ hai vợ_chồng Thọ , Cường nhận_định : vấn_đề này thuộc quan_hệ tình_cảm .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện có_thể theo bốn khả_năng .
</s>
<s> Thứ nhất , đây đơn_thuần là sự trêu_chọc .
</s>
<s> Thứ hai , đây là mối quan_hệ tình_cảm giữa Thu và người nhắn_tin nhưng bây_giờ Thu bỏ chạy và đối_phương vừa khủng_bố , đe_dọa vừa trả_thù .
</s>
<s> Thứ ba , đây là một kẻ theo_đuổi Thu nhưng không được đáp lại , hắn hành_động như trên để chia_rẽ hạnh_phúc gia_đình Thu đồng_thời để lôi_kéo Thu .
</s>
<s> Và thứ tư , thủ_phạm thuộc mối quan_hệ của người chồng .
</s>
<s> Điều đáng lưu_ý nhất ở đây là cả hai vợ_chồng khách_hàng đều chưa_thể kết_luận ai là người trung_thực bởi ai cũng có khả_năng là tòng_phạm .
</s>
<s> Thám_tử sẽ phải vừa kết_hợp với cả hai vợ_chồng để chống kẻ quấy_rối , vừa phải kết_hợp với từng người một để theo_dõi người còn lại và thám_tử phải luôn thăm_dò cảnh_giác cả hai ...
</s>
<s> Mọi cơ_hội đều phải tận_dụng triệt_để nhưng mỗi bước_đi đều cần có giới_hạn nhất_định ...
</s>
<s> Sáng hôm sau , Cường gặp riêng Thọ .
</s>
<s> Cường hỏi : " Thâm_tâm anh có nghi_ngờ vợ anh không ? " .
</s>
<s> Thọ cho biết vợ_chồng anh rất hạnh_phúc và Thu chưa có hiện_tượng trăng_gió bao_giờ ...
</s>
<s> Gạn_hỏi kỹ_càng thì Thọ có nhớ một chuyện : kể từ ngày Thu đi làm ở công_ty mới đã bốn năm nay , vợ_chồng anh thường qua_lại nhà giám_đốc của Thu .
</s>
<s> Có lần Thọ thấy khó_chịu bởi sự quan_tâm khác_thường của ông giám_đốc tới vợ mình .
</s>
<s> Qua câu_chuyện , ông có_vẻ rất để_ý đến những chi_tiết nằm ngoài công_việc của Thu .
</s>
<s> Nhưng chuyện cũng chỉ dừng ở đó và Thọ cũng không nghi_ngờ thêm đối_tượng nào nữa .
</s>
<s> Cường dặn : trước_mắt , Thọ về nhà bí_mật đặt dịch_vụ hiện số ở điện_thoại cố_định và nên tránh cầm máy khi có điện_thoại gọi đến nhà .
</s>
<s> Những buổi chiều , Thọ cố_tình về muộn hơn thường_lệ chừng một tiếng .
</s>
<s> Thọ cần giấu Thu cuộc gặp_gỡ hôm_nay .
</s>
<s> Hôm sau Cường lại gặp riêng Thu .
</s>
<s> Anh hỏi thẳng có ai đang theo_đuổi Thu không ?
</s>
<s> Thu nói : vài người có cảm_tình nhưng Thu không cho họ cơ_hội và chuyện đó cũng chỉ sơ_sơ như rất nhiều tình_trạng của những phụ_nữ khác .
</s>
<s> Tóm lại không có gì đáng nghi .
</s>
<s> Cường hỏi Thu có nghĩ tới chuyện một cô gái nào đó yêu Thọ mà làm thế không ?
</s>
<s> Thu nói không loại_trừ ...
</s>
<s> Cường dặn Thu từ mai tạm không dùng điện_thoại_di_động .
</s>
<s> Thu hãy nói với chồng , với đồng_nghiệp ở cơ_quan và một_số bạn_bè thân là mình mất điện_thoại .
</s>
<s> Tuy vẫn nhờ bưu_điện giữ lại số máy cũ nhưng hiện chưa biết nên mua loại điện_thoại nào .
</s>
<s> Chuyện này Thu phải giấu Thọ .
</s>
<s> Hai đồng_minh đồng_thời đều có_thể là đối_thủ của thám_tử , nên Cường đã cùng mỗi người buông một mồi câu giăng bắt thủ_phạm , và chính những mồi câu này của Cường cũng có khả_năng làm lộ diện ngay cả người đang hợp_tác với mình ...
</s>
<s> Ngày_mai cái mồi nào của Cường sẽ dính cá ?
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Khủng_bố bằng điện_thoại : " Tặng_phẩm " cho thủ_phạm .
</s>
<s> Cường giao cho Thu và Thọ mỗi người một " chiếc cần_câu " để buông mồi và canh_giữ nó .
</s>
<s> Mấy hôm sau Thọ đến báo : vợ anh mất điện_thoại , liệu có liên_quan đến thủ_phạm ?
</s>
<s> Cường phân_tích nếu liên_quan càng dễ tìm .
</s>
<s> Người giấu mặt trong buồng điện_thoại công_cộng ?
</s>
<s> Thọ cho biết ngày thứ ba sau khi vợ mất điện_thoại thì có một số máy lạ gọi đến nhà lúc anh chưa đi làm về .
</s>
<s> Số này là ở một buồng điện_thoại công_cộng trên đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh .
</s>
<s> Thời_gian đàm_thoại 4 giây .
</s>
<s> Ngày thứ tư , khi cả hai vợ_chồng Thọ ở nhà thì có một cuộc điện gọi đến và Thọ để vợ nghe máy .
</s>
<s> Thu chỉ nói một câu : " Nhầm số rồi ! " và cúp máy .
</s>
<s> Tối hôm đó , Thọ kiểm_tra lại thì cũng chính là số ở buồng điện_thoại trên đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh .
</s>
<s> Thọ nghi_ngờ số điện_thoại này và đề_nghị đặt máy_ghi_âm nghe trộm các cuộc thoại trong nhà ...
</s>
<s> Cường suy_đoán : có_lẽ sau khi không_thể nhắn_tin vào máy di_động của Thu , kẻ quấy_rối đã quay sang tấn_công điện_thoại cố_định .
</s>
<s> Thủ_phạm là người khá gần Thu và chỉ nằm trong diện những người được Thu cho biết mất máy điện_thoại_di_động .
</s>
<s> Với tình_cảm đặc_biệt , dù là yêu hay ghét mà lại ở gần Thu thì rất khó có chuyện Thu không biết người này là ai .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa hai lần LBKT nếu là người này RBKT gọi điện đến nhà mà Thu cầm máy nghe thì câu đầu_tiên hắn không_thể nói những câu không có thông_tin để đến_nỗi Thu kêu là nhầm máy .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa khi nghe giọng Thu trong máy , tên này sẽ có những lời_nói đặc_trưng LBKT có_thể như trong nhắn_tin RBKT từ mối quan_hệ của hai người .
</s>
<s> Nếu nghe được , đáng_lẽ Thu phải sinh nghi , bám sát hay báo cho chồng để cùng nhau truy_tìm thủ_phạm .
</s>
<s> Nhưng Thu đã vội_vàng dập máy và không báo gì .
</s>
<s> Ngược_lại , Cường không loại_trừ khả_năng Thọ mới là người có quan_hệ với thủ_phạm .
</s>
<s> Thậm_chí có_thể Thọ tự dựng lên với Cường một cái tên nào đó có nhà gần đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh để đánh lạc hướng Cường , che_giấu mối quan_hệ của mình .
</s>
<s> Riêng về đề_nghị đặt máy_ghi_âm điện_thoại gia_đình , Cường khuyên thôi .
</s>
<s> Bởi như thế anh sẽ rất khó kiểm_soát tình_hình , nhất_là khi Thọ phát_hiện điều gì đó của vợ ...
</s>
<s> Cường dặn Thọ nên tiếp_tục theo_dõi .
</s>
<s> Một tuần sau Thọ lại lần_lượt phát_hiện ba số máy từ các buồng điện_thoại sát nhau trên đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh gọi đến nhà và thời_gian đàm_thoại cũng không quá 5 giây .
</s>
<s> Thọ quá sốt_ruột .
</s>
<s> Cường nói : " Anh thử tính xem người quen của vợ anh có ai nhà ở gần đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh hay có ai thường đi học , đi làm buổi tối về qua tuyến đường này ? " .
</s>
<s> Thọ nghĩ mãi nhưng không ra .
</s>
<s> Cường kết_luận : Thọ là người đáng tin .
</s>
<s> Vì nếu anh ta dựng nên chuyện này thì thế_nào cũng đưa ra một_số nhân_vật để đánh lạc hướng Cường .
</s>
<s> Cường nói Thọ hãy kể địa_chỉ nhà một_số người cùng công_ty Thu .
</s>
<s> Thọ liệt_kê từ thanh_niên chưa gia_đình đến ông_già sắp về hưu và khi nhắc đến ông giám_đốc thì Thọ giật_mình : nhà ông ta cách khu_vực có các buồng điện_thoại đó chừng 500 m .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện đến đây cần hết_sức tinh_tế .
</s>
<s> Chiến_hữu đắc_lực .
</s>
<s> Cường phân_tích , nếu kẻ khủng_bố là ngài giám_đốc thì sẽ có một_số hình_thức thực_hiện sau : tự ông ta đi gọi , hoặc nhờ người khác gọi nhưng ông ta quản_lý và giám_sát .
</s>
<s> Và cuối_cùng là ông ta phó_thác cho một kẻ khác .
</s>
<s> Nếu rơi vào hai hình_thức cuối thì mục_tiêu khủng_bố để lôi_kéo và trả_thù là chính .
</s>
<s> Nếu ông ta tự gọi thì rất dễ hai người đã có tình_cảm với nhau , thậm_chí đã có quan_hệ gì đó với nhau , nay Thu bỏ chạy .
</s>
<s> Mục_đích ông ta là chia_rẽ vợ_chồng Thọ để dễ_bề nối lại quan_hệ với Thu .
</s>
<s> Cộng với sự phân_tích tâm_lý Thu thì giả_thiết này có khả_năng nhiều hơn .
</s>
<s> Cường loại_bỏ phương_án một là sẽ phục ở các buồng điện_thoại khả_nghi trong những giờ cao_điểm để " bắt " ngài giám_đốc nọ .
</s>
<s> Vì phương_án này hoặc là kết_quả không đủ tính thuyết_phục hoặc là sẽ gây tổn_thương cho Thọ và câu_chuyện sẽ phức_tạp hơn .
</s>
<s> Cường áp_dụng mưu_kế theo binh_pháp là " xua hổ nuốt sói " .
</s>
<s> Tức_là mình không cần ra_tay mà dắt đường cho kẻ khác xử_lý kẻ_thù của mình .
</s>
<s> Trung_thành với kế_hoạch , Thọ thường_xuyên ngồi bên điện_thoại trong những giờ " cao_điểm " .
</s>
<s> Đúng lúc số điện_thoại ở buồng công_cộng gọi đến , Thọ không nhấc máy mà bấm máy di_động gọi thẳng đến nhà ông giám_đốc kia .
</s>
<s> Như phán_đoán , bà vợ nói ông vừa đi bộ ra ngoài .
</s>
<s> Để chắc_chắn hơn , Thọ đợi lần sau đúng lúc số điện_thoại lạ hiện trên máy cố_định , anh lại gọi về nhà giám_đốc .
</s>
<s> Bà vợ cũng nói ông ta vừa ra ngoài .
</s>
<s> Lần này Thọ xưng rõ danh_tính với bà LBKT vì là chỗ thân_tình LBKT và tâm_sự chuyện gia_đình đang có rắc_rối .
</s>
<s> Thọ hẹn ngày_mai đến cơ_quan bà nhờ tư_vấn , chỉ_bảo .
</s>
<s> Sáng hôm sau , như một người em gặp nạn đang bế_tắc , Thọ kể hết tình_đầu câu_chuyện với bà vợ giám_đốc .
</s>
<s> Anh đưa cho bà toàn_bộ nội_dung các tin nhắn anh có từ máy của Thu , toàn_bộ danh_sách các cuộc gọi lạ từ những buồng điện_thoại công_cộng ở đường Nguyễn_Chí_Thanh cùng ngày , giờ , địa_chỉ cho bà .
</s>
<s> Anh cũng nói rất có_thể đối_tượng đó là người cùng công_ty Thu .
</s>
<s> Anh tin bà biết rõ nội_tình công_ty chồng , cộng với kinh_nghiệm thì bà có_thể giúp anh tìm ra thủ_phạm .
</s>
<s> Mặt bà vợ giám_đốc biến_sắc theo từng tình_tiết câu_chuyện .
</s>
<s> Bà nhận giúp Thọ bằng một lời hứa đanh_thép , cứng nghẹn cổ_họng .
</s>
<s> Cường nhận_định sau khi bà vợ nghe câu_chuyện trên , sự_việc có_thể sẽ diễn theo ba tình_huống : bà âm_thầm theo_dõi cho đến khi bắt được quả_tang ông nhà đang thổn_thức trong hộp điện_thoại công_cộng ; bà sẽ lập_tức lôi ông ra phỏng_vấn với những dữ_liệu đầy bất_lợi cho ông hoặc bà sẽ giao lại việc này cho ông với thái_độ không quan_tâm ...
</s>
<s> Và cho_dù xảy ra tình_huống nào thì ông giám_đốc cũng chột_dạ .
</s>
<s> Không biết bà vợ của ông giám_đốc đã chọn phương_án nào nhưng những mẩu tin và cuộc điện quái_ác từ đó không làm_phiền vợ_chồng Thọ nữa .
</s>
<s> Công_việc của Thu vẫn suôn_sẻ , gia_đình Thọ vẫn trong_ấm_ngoài_êm .
</s>
<s> Và cho đến lúc này cả hai cũng chỉ biết một_nửa câu_chuyện của chính nhà mình .
</s>
<s> Cường cũng không muốn mổ_xẻ câu_chuyện quá_khứ của Thu thêm .
</s>
<s> Bài_học lớn nhất của thám_tử Cường trong vụ_việc này là không phải lúc_nào cũng dựa hoàn_toàn vào thông_tin , nhận_định và sự hợp_tác của khách_hàng .
</s>
<s> Bởi đôi_khi họ không đủ sáng_suốt , thiếu khách_quan , thậm_chí không trung_thực ...
</s>
<s> Bài_học này càng trở_nên vô_cùng quí_giá khi ngày_mai các thám_tử bước vào cuộc truy_tìm kẻ khủng_bố với những mớ bòng_bong rắc_rối , bùng_nhùng chưa từng thấy ...
</s>
<s> Cô sinh_viên mù trên đất Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Tên cô là Nguyễn_Thị_Thanh_Mai , 26 tuổi , ở làng Vân_Gia , xã Trung_Hưng LBKT ngoại_ô thị_xã Sơn_Tây , Hà_Tây RBKT , một vùng địa_linh_nhân_kiệt nằm nép mình bên dòng sông Tích , cạnh đền Và nổi_tiếng xứ Đoài .
</s>
<s> Mai có gương_mặt nghị_lực với nụ cười e_lệ , duy có đôi mắt ngay từ lúc mới sinh ra đã ...
</s>
<s> Những tấm lòng người Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Cha của Mai là ông Nguyễn_Văn_Phúc , 58 tuổi , kể rằng khi hai chị_em cô chào_đời sinh_đôi được vài ngày thì họ phát_hiện cả hai đều bị mù LBKT được vài tháng người chị tắt_thở RBKT .
</s>
<s> Thương con , năm 1990 ông đưa cô về Hà_Nội xin vào Trường Nguyễn_Đình_Chiểu học chữ_nổi .
</s>
<s> Hồi đó , mặc_dù trường không bắt_buộc học_sinh mù học tiếng Anh nhưng cô vẫn tha_thiết xin cô_giáo Nguyễn_Thị_Loan cho học .
</s>
<s> Năm 1996 , được tin quận tổ_chức thi Olympic tiếng Anh lớp 6 , cô Loan dẫn Mai tham_gia và Mai đã giành giải nhất .
</s>
<s> Rồi cô tiếp_tục thi cấp thành_phố .
</s>
<s> Lần này Mai giành giải nhì thi viết , còn phần thi nói thì một phụ_nữ là thành_viên ban giám_khảo tên John_Woodward LBKT đang làm tình_nguyện_viên tại VN RBKT đề_nghị cho cô giải nói tiếng Anh hay nhất .
</s>
<s> Sau đó chính bà John - một người Mỹ nghèo - trực_tiếp dạy cô tiếng Anh và vi_tính rồi lặn_lội trở về nước tìm nguồn tài_trợ đưa Mai sang học một trường mù ở Philadelphia .
</s>
<s> Sau đó bà lại xin cho cô tới học miễn_phí tại trường mù ở Washington .
</s>
<s> Trong khi đó , vì lòng cảm_phục cô gái , ông đem chuyện cô thuật cho một phóng_viên tờ Olympian_Newspaper của thành_phố .
</s>
<s> Tờ báo ra buổi chiều in ngay trang nhất câu_chuyện một bà_già nghèo tốt_bụng đã đưa cô gái mù VN sang Mỹ học , nhưng bà lại sắp phải đưa cô trở về vì không_thể nào lo nổi học_phí .
</s>
<s> Bất_ngờ ngay sáng hôm sau có một phụ_nữ tên Susan_Gilbert LBKT đã nghỉ hưu RBKT sống ngay gần trường gọi điện cho Mai tặng 1.000 USD và nhận tài_trợ cho cô ăn_học từ số tiền thừa_kế của cha bà .
</s>
<s> Và hằng năm cứ tới kỳ hè , bà lại mua vé khứ_hồi để Mai được trở về sống với gia_đình ở Sơn_Tây .
</s>
<s> " Bà John , bà Susan là những ông Bụt đến với đời tôi ...
</s>
<s> Bà Susan hứa sẽ giúp tôi học tới thạc_sĩ - Mai xúc_động - Thứ_sáu tuần này LBKT 3 - 8 RBKT tôi lại bay sang bên đó tiếp_tục kỳ học mới " .
</s>
<s> Cô gái chỉ học bằng ... tai !
</s>
<s> Chỉ còn một kỳ học nữa cô sinh_viên mù VN sẽ tốt_nghiệp đại_học Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Sự chọn_lựa của cô thật bình_dị : học văn_khoa để sau_này trở_thành cô_giáo hoặc người nghiên_cứu văn_học nước_ngoài .
</s>
<s> Trong những năm sống nơi đất Mỹ , cô gái tật_nguyền thành Sơn đã vắt kiệt mình để học , trước_hết là để đáp nghĩa những người đã cưu_mang , đùm_bọc cô , để vượt lên thân_phận thiệt_thòi , để trở về nước " được truyền lại những kiến_thức mà tôi học được cho nhiều bạn VN cũng kém may_mắn như tôi " .
</s>
<s> " Khi sang Mỹ tôi gặp rất nhiều khó_khăn , nhất_là trong giao_tiếp và đi_lại " - cô kể .
</s>
<s> Trước , ngày nào cô cũng tự ra bến đón xe_buýt tới trường .
</s>
<s> Rồi tự ra sân_bay về nước .
</s>
<s> Khi chuyển lên học đại_học , Mai học văn_học bằng tiếng Anh và chuyện học_tập của cô mới " đáng thương " : cô không_thể đọc sách in đã_đành mà sách chữ_nổi cũng không có nên phải " đọc " văn , cảm_nhận , nghiên_cứu văn_chương , tư_liệu thông_qua ... giọng đọc của những người khác !
</s>
<s> " Khi chuyển lên đại_học tôi rất khổ vì cả trường toàn sinh_viên sáng_mắt , chỉ riêng tôi sinh_viên mù .
</s>
<s> Sự khiếm_khuyết nặng_nề trên gương_mặt cô gái trẻ chính là hậu_quả của những độc_tố mà lính Mỹ đã rải xuống VN thuở trước .
</s>
<s> Chỉ duy_nhất Mai là người khiếm_thị nên không giáo_viên nào bõ công " học " chữ_nổi hoặc các " mật_mã " bàn_phím vi_tính để dạy riêng cô mà cứ giảng tự_nhiên .
</s>
<s> Trong giảng_đường tất_cả sinh_viên đều ghi_ghi , chép_chép , chỉ trừ một cô gái mù ngồi lặng_lẽ thu các tri_thức vào băng .
</s>
<s> Sáng và chiều Mai cần_mẫn cầm gậy dò từng bước từ khu nội_trú LBKT hiện cô đã rời nhà bà Susan vào trọ tại ký_túc_xá RBKT tới lớp_học với " học_cụ " duy_nhất là chiếc máy_ghi_âm để thu toàn_bộ bài giảng dài 5 - 6 tiếng đồng_hồ , rồi đêm về lại hì_hục bật những cuộn băng nghe lại , chép ra chữ_nổi , lưu vào vi_tính .
</s>
<s> " Hiếm nhất là sách văn_học chữ_nổi vì sinh_viên hỏng mắt theo văn_khoa không nhiều nên họ không_thể in loại sách ấy hàng_loạt .
</s>
<s> Vì_thế mỗi khi cần tìm một tác_phẩm mới để mày_mò nghiên_cứu thì tôi phải nhờ tổ_chức tình_nguyện LBKT những người chuyên đọc sách cho người mù RBKT hoặc nhờ bạn_bè đọc vào băng .
</s>
<s> Nhưng khó nhất là khi trả_bài cho cô_giáo , tôi không_thể đưa cho họ bảng chữ_nổi mà phải dùng vi_tính chuyển sang chữ_viết vì không giáo_viên nào biết chữ_nổi .
</s>
<s> Theo học văn_khoa , được tôi_luyện trong môi_trường giáo_dục Mỹ , cộng nghị_lực thép nơi một người mù đã giúp Mai nắm_bắt nhiều kiến_thức về văn_học thế_giới .
</s>
<s> Mai mong có một ai đó giúp cô tiếp_cận văn_học VN , lo cho cô một " bến đậu " tại chính mảnh đất VN khi ra trường .
</s>
<s> Khi tôi đọc tặng Mai bài Đôi mắt người Sơn_Tây của nhà_thơ Quang_Dũng , Mai đã khóc ...
</s>
<s> Cuộc_đời dưới vành mũ thám_tử .
</s>
<s> Thủ_phạm đằng sau thủ_phạm : Ham_muốn của người hàng_xóm .
</s>
<s> Đến văn_phòng công_ty thám_tử hôm_nay là người đàn_ông tầm_thước , tuổi ngoại tứ_tuần nói giọng Nam_bộ với vẻ lo_âu hằn trên nét mặt .
</s>
<s> Bóng đen và những lá thư ma .
</s>
<s> Ông nói đang bị khủng_bố , đe_dọa và theo_dõi ráo_riết từ ba tháng nay .
</s>
<s> Kẻ khủng_bố trực_tiếp gặp_mặt , gọi điện , viết giấy ném vào nhà và gửi thư qua bưu_điện đe_dọa ông .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương cảm_giác thường_xuyên có kẻ bám sát mình mỗi khi ông ra khỏi nhà .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương cho biết nơi ông làm_việc là ở phường Láng_Thượng LBKT quận Cầu_Giấy , Hà_Nội RBKT , nơi ông sống là một căn nhà ở phường Kim_Giang LBKT quận Thanh_Xuân RBKT .
</s>
<s> Sống cùng ông là một cô gái tên Kim 27 tuổi , quê ở Bắc_Ninh , làm nghề_tự_do , ông quen và yêu Kim từ ngày ra Hà_Nội công_tác LBKT ba năm trước RBKT .
</s>
<s> Căn nhà được ông thuê từ khi có quyết_định sống chung với Kim .
</s>
<s> Ông và Kim đều chưa có gia_đình riêng .
</s>
<s> Hai người ở với nhau hòa_hợp , chân_thành và hoàn_toàn vì tình_cảm .
</s>
<s> Văn_phòng công_ty ông Chương có 11 nhân_viên đều là người miền Bắc , ông quan_hệ với tư_cách đồng_nghiệp .
</s>
<s> Hai người kết_bạn từ thuở hàn_vi , hợp_tác chân_thành và không đố_kỵ .
</s>
<s> Ngoài_ra , tất_cả các mối quan_hệ xã_hội khác của ông Chương đều đơn_thuần vì công_việc .
</s>
<s> Trong kinh_doanh thì văn_phòng của ông gần_như không có đối_thủ vì những đơn_vị hoạt_động cùng lĩnh_vực ở Hà_Nội rất ít và đều nhỏ_bé , không có sức cạnh_tranh với công_ty ông .
</s>
<s> Các đối_tác phần_lớn không ở Hà_Nội và số còn lại không có khả_năng xung_đột quyền_lợi ...
</s>
<s> Tóm_lại ông không đoán ra kẻ_thù của mình có_thể thuộc dạng nào và vì_sao lại ghét mình .
</s>
<s> Thế nhưng sự khủng_bố , đe_dọa ngày_một gia_tăng cả về tần_số lẫn mức_độ gay_gắt ...
</s>
<s> Người được giao nhiệm_vụ giúp ông Chương là thám_tử Hùng .
</s>
<s> Không có cơ_sở để phán_đoán kẻ khủng_bố quan_hệ với ông Chương ở lĩnh_vực gì , Hùng tập_trung nghiên_cứu hành_vi , cách_thức khủng_bố của họ .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương cung_cấp : lần khủng_bố đầu_tiên xảy ra chừng 7 g tối .
</s>
<s> Trời nhá_nhem , ông Chương từ văn_phòng về bằng xe_ôm .
</s>
<s> Đến đầu ngõ , ông xuống xe đi bộ về nhà .
</s>
<s> Từ trong ngõ có một người đi xe_máy phóng ra ép ông vào tường .
</s>
<s> Hắn dừng xe , ghé vào tai ông rít lên qua kẽ răng , nhỏ nhưng rành_rọt : " Mày cuốn_xéo khỏi Hà_Nội ngay ! " và phóng đi luôn .
</s>
<s> Đó là người đàn_ông to đậm , râu_quai_nón , đầu trọc , hung_dữ , chừng 30 tuổi .
</s>
<s> Lần thứ hai là qua điện_thoại nhà_riêng .
</s>
<s> Người gọi đến xin gặp ông và cũng chỉ nói một câu : " Mày phải cút khỏi Hà_Nội ngay " .
</s>
<s> Lần thứ ba là vào buổi sáng sớm , khi ông dậy tập_thể_dục thì thấy một mảnh giấy nhét vào khe cửa , viết : " Không biến khỏi Hà_Nội thì mày khốn đấy ! " .
</s>
<s> Giấy viết chữ in , cỡ to và có_vẻ cố nguệch_ngoạc .
</s>
<s> Sau ba lần nhét giấy qua khe cửa cũng một nội_dung như_vậy thì kẻ khủng_bố chuyển sang gửi thư qua bưu_điện .
</s>
<s> Dấu bưu_cục đóng trên bì_thư có địa_chỉ ở Hà_Nội .
</s>
<s> Nội_dung cũng tương_tự những thông_điệp trước .
</s>
<s> Thư viết chữ in cỡ to , có_vẻ viết bằng tay_trái hoặc cố_tình viết khác_thường .
</s>
<s> Từ đó đến nay thông_điệp của kẻ khủng_bố đều là gửi thư qua bưu_điện , nội_dung không khác những lần trước ...
</s>
<s> Hùng nhận_định : kẻ khủng_bố ngày_một khôn_ngoan , kín_đáo hơn trong hành_vi của mình .
</s>
<s> Nghiên_cứu về ý_đồ thủ_phạm qua nội_dung thư , Hùng kết_luận : đây không phải là chuyện nợ_nần hay cay_cú vì tiền_bạc , vì không ai lại đuổi con_nợ của mình đi cả .
</s>
<s> Đây cũng rất khó là chuyện mâu_thuẫn trong kinh_doanh vì những chiến_lược phát_triển là do lãnh_đạo công_ty quyết_định .
</s>
<s> Hơn_nữa nếu khủng_bố để ông Chương " cút khỏi Hà_Nội " thì lại có người khác lên thay .
</s>
<s> Mặt_khác , nếu vì cạnh_tranh kinh_doanh thì hình_thức này rất kém hiệu_quả .
</s>
<s> Đây có_thể là chuyện tình_cảm , địa_vị xã_hội hoặc tranh_chấp tài_sản .
</s>
<s> Dấu_hỏi bên kia bờ_rào .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương chỉ có một người hàng_xóm sát vách , thỉnh_thoảng chào_hỏi xã_giao .
</s>
<s> Ông thường đi làm từ 7 g đến 18 g mới về nhà .
</s>
<s> Thời_gian chạm_mặt với hàng_xóm rất ít .
</s>
<s> Hai nhà kín_cổng_cao_tường và không chung_đụng thứ gì .
</s>
<s> Từ ngày chuyển về đây hai bên không một lần va_chạm .
</s>
<s> Tóm_lại ông không có mâu_thuẫn với họ .
</s>
<s> Hùng hỏi : " Từ khi đến đây ông đã từng nói chuyện gì với họ ? " .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương nhớ có một lần bà vợ hàng_xóm nói rất thích căn nhà ông ...
</s>
<s> Hùng giật_mình : " Nhưng đó là nhà ông thuê cơ_mà ? " .
</s>
<s> Ông Chương lúng_túng : " À , xin_lỗi anh , thật_ra đó là nhà tôi mua từ khi muốn ở_riêng với cô Kim " .
</s>
<s> " Vì nhà tôi liên_tục lên giá .
</s>
<s> Nhất_là khi có tin sẽ mở thêm một ngõ phố rộng chạy sát đầu_hồi nhà tôi , lúc đó căn nhà sẽ có hai mặt_tiền .
</s>
<s> Nhà hàng_xóm cũng biết tôi ra Hà_Nội công_tác một thời_gian rồi sẽ về nên họ dặn nếu bán nhà thì ưu_tiên cho họ " .
</s>
<s> " Vậy ông đã nói gì với họ ? " .
</s>
<s> " Tôi cũng chỉ hứa chung_chung rằng nếu có nhu_cầu đó , tôi sẽ nhớ đến họ .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện đó được nhắc đến hai lần , ngắn_gọn trong những lúc chào nhau xã_giao ... " .
</s>
<s> Gia_đình hàng_xóm gồm hai vợ_chồng tuổi ngoài 50 và hai con gái đang học phổ_thông .
</s>
<s> Nhà họ trông vào nguồn thu chủ_yếu từ quán cà_phê , giải_khát mở tại nhà .
</s>
<s> Dân trong ngõ này hầu_hết là giới lao_động và tiểu_thương .
</s>
<s> Từ khi có tin mở ngõ mới đã có một_số người hỏi mua nhà ông Chương , trong đó có gia_đình hàng_xóm ...
</s>
<s> Đến đây Hùng rút ra hai vấn_đề : thứ nhất , ông Chương còn nhiều uẩn_khúc không nói với thám_tử , có nghĩa là thông_tin và nhận_định của ông ta đưa ra chưa_thể tin_cậy ; thứ hai , thủ_phạm khủng_bố là nhà hàng_xóm là có cơ_sở .
</s>
<s> Nếu xét theo nhận_định ban_đầu về nội_dung và cách_thức khủng_bố thì suy_đoán này cũng có logic .
</s>
<s> Để biết rõ hơn , Hùng phải dùng " thuốc_thử " với đối_tượng nghi_vấn .
</s>
<s> Kế_hoạch là ông Chương sẽ cho hàng_xóm biết tin : công_ty trong Nam có kế_hoạch rút ông về .
</s>
<s> Ông rất muốn về nhưng họ chưa thực_hiện kế_hoạch này nên ông chán_nản và sốt_ruột ...
</s>
<s> Kế_hoạch này tinh_tế ở chỗ ông Chương chung nguyện_vọng với nhà hàng_xóm là : đi khỏi Hà_Nội .
</s>
<s> Nhưng vì lý_do khách_quan ông chưa đi được .
</s>
<s> Tuy_nhiên vướng_mắc đó rất có hy_vọng tháo_gỡ .
</s>
<s> Trong hoàn_cảnh này nếu nhà kia có tâm_địa " đuổi " ông Chương , họ sẽ hùa vào cùng bàn phương_án tháo_gỡ với ông .
</s>
<s> Tiến_hành : một buổi sáng chủ_nhật , ông Chương dậy muộn và sang quán cà_phê nhà hàng_xóm uống nước .
</s>
<s> Sau một_vài câu_chuyện xã_giao không dính_dáng tới nhà_cửa hay công_tác , chọn lúc vắng khách nhất thì điện_thoại_di_động của ông Chương đổ chuông .
</s>
<s> Ông bấm máy nói_chuyện với đầu dây bên kia như với một người bạn .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện của ông xoay quanh nội_dung : ông khó_chịu với thời_tiết , món ăn , lối sống ... của Hà_Nội và một_số vướng_mắc khó nói khác .
</s>
<s> Ông rất muốn về Sài_Gòn .
</s>
<s> Công_ty của ông cũng có kế_hoạch rút ông về từ lâu nhưng không biết họ còn chờ gì nữa mà chưa thực_hiện .
</s>
<s> Ông chán_ngán Hà_Nội lắm rồi ...
</s>
<s> Sau cuộc thoại rất sôi_nổi như để giải_tỏa đó , ông Chương thở_dài ngao_ngán và than_vãn mấy câu bâng_quơ .
</s>
<s> Vợ_chồng chủ quán thấy người hàng_xóm có tâm_trạng cũng đến bắt_chuyện chia_sẻ .
</s>
<s> Bà vợ đon_đả hỏi_thăm quê_quán , công_việc của ông Chương và nói tiếp một câu nhẹ_nhàng : Nếu có bán nhà thì anh gọi chúng_tôi nhá ! " .
</s>
<s> Ông chồng thì không nói gì .
</s>
<s> Nghe lại băng ghi_âm và qua mô_tả của ông Chương thì Hùng thấy thái_độ gia_đình này rất bình_thường , không thể_hiện gì lạ .
</s>
<s> Sau lần trao_đổi đó , nhà hàng_xóm không có_vẻ gì săn_đón ông Chương .
</s>
<s> Đặc_biệt là những lá thư khủng_bố vẫn gửi đến đều_đều và nội_dung không thay_đổi .
</s>
<s> Hùng tạm kết_luận : nhà hàng_xóm " trong_sáng " !
</s>
<s> Lúc này , ông Chương lại nhận được một lá thư có nội_dung mới : " Không biến khỏi Hà_Nội thì mày sẽ mất tất_cả ! " .
</s>
<s> Hùng cho rằng đây là chuyện bình_thường .
</s>
<s> Vì theo qui_luật tâm_lý , kẻ khủng_bố đã tăng " đô " .
</s>
<s> Tuy_nhiên , điều Hùng rất mừng là với thông_điệp này có_thể hiểu kẻ khủng_bố không có ý_định đe_dọa tính_mạng ông Chương .
</s>
<s> Nhưng , mất tất_cả !
</s>
<s> Vậy ông Chương đang có những gì và có_thể mất gì ?
</s>
<s> Đó là hướng mới cho thám_tử Hùng khai_thác ngày_mai .
</s>
<s> Tổng_kết cuộc thi viết Phóng_sự - ký_sự 2004 : Đậm_nét cái đẹp trong cuộc_sống .
</s>
<s> Nếu cuộc thi năm 2003 chỉ nhận được 181 bài thì cuộc thi năm 2004 đã nhận được đến 527 bài dự thi .
</s>
<s> Ban sơ_khảo cuộc thi đã chọn đăng trên 50 bài . nghĩa_là bình_quân cứ năm bài dự thi thì có một bài được chọn đăng , vào sơ_khảo .
</s>
<s> Tỉ_lệ ấy chưa phải là cao nhưng cũng cho thấy bản_lĩnh của bạn_đọc trong việc chọn đề_tài và thể_hiện đề_tài .
</s>
<s> " Bạn_đọc biết viết phóng_sự và viết phóng_sự khá tốt " , nhiều người theo_dõi cuộc thi đã nói thế .
</s>
<s> " Nàng tiên nhỏ " trong gia_đình " cái_bang " LBKT của Tiến_Dũng RBKT là một trường_hợp .
</s>
<s> Tác_giả đã phát_hiện nơi làng quê heo_hút của một xã miền núi xa LBKT Nghệ_An RBKT có một cô bé " còn hơn cả vàng_mười " .
</s>
<s> Cô bé lớn lên dưới mái lều tranh rách_nát , trong một gia_đình có bốn thế_hệ phải xách bị_gậy đi ăn_xin .
</s>
<s> Từ thuở mới lọt_lòng , cô bé đã phải quặt_quẹo sau lưng người mẹ địu đi xin ăn khắp đầu_đường_xó_chợ .
</s>
<s> Ấy vậy nhưng khi lên 7 tuổi cô bé không chịu theo mẹ đi ăn_xin nữa , đòi đi học .
</s>

<s> Cha , con và nỗi đau da_cam .

<s> Mình chẳng phải là duy_tâm , mê_tín gì , nhưng nhiều lúc nhìn chúng_nó còng_queo , vô_cảm , mình cứ cầu_trời_khấn_phật cho chúng khỏe_mạnh , nói_năng , đi_lại như con người_ta .

<s> Phải sống .
</s>
<s> Mới 16 tuổi LBKT năm 1971 RBKT Nguyễn_Văn_Quí tình_nguyện nhập_ngũ .

</s>
<s> Từ 1971 - 1975 , ông và đồng_đội chỉ sống trong rừng , lúc Đắc_Tô , Tân_Cảnh LBKT Kon_Tum RBKT , lúc về Ba_Tơ , khi về Sa_Huỳnh LBKT Quảng_Ngãi RBKT .

<s> Năm năm làm anh lính thông_tin hữu_tuyến , Quí và đồng_đội chỉ uống nước suối , ăn rau rừng với bữa cơm , bữa cháo .
</s>
<s> Giải_phóng rồi , Quí cùng đồng_đội vẫn ở lại thêm hai năm để gỡ bom mìn ở Quảng_Nam - Đà_Nẵng .

<s> " Hồi ấy , mình và đồng_đội là những thanh_niên khỏe_mạnh , ăn_uống vào có nhiều lúc thấy hơi choáng_váng , nhức đầu .

<s> Tưởng chỉ có vậy , ai biết cái chất_độc đấy nó để lại cho con_cháu thế này ...
</s>
<s> Là cha , là mẹ , nhìn cảnh con người_ta lành_lặn , chạy nhảy chơi_đùa , ríu_rít đến trường , trông lại các con mình mà đau_đớn , xót_xa .
</s>
<s> Chúng cũng là người , chúng phải được sống .

<s> Vậy_mà quyền được sống của chúng cũng chẳng ra sống vì đau_đớn , bệnh_tật .

<s> Thấy cảnh mẹ_con người_ta ríu_rít đưa nhau đến trường mà thèm .
