</s>
<s> Lại có nhiều khoảnh rừng thông từng được Nhà_nước bỏ tiền ra trồng đã bị đốt cháy sém đang dần khô lá úa cành .
</s>
<s> Còn đây là những cây rừng cổ_thụ đang bị giết chết bằng cách đẽo vỏ xung_quanh gốc làm cây mất nước chết dần LBKT dân rừng gọi_là " ken " RBKT .
</s>
<s> Không_tài_nào xác_định bao_nhiêu cánh rừng bị tàn_phá , chỉ biết giờ_đây đứng nhìn thì " tầm_nhìn_xa trên 10 km " là rẫy .
</s>
<s> Bên cạnh đó , rừng Lộc_Ngãi với diện_tích hơn 3.000 ha , trong đó hơn 300 ha là rừng trồng đang ngày_một thu_hẹp .
</s>
<s> Những người phá rừng vẫn đang ngày_đêm triệt_phá .
</s>
<s> Cứ thế , theo " thổ_địa " thì hết năm này sang năm khác khi cây rừng nằm_xuống cũng là lúc diện_tích đất rừng biến thành đất nông_nghiệp nằm thỏm vào bàn_tay tư_nhân .
</s>
<s> Nguồn lợi này là một trong những lý_do chính khiến nhiều người xông vào phá rừng .
</s>
<s> Lúc này , vào rừng Bảo_Lâm có_thể nghe , thấy các hoạt_động môi_giới , mua_bán rẫy , đất rừng làm trang_trại với diện_tích ít_nhất cũng 10 ha .
</s>
<s> Có rất nhiều nương_rẫy của cán_bộ kiểm_lâm , công_an ... địa_phương đang hiện_diện ở đây đã được Nhà_nước cấp sổ_đỏ .
</s>
<s> " Thổ_địa " khẳng_định phải mất 10 ngày mới đi thực_địa hết những cánh rừng bị tiêu_diệt .
</s>
<s> Chính chủ_tịch huyện Bảo_Lâm , ông Lương_Văn_Minh khi trao_đổi với chúng_tôi vào sáng 11 - 10 cũng thừa_nhận : " Đi vòng_vòng ở ngoài thật_tình không thấy gì đâu , nhưng vô trong thì toàn là những rẫy cà_phê 3 , 4 , 5 tuổi .

<s> Ở đó người_ta đã xây_dựng nhà_cửa hẳn_hoi .

</s>
<s> Đáng nể nhất là khu Nao_Quang nằm cách trung_tâm huyện Bảo_Lâm 25 km với hàng trăm hecta cà_phê , chè_lá lấn chỗ của từng ấy hecta rừng .
</s>
<s> Bảo_vệ rừng làm_ngơ cho phá rừng ?
</s>
<s> Hầu_hết khu rừng bị phá thuộc địa_bàn quản_lý của ban quản_lý LBKT BQL RBKT rừng Bảo_Lâm LBKT trực_thuộc UBND huyện Bảo_Lâm RBKT .

</s>
<s> Còn những năm trước đó ?
</s>
<s> Một phó BQL bộc_bạch : " Chúng_tôi chưa thống_kê hết được " .

<s> Trao_đổi với chúng_tôi , câu đầu_tiên ông Nguyễn_Bá_Đông , trưởng BQL rừng Bảo_Lâm , nói : " Tình_hình như hiện_nay thế là ổn lắm rồi đó " .
</s>
<s> Ông khẳng_định : " Chúng_tôi biết tất_cả những đối_tượng phá rừng nhưng không_tài_nào bắt quả_tang , do_vậy không sao xử_lý được .
</s>
<s> Tại Lộc_Ngãi , chúng_tôi đã xác_định có một làng lâm_tặc đấy , nhưng thật_tình cũng chưa_thể làm gì .
</s>
<s> Rừng Lộc_Ngãi từng được giao cho công_an huyện , huyện_đội , tỉnh_đội rồi xã , thôn quản_lý nhưng không hiệu_quả .

<s> Nay giao lại cho BQL khiến chúng_tôi cũng đau đầu " .

<s> Nhưng chính người dân địa_phương này khẳng_định chỉ có sự làm_ngơ của những người_quản_lý rừng thì người_ta mới dám phá rừng ?
</s>
<s> " Dư_luận thì có chuyện đó , nhưng thực_tế không phải vậy đâu " , ông Đông nói .

<s> Theo ông Đông , trước đây có chuyện người dân xã Lộc_Phú làm đơn tố_cáo ông Lê_Văn_Tú LBKT cán_bộ BQL rừng quản_lý cụm tiểu_khu Lộc_Phú RBKT đã lợi_dụng chức_vụ để bán đất lâm_nghiệp , thuê người phá rừng .

<s> Sau khi tiếp_nhận đơn , Hạt kiểm_lâm Bảo_Lâm đã lập đoàn kiểm_tra nhưng không phát_hiện chuyện đó .

<s> Có_thể do ông Tú làm_việc quá căng nên bị dân ghét !

</s>
<s> Chỉ xác_định được hai vị_trí thể_hiện rõ hành_vi bán đất và lấn_chiếm đất của ông Tú và người_làm .

<s> Lớn lên lại theo nghiệp làm nông , rồi cưới vợ , sinh con , yên bề gia_thất .
</s>
<s> " Tui làm đủ thứ nghề , trồng lúa , nuôi heo , nuôi bò , rảnh thì đi làm_thuê kiếm sống , nhưng cái khó nghèo vẫn mãi đeo_bám suốt mấy chục năm ... " - anh Kiệm tâm_sự .
</s>
<s> Trong cảnh khó nghèo quá , làm ra lúa bán rẻ , tính_toán không đủ tiền công , phân_bón , anh nghĩ đem gạo ra chế_biến để bán may_ra khá hơn ...
</s>
<s> Thế_là anh quyết_định mở lò bún .
</s>
<s> Lúc đầu do làm thủ_công , không kiếm được bao_nhiêu lại quá cực_nhọc .
</s>
<s> " Trong đầu tui lúc đó chỉ nghĩ đến một điều là -H_làm_sao vút sạch gạo mà không cần phải dùng bằng tay thì đỡ công biết_mấy " - anh Kiệm tâm_sự .
</s>
<s> Tính thông_minh , lại tò_mò , anh Kiệm bắt_đầu đi đến các xưởng cơ_khí để quan_sát các loại máy_móc , rồi về nhà suy_nghĩ và cầm bút vẽ phác_họa ra cái máy vút gạo .
</s>
<s> Ròng_rã suốt 10 ngày quên ăn , quên ngủ , cuối_cùng đồ_án chiếc máy vút gạo đã hình_thành trên giấy .
</s>
<s> Có tiền , anh tức_tốc tìm đến các bãi phế_liệu lục tìm mua ống sắt phi 76 , ruột xoắn và nhiều sắt thép phế_liệu khác , rồi đón xe_khách ra Đà_Nẵng , tìm đến chợ_trời bán đồ cũ mua một môtơ .
</s>
<s> Hơn sáu ngày sau , cỗ máy hoàn_thành và đi vào vận_hành mà như lời anh mô_tả là theo " nguyên_lý trục xoắn " , và cho chạy thử_nghiệm .
</s>
<s> Lúc đầu anh đổ thử 1 kg gạo , chỉ trong nháy_mắt gạo được đánh sạch_bóng , đem gạo ra vo thử không có chút nước đục .
</s>
<s> Anh kết_luận : thành_công .
</s>
<s> " Cái được của chiếc máy này là vừa vút được gạo sạch , vừa đãi được sạn .
</s>
<s> Bây_giờ thì làm sạch 200 kg gạo chỉ mất 15 phút , không cần phải có người theo_dõi .
</s>
<s> Chỉ cần đổ gạo vào máy , bắt nước chảy vô và bật máy .
</s>
<s> Chỉ trong vòng một tuần sau , những người làm bún trong vùng , rồi các tỉnh tìm đến xem máy vút gạo của anh .
</s>
<s> Sau khi chứng_kiến , họ lại đặt_hàng anh sản_xuất cung_cấp máy .
</s>
<s> Bắt_đầu từ đó anh lại tất_bật với công_việc chế_tạo chiếc máy vút gạo làm bún độc_quyền cho khách_hàng .
</s>
<s> Đam_mê chế_tạo_máy .
</s>
<s> Đến đầu năm 2004 , sau gần hai tháng mày_mò chế_tạo , anh lại trình_làng chiếc máy lọc sạn muối 1 - 5 li , làm bất_ngờ giới thầu vật_liệu xây_dựng trong vùng .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện chế_tạo chiếc máy lọc sạn cũng khá bất_ngờ .
</s>
<s> Nhận thấy nhu_cầu cát xây_dựng ngày_một tăng , lại sống ven sông , anh nảy sang ý_định khai_thác cát cung_cấp cho xây_dựng .
</s>
<s> Những vị khách khó_tính này đòi_hỏi sạn muối phải khai_thác tại Duy_Trung và đảm_bảo tiêu_chuẩn , bởi đây là loại vật_liệu dùng cho thi_công công_trình trọng_yếu với yêu_cầu kỹ_thuật cao .
</s>
<s> " Ký hợp_đồng xong , tui về ngồi nghĩ_lại thấy toát mồ_hôi , làm thế_nào để cung_cấp đủ lượng sạn như hợp_đồng , lại theo qui_chuẩn ngặt_nghèo ... " - anh Kiệm tâm_sự .
</s>
<s> Theo tính_toán , để làm ra 1 m3 sạn muối theo qui_chuẩn đã ký_kết thì phải mất ít_nhất bốn người làm trong một ngày , mà giá sạn lại thấp , _làm_sao đủ trả tiền công , nếu không tìm cách thì với hợp_đồng này anh chỉ còn nước bán nhà để đền hợp_đồng .
</s>
<s> Hơn 20 ngày sau khi ký hợp_đồng , anh bỏ ăn , bỏ ngủ , đêm nào cũng thức trắng đi vô , đi ra với tờ giấy khổ lớn trên tay , cuối_cùng bản_vẽ chiếc máy lọc sạn muối cũng được hoàn_thành .
</s>
<s> Máy chạy , những hạt sạn muối đúng chuẩn ào_ào lọt ra từ chiếc máy ...
</s>
<s> Anh mời đơn_vị ký hợp_đồng vào nghiệm_thu sản_phẩm , họ gật đầu đồng_ý ngay .
</s>
<s> Anh Kiệm đưa tay chỉ chiếc máy và cho biết : " Chỉ cần hai người vận_hành , mỗi giờ có_thể sàng được từ 5 - 10 m3 .
</s>
<s> Chủ_tịch UBND xã Quế_Xuân 1 Lê_Trung_Thành không tiếc lời khi kể về anh nông_dân Nguyễn_Văn_Kiệm : " Cũng nhờ anh Kiệm mà bà_con nông_dân trong vùng bớt khổ , thoát cái cảnh quanh_năm bán mặt cho đất bán lưng cho trời ...
</s>
<s> Bây_giờ thì anh Kiệm đã trở_thành kỹ_sư chuyên chế_tạo_máy cho bà_con nông_dân trong vùng , khi bà_con yêu_cầu là anh sẵn_sàng đáp_ứng không đòi_hỏi lời_lỗ ... " .
</s>
<s> Dankia vẫn lặng_lẽ " nhỡ_nhàng " ...
</s>
<s> Đứng trên đỉnh Lang_Bian nhìn xuống , người_ta mê_mẩn cảnh Dankia dưới kia .
</s>
<s> 110 năm trước , Yersin đã bàng_hoàng trước vẻ đẹp của vùng rừng_núi ấy , để rồi bừng lên ý_tưởng về một thành_phố nghỉ_dưỡng .
</s>
<s> Nhưng rồi Đà_Lạt ra_đời lại không nằm ở Dankia , mà bên suối Lat LBKT hồ Xuân_Hương nay RBKT .
</s>
<s> Vậy nên vùng_đất tuyệt đẹp kia vẫn mãi nằm lặng_lẽ , quyến_rũ , gọi mời ...
</s>
<s> Phận " hồng_nhan " .
</s>
<s> Sáng nay phóng xe_máy từ Cam_Ly vào Dankia bất_chợt tôi bàng_hoàng : một con đường sang_trọng , vút dài bóng mượt , giữa một rìa phía tây trải xuống cánh cung đông_bắc còn gần như nguyên_sơ của thành_phố cao_nguyên đã hình_thành .
</s>
<s> Nghe_đâu không dưới 50_tỉ đồng đã đổ xuống con đường suốt hai năm qua .
</s>
<s> Ấy thế mà con đường sao vắng_lặng , hiếm bóng người , xe_cộ , tựa như " thoát_ly " khỏi thành_phố du_lịch này .
</s>
<s> Điểm cuối của con đường là vùng sơn_thủy gần như trinh_nguyên mà ta có_thể nhìn thấy nó từ đỉnh cao hơn 1.900 m của dãy Lang_Bian .
</s>
<s> Nơi đây ngày nào Yersin đã đề_nghị xây_dựng một trung_tâm nghỉ_dưỡng độc_đáo nhất Đông_Dương trên cao_nguyên .
</s>
<s> Dự_án du_lịch này muốn xây_dựng ở đây một " Đà_Lạt thứ hai " , một vùng nghỉ_dưỡng thượng_hạng trên thế_giới , trải ra trên diện_tích rộng tới 5.000 ha , với hệ_thống villa hàng trăm cái ẩn trong những mép rừng thông , khách_sạn năm sao , trung_tâm thương_mại , casino , sân golf thi_đấu quốc_tế , cáp treo , trường đua ngựa ...
</s>
<s> Đầu năm 1998 , dự_án được Chính_phủ phê_duyệt .
</s>
<s> Mọi người chờ_đợi hi_vọng về một " thành_phố thứ hai trên cao_nguyên Lang_Bian " ...
</s>
<s> Nhưng rồi kinh_tế châu_Á bị khủng_hoảng và ... thế_là " Dankia_Resort " ... chết_đứng : nhà_đầu_tư biệt_tăm , còn " nàng sơn_nữ " Dankia xinh_đẹp tiếp_tục " nhỡ_nhàng " .
</s>
<s> " Đón_đầu " ...
</s>
<s> Nhưng Dankia không yên_ổn ...
</s>
<s> Những người làm_vườn nằm ven con đường Cam_Ly đi Dankia hay Tùng_Lâm LBKT hai hướng đường vừa được mở nhưng đều tụ về vùng Dankia RBKT , rồi cả những người thả trâu hoang , chăn ngựa nói với tôi rằng đang có rất nhiều người đổ_xô vào mua đất ở gần đấy .
</s>
<s> Khu Dankia - Suối_Vàng thuộc địa_bàn thành_phố Đà_Lạt và huyện Lạc_Dương .
</s>
<s> Với kiểu " đón_đầu " dự_án , nhiều năm qua đã có rất nhiều người đến đây lấn_chiếm đất rừng trái_phép , mua_bán sang_nhượng đất lâm_nghiệp với mục_đích " đầu_cơ đất " với diện_tích lên đến hàng trăm hecta , trong đó có không ít người là cán_bộ các cấp của địa_phương .
</s>
<s> Được biết , trước_đây do có nhiều " khó_khăn " nên việc thanh_tra , xử_lý những trường_hợp vi_phạm đã không được thực_hiện .
</s>
<s> Một thành_viên đoàn thanh_tra cho biết chậm nhất đến ngày 26 - 10 – 2003 sẽ có kết_quả chính_thức của cuộc thanh_tra để tỉnh có biện_pháp xử_lý kiên_quyết những trường_hợp vi_phạm .
</s>
<s> Phía bên trong của vùng rừng mênh_mông này bây_giờ người_ta có_thể dễ_dàng nhìn thấy những trang_trại đâm thủng đại ngàn .
</s>
<s> Hàng chục trang_trại nằm rải_rác đây_đó trong khu_vực được gọi tên là Suối_Cạn LBKT thuộc ban quản_lý rừng_phòng_hộ Sêrêpôk RBKT và nhiều lâm phận không tên khác .
</s>
<s> Một_vài chủ trang_trại nói với tôi là đang rao bán những rẫy cà_phê , từ 1 - 3 ha , với giá 200_triệu đến hàng tỉ đồng có giấy chứng_nhận quyền sử_dụng đất do chính_quyền huyện Lạc_Dương cấp .
</s>
<s> " Hầu_như tất_cả những người sở_hữu trang_trại ở đây đều là nhân_viên ban quản_lý rừng_phòng_hộ Sêrêpôk ! " - một người chủ trang_trại ở khu_vực Suối_Cạn nói .
</s>
<s> Cứ thế , dưới bóng thông ngàn , đây_đó những con đường bị ủi tung , đỏ_lòm đất bazan , những trang_trại ra_đời và tồn_tại ...
</s>
<s> Cây cà_phê , cây hồng ... đang thách_đố cây thông .
</s>
<s> " Trang_trại mà đã xuất_hiện thì -H_làm_sao rừng yên ! " , ông Phạm_Văn_Án - chi_cục trưởng Kiểm_lâm tỉnh Lâm_Đồng - đã từng nói vậy .
</s>
<s> ... Và " xơi_tái " .
</s>
<s> Ngay bên dưới hồ Dankia , một loạt những hàng_quán , lều , chòi , từ tranh tre đến gỗ thông , rồi gạch đá , ximăng ... , từ tạm_bợ đến kiên_cố hối_hả xuất_hiện .
</s>
<s> Ở đây người_ta tổ_chức cho thuê từ đồ cải_trang LBKT cho giống người Lạch để chụp hình RBKT , ngựa , thợ hình , phục_vụ ăn_nhậu , có quầy bán hàng đặc_sản , áo_quần , và cả ... du_thuyền để chữ " Dankia " cho sang ...
</s>
<s> Và thế_là cái hồ giữ nhiệm_vụ cung_cấp nước_sạch cho cả TP Đà_Lạt , hằng ngày bao_nhiêu là phân ngựa , rác_rưởi thải xuống , rồi có cả mấy cái WC nằm chỉ cách mép nước vài mét nữa .
</s>
<s> Một khu du_lịch chụp_giật đã ra_đời mà chính_quyền không hay .
</s>
<s> Mới_đây , tổng_cục_trưởng Tổng_cục Du_lịch Võ_Thị_Thắng vào đến tận đây , rồi người_ta thấy bà lắc_đầu ngao_ngán .
</s>
<s> Nhưng đó_đây vẫn còn những người chú_tâm nhìn về Dankia , vẫn hi_vọng ...
</s>
<s> Dankia ơi , hãy chờ nhé !
</s>
<s> 17 năm trên ốc_đảo .
</s>
<s> Trên bãi đất bồi mà người địa_phương gọi là cồn Giá nổi lên như một ốc_đảo hoang_vu giữa bốn bề trời nước của đầm Cầu_Hai LBKT một đầm lớn ở phía nam Thừa_Thiên - Huế RBKT , đã ra_đời một trang_trại nuôi tôm với hệ_thống bờ_đập , kênh_mương , ao_hồ công_phu .
</s>
<s> Đó là kết_quả của cuộc vật_lộn bền_bỉ gần 17 năm của Huỳnh_Đỗi .
</s>
<s> Câu_chuyện về anh hấp_dẫn như trong phim Ốc_đảo .
</s>
<s> Từ căn chòi chơ_vơ ...
</s>
<s> Cái buổi ban_đầu của Đỗi là năm 1986 .
</s>
<s> Sau những lần đi thu_gom tôm đất do ngư_dân đánh_bắt dưới đầm để bán cho nhà_máy chế_biến hải_sản xuất_khẩu , anh phát_hiện trong đó có lẫn những con tôm_sú .
</s>
<s> Lại nghe kể đâu_đó ngoài Quảng_Công , Quảng_Ngạn người_ta đang nuôi tôm_sú xuất_khẩu .
</s>
<s> Sao mình không thử nuôi xem sao ?
</s>
<s> Vậy_là Đỗi lặng_lẽ đào đắp , biến mảnh ruộng trước nhà thành hồ nuôi tôm .
</s>
<s> " Đời_thuở mô con tôm mà lại nuôi ? " , người dân thôn Trung_Hưng trố mắt ngạc_nhiên , vì từ bao đời nay họ chỉ biết đánh_bắt con tôm , con cá tự_nhiên trong đầm .
</s>
<s> Ông chủ_nhiệm hợp_tác_xã thì kiên_quyết bắt Đỗi phải lấp hồ để cấy lúa .
</s>
<s> Sau khi xem tận_mắt việc nuôi tôm ở Quảng_Công , một xã ven phá Tam_Giang có vị_trí tương_tự như Vinh_Hưng , chủ_tịch xã đã hiểu ra việc_làm của Đỗi mới chính là cách làm_giàu bằng thế mạnh đầm_phá , liền phát_động dân nuôi tôm .
</s>
<s> Đỗi là người đầu_tiên viết đơn , nhưng lại xin cấp đất ở ngoài tận cồn Giá .
</s>
<s> Cái bãi bồi hoang_vu trước_đây có cấy lúa , nhưng vì nhiễm mặn nên đã bị bỏ quên từ lâu .
</s>
<s> Chủ_tịch Trần_Đình_Quang lắc_đầu : " Nếu anh nuôi trong bờ thì xin mấy xã cũng cấp , còn ngoài đó phiêu lắm " .
</s>
<s> Nhưng Đỗi vẫn kiên_quyết : " Tui đã đi coi hết cả vùng , tính kỹ lắm rồi mới xin ra ngoài đó , các anh cứ tin tui đi " .
</s>
<s> Vậy_là xã đành cho Đỗi mặc_sức mà khai_hoang cái cồn giá_lạnh đó .
</s>
<s> Thuở ban_đầu , anh dựng một cái chòi trên cồn .
</s>
<s> Đỗi thuyết_phục ông anh rể và cậu em_trai cùng tham_gia , đồng_thời đốc_thúc vợ chạy quanh nội ngoại , bạn_bè , vay mỗi người một_vài trăm ngàn để chuẩn_bị cuộc " tiến_công " ra cồn Giá .
</s>
<s> Nhân_công đã mời , vật_liệu đã tập_kết thì 9 giờ tối ông anh rể bỗng_nhiên hạ giọng : " Cậu Đỗi ơi , tui không làm nữa " , cậu em_trai cũng thối_chí xin lui luôn .
</s>
<s> Đỗi không nói một lời , lẳng_lặng đi nằm nhưng suốt đêm cái đầu cứ thao_thức .
</s>
<s> Ruộng vườn vốn hẹp lại nhiễm mặn ; sống nhờ con tôm , con cá trời cho thì chỉ qua_ngày , tương_lai mờ_mịt lắm ; đi vào Nam mà tay_trắng cũng chỉ bán vé_số .
</s>
<s> Muốn sống được với cái đầm Cầu_Hai này thì phải tự nuôi lấy con tôm , con cá .
</s>
<s> Mờ sáng , hỏi ý vợ .
</s>
<s> Vợ bảo tùy anh .
</s>
<s> Vậy_là Đỗi kéo quân ra cồn , quần_quật suốt cả mấy tháng trời và những con đê , bờ đập đã dần thành_hình .
</s>
<s> Vay được bao_nhiêu tiền , anh đều đổ vào mua vật_liệu .
</s>
<s> Tre mua lần cả vườn , đá thuê đò qua tận Đá_Bạc chở về .
</s>
<s> Dân_làng xì_xào : " Phải có công_ty mô đó sau lưng thì thằng Đỗi mới làm dữ_dằn rứa " .
</s>
<s> Không ai biết rằng anh đã nợ ngập_đầu .
</s>
<s> Nhưng đợi mãi chẳng thấy gì , trong khi vợ và đàn con phải khổ_ải theo anh .
</s>
<s> Một cái chòi nhỏ chưa đầy 5 m2 vừa là chỗ nấu , chỗ ăn , chỗ ngủ chơ_vơ giữa bãi cồn hoang_vu .
</s>
<s> Trời mưa lớn coi như phải nhịn_đói .
</s>
<s> Đêm khuya con_bé trở_mình lăn rớt xuống hồ , chị vợ nhảy xuống vớt lên kịp .
</s>
<s> " Trăng lặn tui mới về đến chòi , thấy hai mẹ con ôm nhau khóc , ruột_gan tui cứ đứt từng đoạn " .
</s>
<s> Một lần chị vợ chèo chiếc đò xập_xệ đi bán ký tôm để mua gạo , bị thuyền máy đâm chìm suýt chết .
</s>
<s> Một đêm mưa bão , nhằm lúc anh đi vắng , một_mình chị sợ tôm trôi , lội nước mò đất be bờ mệt xỉu ngoài đê .
</s>
<s> Mấy đứa con khóc kêu mẹ khản cả cổ .
</s>
<s> " Về đi ông Đỗi ơi , ông đày_ải vợ_con chết mất " , ngay cả người làm_công cho anh thấy cảnh đó cũng nản_lòng .
</s>
<s> Với cơ_ngơi hồ đập đó , anh đã được ngân_hàng cho vay 30_triệu .
</s>
<s> " Tui đi ra khỏi ngân_hàng với một balô tiền_lẻ mà hồn bay lên tận trời " .
</s>
<s> Nhưng liên_tục ba năm liền tôm chết , giá rớt , nợ ngân_hàng bắt_đầu " sinh_con_đẻ_cháu " , tiếng_ra_tiếng_vào bao_vây bốn phía , sức chịu_đựng của vợ_con cũng đến đỉnh_điểm .
</s>
<s> Dân_làng nhìn Đỗi như một người điên .
</s>
<s> Trong một cơn cùng_quẫn , Đỗi đã tưới dầu lên chiếc đò rách_nát , rồi chở cả vợ_con chạy ra giữa đầm toan nổi lửa để chấm_dứt mọi sự khổ_ải .
</s>
<s> May_sao bà_con bạn_bè đến cứu kịp .
</s>
<s> Ngân_hàng biết chuyện cũng cử người về an_ủi , khoanh nợ và cho vay tiếp 10_triệu .
</s>
<s> Đỗi đã quay trở_lại cồn Giá và mười năm sau trở_thành người giàu nhất xã Vinh_Hưng .
</s>
<s> ... Đến trang_trại hàng_đầu của tỉnh .
</s>
<s> Đỗi đưa chúng_tôi đi thăm cơ_ngơi của anh mà theo đánh_giá của Sở Thủy_sản Thừa_Thiên - Huế là đã trở_thành một mô_hình trang_trại nuôi tôm .
</s>
<s> Từ 5 ha ban_đầu , đến nay trại tôm của Đỗi đã phát_triển đến 12 ha , đó là chưa kể 2 ha anh đã nhường cho bà_con trong làng .
</s>
<s> Theo chân anh đã có thêm gần 200 hộ kéo ra khai_hoang hết 200 ha cồn Giá , tạo thành một khu nuôi tôm sầm_uất giữa đầm Cầu_Hai .
</s>
<s> Đỗi chỉ cho tôi xem con đê dài gần 500 m , ngăn con lạch : " Đêm trăng , tui xắn đất , mụ vợ mang bầu vác đất đắp con đập này đấy " .
</s>
<s> Tất_cả đều làm bằng tay , vì ở ngoài này kiếm đâu ra xe xúc , máy_điện .
</s>
<s> Đỗi xây ngôi nhà , đưa vợ_con lên bờ ; tiếp đó , bỏ vốn 500_triệu mở một cây xăng_dầu để cung_ứng vật_tư cho vùng nuôi tôm .
</s>
<s> Đỗi chỉ vào ngôi nhà cấp bốn nhỏ_bé của mình , nói : " Nhiều người hỏi tui răng không chịu xây ngôi nhà kha_khá mà ở .
</s>
<s> Tui hỏi , ngôi nhà to có sinh_lợi được không ?
</s>
<s> Nuôi tôm lãi trăm , nhưng nuôi con ăn_học đỗ_đạt thì lãi ngàn , lãi vạn " .
</s>
<s> Đỏ đen gà_chọi .
</s>
<s> Các sới chọi gà vẫn cứ ngang_nhiên tồn_tại , có lúc công_khai rầm_rộ , có lúc lén_lút .
</s>
<s> Những tay chơi gà vẫn tự lấp_liếm cái thú đam_mê cờ_bạc của mình bằng triết_lý " chơi gà_chọi là cái nợ_đời " .
</s>
<s> Nó đã trở_thành một nghề hẳn_hoi , đó là nghề " bạc gà " ...
</s>
<s> Nhập sới .
</s>
<s> Phường gà Ninh_Xá cách thủ_đô Hà_Nội hơn 30 km đường ngay trung_tâm thị_xã Bắc_Ninh .
</s>
<s> Thế nhưng không có sự dẫn đường của Tuấn " cụt " , một tay " bạc gà " lão_luyện đất Bắc_Ninh , tôi khó có_thể tìm được đường vào .
</s>
<s> Nó là một mảnh vườn rộng chừng 200 m2 nằm ẩn sâu trong ngõ chợ Đọ , phường Ninh_Xá , thị_xã Bắc_Ninh .
</s>
<s> Bãi để xe chật kín với đủ các biển số xe từ Hải_Dương , Hà_Nội , Quảng_Ninh ... cho đến Thái_Bình .
</s>
<s> Nơi lòng sới , dân đá gà vây kín , tất_cả đều dán mắt vào cặp gà đang đá nhau chí_tử .
</s>
<s> Con tía lửa LBKT màu đỏ RBKT đến từ Hà_Nội có_vẻ thắng_thế hơn , con ô LBKT màu đen RBKT bản_địa vẫn điềm_tĩnh thủ_thế .
</s>
<s> Cứ mỗi đòn buông ra là cả sới gà như nổ tung bởi những tiếng bình_phẩm xuýt_xoa ... và những lời khích_bác nhau .
</s>
<s> Phần_đông là dân cá_độ chuyên_nghiệp , số còn lại dính đến cá_độ theo lối " tài_tử " .
</s>
<s> Trận này đôi gà đá " bằng_phân " nhau - tức năm ăn , năm thua .
</s>
<s> Tuấn " cụt " , vốn đã nhẵn_mặt ở phường gà này , đặt_cược cho con ô .
</s>
<s> Tôi rút tờ 100_._000 đồng đặt theo để xem thử cảm_giác cá_cược gà thế_nào .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ so với dân bạc gà , tôi là thằng đặt_cược hạng bét .
</s>
<s> Cả sới gà bỗng nhao lên vì con gà ô bắt_đầu phản đòn .
</s>
<s> Sau cú đá hiểm_hóc của con gà ô , Tuấn " cụt " dâng luôn tỉ_lệ cá_cược từ năm ăn , năm thua lên năm ăn một .
</s>
<s> Lại một đòn nữa của con ô .
</s>
<s> Cả sới gà náo_động .
</s>
<s> Lượng tiền " cốp " tăng chóng_mặt , tỉ_lệ cá_cược thay_đổi liên_tục .
</s>
<s> Đã hết hồ thứ sáu LBKT mỗi trận được tính làm 10 hồ - hiệp đấu , mỗi hồ 15 phút RBKT , cặp gà vẫn chưa phân thắng_bại .
</s>
<s> Sới tạm nghỉ cho hai đấu_thủ hồi_sức , dân đá gà tản ra ngồi uống nước .
</s>
<s> Tuấn " cụt " tỏ ra rất vui vì đã dốc gần 5_triệu cho trận đá này .
</s>
<s> Chân_dung những kẻ " bạc gà " .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ cuộc_đời của Tuấn " cụt " đã là một minh_chứng tiêu_biểu cho triết_lý " chơi gà_chọi là cái nợ_đời " .
</s>
<s> Hắn biết chơi gà và ham gà_chọi từ ngày còn " thò_lò_mũi_xanh " , đến nay hắn đã 41 tuổi .
</s>
<s> Gần 30 năm lăn_lộn trong nghề đã khiến hắn trở_thành một tay bạc gà lão_luyện của vùng Bắc_bộ .
</s>
<s> Hắn đã lập gia_đình , nhưng cái gia_đình ấy đã tan_vỡ .
</s>
<s> Thế nhưng mức_độ chơi bạc gà của Tuấn " cụt " chưa ăn_thua gì so với Hậu " trọc " .
</s>
<s> Dân đá gà miền Bắc chỉ biết hắn có hộ_khẩu thường_trú tại Hà_Nội chứ không ai biết chính_xác hắn làm nghề gì .
</s>
<s> Hắn thường hay bê gà đi khắp các sới bằng chiếc ôtô hiệu Camry trị_giá vài chục ngàn USD của mình .
</s>
<s> Nói đến chân_dung những kẻ bạc gà không_thể quên những tay chủ sới .
</s>
<s> Phần_nhiều họ là những thành_phần có " máu_mặt " ở địa_phương , nếu chỉ là người bình_thường chắc chẳng đủ gan để mở một sới ngay giữa ban_ngày_ban_mặt .
</s>
<s> Họ đồng_thời cũng là những " tín_đồ " của " đạo bạc gà " .
</s>
<s> Họ mở sới không phải chỉ là tạo sân_chơi " lành_mạnh " cho dân mê gà mà cốt để kinh_doanh , thu tiền sới sau mỗi trận đấu , trong đó bao_gồm cả " phí an_ninh " , " phí liên_lạc " .
</s>
<s> Đó là chưa kể hàng trăm thứ dịch_vụ kèm theo như ăn_uống , giữ xe ... với mức giá cắt_cổ .
</s>
<s> Tính nhẩm ra nếu ngày nào đông khách mỗi phường gà thu_nhập không dưới tiền triệu .
</s>
<s> Mỗi sới gà đều có lịch đá cụ_thể .
</s>
<s> Cách tổ_chức đá gà ở những phường gà này đều mang đậm tính chuyên_nghiệp .
</s>
<s> Có sới đá liền cả tuần như sới Vạn_Phúc , Hà_Đông , có sới đá hai ngày một tuần như sới đền Đô , Từ_Sơn , Bắc_Ninh LBKT thứ_ba , thứ_năm RBKT hay sới Yên_Sở , Tây_Hồ , Hà_Nội LBKT thứ_bảy , chủ_nhật RBKT .
</s>
<s> 1.001 thủ_đoạn .
</s>
<s> Nếu sơ_ý bắt phải gà " chột " là đi tong .
</s>
<s> Phải xem phong_độ , hôm ra trận phân nó phải đen , da nó phải đỏ , thần_khí nó phải linh_hoạt ...
</s>
<s> Vài năm trước dân đá gà chuyên_nghiệp hẳn chưa quên con gà ô rụt của Sự " già " người Thái_Bình .
</s>
<s> Con ô rụt này có đặc_điểm : khi lâm_trận chỉ rụt cổ lại , lì đòn và đánh trả rất ít trong mấy hồ đầu .
</s>
<s> Điều này khiến đối_phương lầm tưởng là nó sắp thua liền tăng tiền cọc theo " cửa trên " .
</s>
<s> Lúc này con ô rụt mới tung ra những đòn khốc_liệt .
</s>
<s> Loại gà này khi chưa đánh thì rất hiền_lành , khi đánh rồi thì thật đáng sợ .
</s>
<s> Chính vì_thế mà con ô rụt đã từng một thời tung_hoành khắp các sới gà miền Bắc và khiến bao tay chơi gà nhớ mãi " bài_học cay_đắng " ấy .
</s>
<s> Vì đồng_tiền , các con_bạc không từ một thủ_đoạn đê_tiện nào .
</s>
<s> Có_khi chúng lừa lúc chủ gà sơ_ý liền đánh thuốc_mê , cho gà ăn bả ... , thậm_chí còn dùng cả kim tẩm độc châm vào mình gà .
</s>
<s> Dính phải những " độc_chiêu " này , nạn_nhân gà chỉ còn cách nằm_bẹp gí trên sới hoặc về " chầu_giời " sớm .
</s>
<s> Chơi đá gà đã khiến không ít kẻ bị khuynh_gia_bại_sản và cũng có không ít người sống bám vào nó .
</s>
<s> Điều đáng ngạc_nhiên là sự tồn_tại của các sới gà cờ_bạc thứ_thiệt này ngày_một lộ_liễu , thậm_chí có sới còn tồn_tại vài năm trời với qui_mô ngày_một lớn .
</s>
<s> Người không sợ điện .
</s>
<s> Qua đò Cây_Trâm đi thêm gần 2 km vào ấp Cái_Rô trên con đường giao_thông nông_thôn ngoằn_ngoèo , cuối_cùng chúng_tôi cũng tìm được nhà anh .
</s>
<s> Đang cặm_cụi hàn điện , nhưng thấy người lạ vào nhà mà gọi đúng biệt_danh của mình nên anh Huỳnh_Văn_Hùng LBKT 41 tuổi , ở xã Định_Bình , thành_phố Cà_Mau RBKT vội ngừng công_việc lên nhà trên tiếp khách .
</s>
<s> Hút chưa xong điếu thuốc thì đám thanh_niên trong ấp cũng kéo đến vì nghe tin anh có khách , thế_nào cũng " giỡn mặt " với ... điện !
</s>
<s> Thắng độ ... 123 tháng lương !
</s>
<s> Đang lúc chuẩn_bị biểu_diễn biệt_tài dùng tay cắm vào ổ điện thì nhà anh bỗng_nhiên cúp điện .
</s>
<s> Cả đám thanh_niên đang vây quanh trước cửa nhà ồ lên cười vì cho rằng anh nói_dối nên đã dặn người_nhà đóng cầu_dao .
</s>
<s> Để minh_chứng lời_nói của mình , anh vội móc điện_thoại_di_động trong túi ra và gọi cho một người bạn ở khác ấp để tìm cho được nơi có điện .
</s>
<s> Cuối_cùng giây_phút hồi_hộp chờ_đợi của chúng_tôi và mọi người trong xã đã đến khi tìm được khu_vực không bị cúp điện .
</s>
<s> Sợ mọi người không tin , trước khi biểu_diễn anh đã lấy một cây quạt cắm vào ổ điện cho nhiều người cùng xem .
</s>
<s> Sau đó anh mở nắp cầu_dao , dùng cây_bút thử điện lia_qua_lia_lại , điện bắn " tẹt , tẹt " sáng ánh .
</s>
<s> Cuối_cùng anh đưa hai ngón tay vào ổ điện trong tiếng vỗ_tay liên_hồi của mọi người , trong đó một_số người_thân sợ anh bị điện giật chết nên đã run lên bần_bật và toát mồ_hôi hột , còn anh vẫn cười tươi như không có chuyện gì xảy ra .
</s>
<s> Thoạt_đầu mới nghe qua cứ tưởng anh là một người có thân_hình to_cao và ... không bình_thường , nhưng khi gặp mặt mới thấy anh chỉ nặng chưa đầy 50 kg và cao chừng 1,6 m .
</s>
<s> Sinh ra trong một gia_đình thuần nông ở thị_trấn Hộ_Phòng , huyện Giá_Rai LBKT Bạc_Liêu RBKT , gia_đình anh ai cũng nhút_nhát khi tiếp_xúc với điện , còn anh rất mê được làm thợ_điện .
</s>
<s> Năm 26 tuổi anh Hùng bắt_đầu hành_nghề sửa_chữa điện gia_dụng .
</s>
<s> Một năm sau đó anh xin vào làm_việc tại Xí_nghiệp Cơ_khí huyện Giá_Rai với nhiệm_vụ trông_coi nhà_máy đèn của xí_nghiệp .
</s>
<s> Trong một lần mất điện , anh đã vào sửa máy nhưng quên không ngắt cầu_dao , lúc có điện lại anh vẫn còn cầm trên tay sợi dây_điện nhưng không bị giật .
</s>
<s> Anh nhớ lại : " Bên ngoài mấy ông thợ ghim điện hàn chì ì_xèo nhưng tôi đâu có biết , tưởng chưa có điện nên tôi cứ nối dây bình_thường .
</s>
<s> Từ đó mới biết mình không bị điện giật " .
</s>
<s> Những ngày đầu biết được cơ_thể " khác người " của mình đã làm anh mất_ăn_mất_ngủ , nhiều người ác_miệng còn bảo anh là ... " người cõi trên " và đặt cho anh biệt_danh Hùng " điện " .
</s>
<s> Tuy lo_lắng vì không biết có mang trong cơ_thể loại bệnh gì không nhưng anh vẫn cố bình_tĩnh vào cơ_quan làm_việc , và mỗi lúc bạn_bè kêu anh biểu_diễn dùng tay nắm dây_điện trần đang dẫn_điện thì anh lại bảo là có " độ " mới làm .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người không tin nên đã cá_độ với anh , khi thì một chầu ăn sáng , uống cà_phê hay nhiều hơn là một độ nhậu bia_lon ... và anh đều thắng .
</s>
<s> Anh cười tươi : " Nếu không thắng thì đâu còn sống đến bây_giờ .
</s>
<s> Mà lúc ấy liều thiệt , chưa biết cơ_thể mình có không bị điện giật hoài không nhưng nghe có độ với mấy thằng bạn là " máu " liền " .
</s>
<s> Một trong những lần thắng độ mà anh Hùng cho là vẻ_vang nhất vào năm 1990 khi ông giám_đốc xí_nghiệp của anh lúc đó LBKT ông Võ_Thành_Long RBKT đã thua anh bằng cách xuất tiền_túi trả cho 123 công_nhân mỗi người một tháng lương .
</s>
<s> " Lúc đầu tôi chỉ cá với ổng bằng cách tặng tôi một tháng lương để nhậu với anh_em làm chung , nhưng có_lẽ thấy mang một mạng người ra cá_độ chỉ với mấy trăm_ngàn là quá ít hay_sao đấy mà sếp tăng_giá đến vậy LBKT ? ! RBKT " - anh nói .
</s>
<s> Vái cho ... điện giật chết !
</s>
<s> Sau nhiều năm " giỡn mặt " với điện , thấy cơ_thể vẫn khỏe_mạnh nên anh quyết_định lấy vợ .
</s>
<s> Tuy_nhiên , lo_sợ chị Quách_Hồng_Lê LBKT vợ anh RBKT bị anh ... truyền điện nên anh dặn bạn_bè không cho vợ biết chuyện và giấu luôn biệt_danh Hùng " điện " của mình .
</s>
<s> Tuy_nhiên , cây kim trong bọc cũng có ngày lòi ra .
</s>
<s> Anh kể : " Cưới vợ gần một tháng , hôm đó khi đi đám giỗ ngang qua nhà anh Năm_Truyền LBKT Trần_Văn_Truyền RBKT ở ấp Cây_Trâm , không biết ảnh quên hay sao mà hỏi tôi : " Ê , khỏe không Hùng " điện " ? " " .
</s>
<s> Còn chị khi biết được anh Hùng hay thường_xuyên cá_độ với bạn_bè bằng cách lấy ngón tay làm " cầu_chì " thì chị đã khóc ròng và cấm anh nếu còn cá_độ sẽ bỏ về bên nhà nhưng cũng không ngăn được anh .
</s>
<s> " Vì quá thương tôi nên bả mới làm vậy chứ tôi biết đâu có chuyện gì xảy ra .
</s>
<s> Mấy lần sau khi thấy tôi nắm dây_điện bả chỉ ... vái cho tôi bị điện giật chết " - vừa nói anh vừa nhìn vợ tỏ_vẻ đắc_ý .
</s>
<s> Anh Năm_Truyền chen lời : " Hôm trước nghe chuyện này ông Hai_Bình bực_mình đòi cá 1.000 giạ lúa với nó , nhưng nghe ai cũng nói thằng Hùng không sợ điện giật nên ổng vội ... rút_lui " .
</s>
<s> Cũng theo anh Hùng , khi xem tivi về chuyện ông Nguyễn_Thành_Vinh ở Tiền_Giang không bị điện giật , anh đã dùng sợi dây_nóng cắm vào ly nước và để tay vào nhưng cũng không thấy giật nên anh đã cầm ly nước uống bình_thường như ông Vinh .
</s>
<s> Anh cười : " Chuyện đó dễ_ợt , tôi làm hoài " .
</s>
<s> Trước khi tiễn khách anh Hùng còn bật_mí : " Đến năm 45 tuổi tôi sẽ biểu_diễn hơn ông Vinh nhiều thứ nữa cho các anh xem , còn bây_giờ thì đang ... luyện công .
</s>
<s> Thằng Tính bạn tôi ở Điện_lực Tắc_Vân nhiều lúc đi sửa điện cho bà_con thấy không kịp nên kêu tôi giúp và vụ nào tôi cũng nối dây_điện " sống " , chưa bao_giờ tôi biết cúp cầu_dao là gì " .
</s>
<s> Đứng vững trên đôi chân tật_nguyền .
</s>
<s> Cố_gắng lắm chị mới sắp_xếp được cho tôi một buổi gặp ngắn_ngủi , vì thời_gian làm_việc của chị hầu_như chật kín .
</s>
<s> Và chị đã kể tôi nghe về mình .
</s>
<s> Tuổi_thơ của chị là chiến_tranh , bom_đạn , chết_chóc và hình_ảnh người mẹ còng lưng nhặt từng hạt thóc để nuôi bốn đứa con ăn_học .
</s>
<s> Là hình_ảnh của những ngày chị cố lê đôi chân tật_nguyền để đến trường trên quãng đường đất_đỏ mịt_mù .
</s>
<s> Chị là Võ_Thị_Hoàng_Yến LBKT 38 tuổi RBKT sinh ra và lớn lên ở một làng quê xa thuộc xã Hiệp_Phước , huyện Nhơn_Trạch LBKT Đồng_Nai RBKT .
</s>
<s> Từ cú sốc đầu đời .
</s>
<s> Nghĩ đến thân_phận của mình chị cũng buồn , cũng tủi .
</s>
<s> Chị nói : " Nhiều đứa bé tật_nguyền khác khi bị trêu_chọc thì hay mắc_cỡ nên bỏ học , nhưng không hiểu sao lúc đó mình lại tự_tin ghê_gớm , đã không bị mặc_cảm mà_còn tâm_niệm rằng phải học thật giỏi .
</s>
<s> Càng bị coi_thường càng phải học giỏi " .
</s>
<s> Quyết_tâm học_tập của chị lúc đó như một sự phản_kháng , một cách tự_vệ cho riêng mình .
</s>
<s> Không chỉ học giỏi , chị còn tham_gia công_tác Đoàn - Hội ở trường .
</s>
<s> Lên cấp III , cô Út học giỏi lại tiếp_tục tham_gia công_tác Đoàn và làm bí_thư Đoàn trường ...
</s>
<s> Chị nói dù là con nhà nghèo , dù là đứa trẻ tật_nguyền nhưng lúc_nào chị cũng là một người tự_tin vào năng_lực của mình .
</s>
<s> Nhờ thế suốt những năm cắp sách đến trường , dù gặp không ít những khó_khăn nhưng chị đều vượt qua .
</s>
<s> Thế nhưng , ngay lần đầu_tiên bước ra đời , vác đơn đi xin việc_làm sau khi tốt_nghiệp ĐH Kinh_tế năm 1990 , chị đã bị một cú sốc kinh_khủng đầu đời .
</s>
<s> Đến hôm_nay , khi nghĩ_lại chị cũng không biết rằng cú sốc đó là họa hay may .
</s>
<s> Gõ_cửa nơi nào chị cũng nhận được những cái lắc_đầu đầy thương_hại , có những nơi sau khi kiểm_tra năng_lực của chị người_ta đã đồng_ý nhận ngay , nhưng rồi sau đó lại từ_chối thẳng_thừng khi phát_hiện chị là người khuyết_tật LBKT NKT RBKT .
</s>
<s> Cả một thời_gian dài dù cố_gắng nhưng chị không xin được việc_làm ở đâu : " Người_ta không nói ra nhưng mình thừa biết mình không được nhận vào làm_việc không phải là vì năng_lực kém , mà chỉ vì là NKT " - chị Yến bùi_ngùi nhớ lại .
</s>
<s> Lặng_thinh hồi lâu , chị lại tiếp : " Lúc đó mình thấy đau lắm , lo_lắng cho mình và cho cả những NKT " .
</s>
<s> Bạn_bè cùng trường ai cũng tỏ ra ái_ngại cho tình_cảnh của chị .
</s>
<s> Xin việc_làm không được , chị nghĩ phải đi học thêm ngoại_ngữ với ý_nghĩ sau_này có cơ_hội thì xin dạy kèm , tự kiếm sống .
</s>
<s> Đồng_thời với vốn ngoại_ngữ học được , chị sẽ tìm đọc thêm những tài_liệu của nước_ngoài liên_quan đến NKT , biết_đâu từ đó có_thể tìm được những cơ_hội không chỉ cho riêng mình mà_còn cho những NKT khác cùng cảnh_ngộ .
</s>
<s> Vậy là năm 1993 , lần đầu_tiên chị làm_quen với tiếng Anh .
</s>
<s> Chị nói : " Hồi trước ở quê mình người_ta chưa dạy ngoại_ngữ , vào ĐH mình mới được học tiếng Nga , còn tiếng Anh thì hoàn_toàn xa_lạ " .
</s>
<s> Học được một năm thì việc học của chị phải gián_đoạn vì đôi chân yếu dần nên phải mổ .
</s>
<s> Hơn một năm trời chị phải nằm ở nhà dưỡng_thương .
</s>
<s> Trong khoảng thời_gian đó chị cố_công tự học tiếng Anh .
</s>
<s> Nói về thành_tích này , chị cười rạng_rỡ : " Thật_ra mình chẳng tài_giỏi gì đâu , chẳng_qua là nhờ mình có khiếu học ngoại_ngữ thôi , với_lại ở nhà mình ai cũng học giỏi hết , chỉ có mình là học ẹ nhất " .
</s>
<s> Chị theo học ngành phát_triển con_người tại ĐH Kansas LBKT Mỹ RBKT .
</s>
<s> Để theo kịp những SV khác buộc những SV VN như chị phải nỗ_lực vượt_bậc .
</s>
<s> Không_những thế chị còn là người trợ_giảng cho một giáo_sư người Mỹ tên Glen_White .
</s>
<s> Hiện_nay công_trình nghiên_cứu của chị đã được in thành sách và được xem như một loại giáo_trình cho SV học_tập tại ĐH Kansas .
</s>
<s> Từ_chối ở lại nước Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Được gặp_gỡ trao_đổi với thượng_nghị_sĩ Tom_Harkins - người đã có những đóng_góp rất nhiều cho các chương_trình và chính_sách dành cho NKT Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Chị còn được mời vào Nhà_Trắng , gặp tiến_sĩ Troy_Justesen - một NKT đang là cố_vấn cho tổng_thống Mỹ về các chính_sách liên_quan đến NKT .
</s>
<s> Rồi cùng nhóm của mình , chị được mời đến Bộ Giáo_dục Mỹ để nói_chuyện với những người phụ_trách các chương_trình nghiên_cứu về khuyết_tật và phục_hồi chức_năng LBKT NIDRR RBKT .
</s>
<s> Một lần nọ , biết chị một_mực đòi quay về quê_hương , giáo_sư Glen_White liền bày_tỏ ý_định xin nhận chị làm con_nuôi và giúp chị ở lại Mỹ .
</s>
<s> Không_những thế , ông hứa sẽ rước cả người mẹ thân_yêu của chị sang Mỹ định_cư , nhưng chị một_mực từ_chối .
</s>
<s> Chị bộc_bạch : " Những năm xa quê_hương , mình mới thấm_thía hết hai tiếng Việt_Nam thiêng_liêng và thân_thiết đến ngần nào " .
</s>
<s> Trở về , chị còn muốn được đóng_góp chút_ít gì đó cho quê_hương VN .
</s>
<s> Chia_tay tôi , chị lại tất_tả lao vào hàng đống tài_liệu , hồ_sơ được mang về từ nước_ngoài để soạn những giáo_trình giảng_dạy phù_hợp với điều_kiện giáo_dục ở VN .
</s>
<s> Được biết , Trường ĐH Đà_Lạt đã mời chị tham_gia giảng_dạy và ngày 6 - 12 - 2004 là lần đầu_tiên chị mang kiến_thức học được của mình truyền_đạt đến các SV VN .
</s>
<s> Nhúm ruột Việt trên đất Isan ... LBKT kỳ 4 RBKT : Gặp một tỉ_phú ... nuôi heo !
</s>
<s> Trên đường từ Sakon_Nakhon về Nakhon_Phanom , bên phải đường , phía ngoại_ô Nakhon có một tòa biệt_thự to đẹp nằm trên khoảng đất rộng_lớn chừng vài hecta , rất ấn_tượng .
</s>
<s> Anh Hải , người đưa chúng_tôi đi trong những ngày ở Thái_Lan , bảo : " Biệt_thự này của một Việt_kiều làm nghề nuôi heo đấy ! " .
</s>
<s> Chúng_tôi tròn mắt ngạc_nhiên .
</s>
<s> Hôm sau , anh Hanh - một học_viên của lớp sinh_viên đi học tiếng Thái ở Nakhon , đồng_thời cũng là đại_diện của Công_ty Du_lịch Quảng_Trị tại vùng đông bắc Thái - dẫn chúng_tôi vào thăm cơ_ngơi của ông chủ trang_trại chăn_nuôi heo .
</s>
<s> Anh tên là Xốm , Phan_Văn_Xốm .
</s>
<s> Giới kinh_doanh trong nghề chăn_nuôi ở Thái hầu_như đều biết đến anh .
</s>
<s> Lập_nghiệp trên đất hoang ...
</s>
<s> Tôi thắc_mắc : " Sao tên tiếng Việt của anh nghe như tên ... Thái ? " .
</s>
<s> Anh Xốm cười : " Bố tôi ngày_xưa đặt tên cho con để gọi tiếng Thái cũng dễ mà đọc tiếng Việt cũng được .
</s>
<s> Tôi họ Phan , nhưng họ để nhập_tịch Thái là Buntaphan - nghĩa_là phúc_đức của họ Phan ! ...
</s>
<s> Phan_Văn_Xốm hay Buntaphan_Xômthat cũng là thế ... " .
</s>
<s> Giọng nói anh còn nặng âm_sắc vùng Ba_Đồn , Quảng_Trạch LBKT Quảng_Bình RBKT dù gia_đình anh sang đây từ những năm 1930 .
</s>
<s> Trước khi đưa chúng_tôi đi thăm hệ_thống chuồng_trại tọa_lạc trên khu đất rộng 60 ha , anh Xốm bảo : " Tôi cũng không ngờ cái vùng_đất đông bắc này lại trở_thành nơi mình gầy_dựng cơ_nghiệp được như thế này " .
</s>
<s> Năm 19 tuổi gia_đình cho đi học sửa_chữa điện_tử ở Bangkok , ra làm nghề sửa tivi đen_trắng và các loại máy_móc .
</s>
<s> Năm 1977 anh lấy vợ , vợ anh người gốc Hà_Tĩnh , gia_đình qua đây cũng đã lâu , tên chị là Nguyễn_Thị_Tình , một phụ_nữ trẻ đẹp .
</s>
<s> Rồi năm 1978 , hai vợ_chồng từ Bangkok về thăm người bà_con bên vợ ở vùng Nakhon này , nhìn đàn gà con ở nhà người chú vợ , anh ... mê_mẩn và bàn với vợ hay về đây nuôi gà !
</s>
<s> Chị Tình kể lại khi nghe chồng nói vậy chị ngạc_nhiên vô_cùng .
</s>
<s> Đang yên_ấm ở Bangkok , cửa_tiệm đàng_hoàng , nay lại về chốn xa_xôi hẻo_lánh thế này nuôi gà LBKT ! RBKT ...
</s>
<s> Nhưng rồi chị cũng đồng_ý vì thấy chồng quá mê chăn_nuôi .
</s>
<s> Khởi_nghiệp của vợ_chồng anh là một chuồng gà_công_nghiệp qui_mô 300 con , rồi tăng dần lên 6_._0000 con .
</s>
<s> Bây_giờ đi giữa một hệ_thống chuồng_trại trên diện_tích 60 ha được thiết_kế hiện_đại và đẹp như ... công_viên , không ai ngờ 20 năm qua anh Xốm đã trải những truân_chuyên như thế_nào để trụ lại được đến giờ .
</s>
<s> " Năm 1983 tôi bắt_đầu chuyển sang nuôi heo với khởi_nghiệp 12 heo nái bình_thường và một heo đực - anh Xốm kể lại - đến năm 1988 nâng lên thành 200 heo nái trong một trại khoảng 8 ha .
</s>
<s> Rồi cứ thế vừa làm_ăn vừa tích_lũy cơ_sở vật_chất , trang_trại cũ quá chật_chội thì tôi tiến ra ngoại_ô xây_dựng hệ_thống chuồng_trại để nuôi theo công_nghệ hiện_đại nhất " .
</s>
<s> Số_lượng heo nái của trang_trại anh đã đạt 4_._000 con .
</s>
<s> Số heo con sau khi cai_sữa được chuyển_giao cho các hộ dân nhận hợp_đồng nuôi gia_công tại gia_đình .
</s>
<s> Công_ty có 40 hộ dân nuôi vệ_tinh với mỗi hộ khoảng 700 con .
</s>
<s> Lượng heo thịt này tôi xuất mỗi đợt hơn 20_._000 con , khoảng ba tháng rưỡi thì xuất chuồng LBKT đạt trọng_lượng trên 100 kg / con RBKT " .
</s>
<s> Hiện mỗi ngày Công_ty Buntaphan xuất bán hơn 200 heo thịt LBKT hơn 20 tấn RBKT .
</s>
<s> Công_ty cung_cấp heo giống , thức_ăn , qui_trình nuôi , thú_y ... và chỉ trả công nuôi cho họ .
</s>
<s> Để có nguồn giống tốt , đích_thân anh sang tận Đan_Mạch , Ireland ... mua heo giống với giá 5_._000 - 6_._000 USD / con .
</s>
<s> Mỗi đợt mua 20 - 30 con , có hồ_sơ từng con hẳn_hoi .
</s>
<s> Có được thành_công ấy , anh Xốm nói là nhờ ở Thái_Lan nhà_nước giúp_đỡ rất nhiều cho ngành nông_nghiệp , từ thuế , giá đất_đai đến chuyển_giao công_nghệ .
</s>
<s> Chẳng_hạn như công_nghệ nuôi heo của công_ty được sự giúp_đỡ rất nhiều từ phía nhà_nước nên giá rất rẻ .
</s>
<s> Chỉ muốn khẳng_định mình là người Việt ...
</s>
<s> Hôm chúng_tôi đến , gặp đoàn công_nhân bên Hà_Tĩnh đang sang tiếp_thu công_nghệ chăn_nuôi từ trang_trại của anh Xốm .
</s>
<s> Hiện_nay Hà_Tĩnh cũng đang xây_dựng mô_hình chăn_nuôi như thế này và đề_nghị anh Xốm chuyển_giao công_nghệ cho bà_con quê ... vợ !
</s>
<s> Lái_xe đưa chúng_tôi đi một vòng tham_quan trang_trại , 16 dãy chuồng có cả hệ_thống điều_hòa_nhiệt_độ , theo_dõi độ_ẩm , hệ_thống vận_hành thức_ăn tự_động cho đến máy_phát_điện chạy bằng khí biogas LBKT gas được sản_xuất từ nguồn phân heo của trang_trại RBKT đảm_bảo vệ_sinh môi_trường , tất_cả đều liên_hoàn và khép_kín .
</s>
<s> Vây quanh trang_trại là những thảm cỏ xanh ngút , bao_bọc ngoài là một vành_đai với hơn 8 ha trồng bưởi mà theo anh Xốm đây là giống bưởi đặc_biệt của Thái , tuyệt ngon và năng_suất rất cao .
</s>
<s> Vui chuyện anh Xốm bảo : " Cách đây tám năm tôi đã trải qua những ngày kinh_hoàng .
</s>
<s> Hai năm 1996 - 1997 , công_cuộc kinh_doanh rơi vào điểm tối_đen nhất , không thấy tương_lai .
</s>
<s> Hồi đó mỗi tháng công_ty lỗ khoảng 40_._000 USD .
</s>
<s> Khi đó tìm đến cái chết thật là dễ_dàng , không đáng sợ nữa , nhưng tôi không chịu được cảm_giác sống nhục_nhã , thất_bại .
</s>
<s> Nhiều ngày có_khi tính_chuyện cùng_quẫn , nhưng rồi gượng dậy mà tin rằng mình phải vượt qua .
</s>
<s> Năm_ngoái , thời_điểm bị cúm_gà , người dân chuyển sang ăn thịt heo , bình_quân mỗi tháng công_ty lãi hơn 150_._000 USD .
</s>
<s> Đưa chúng_tôi đi thăm ngôi biệt_thự , anh bảo : " Năm trước thấy mình sắp vỡ_nợ , năm sau tự_nhiên trả xong nợ rồi xây ngôi nhà " hơi bị to " , nhiều người nghi tôi buôn ... ma_túy !
</s>
<s> Và tôi được chính_quyền sở_tại mời tham_gia hội_đồng an_ninh của tỉnh Nakhon_Phanom này .
</s>
<s> Hôm xong nhà , anh_em trong hội_đồng có tổ_chức một cuộc họp tại đây , dân trong vùng thấy tự_nhiên nhiều xe an_ninh Thái đậu trong khu nhà tôi ai cũng nghĩ là cảnh_sát đến bắt ... " .
</s>
<s> Kể đến đây anh Xốm cười sảng_khoái .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người Việt xa xứ vẫn nhắc đến những người đồng_hương của mình thành_đạt trong các lĩnh_vực nơi đất_khách_quê_người như một niềm tự_hào rất riêng .
</s>
<s> Và sự thành_đạt ấy không chỉ riêng mình ai hưởng .
</s>
<s> Sự nhiệt_tình của anh Xốm để chuyển_giao công_nghệ chăn_nuôi hiện_đại cho Hà_Tĩnh là một minh_chứng cụ_thể .
</s>
<s> Hơn thế , tôi còn được biết anh vẫn lặng_lẽ góp_phần phụng_dưỡng nhiều bà mẹ ở VN , nhưng điều ấy anh không bao_giờ nói ...
</s>
<s> Xóm " đập bao " .
</s>
<s> Giải_quyết công_ăn_việc_làm cho hơn 300 hộ gia_đình nhưng nghề này lại gây ô_nhiễm môi_trường , sinh bệnh_tật và kéo_theo tình_trạng thất_học của nhiều trẻ_em .
</s>
<s> Chính_quyền địa_phương hiện cũng chưa tìm ra hướng giải_quyết ...
</s>
<s> Già , trẻ đều làm bao .
</s>
<s> Hình_ảnh đầu_tiên đập vào mắt tôi khi đi dọc theo các tuyến đường Lương_Văn_Can , Lưu_Hữu_Phước , Bình_Đông là những đống vỏ bao xi-măng cao_ngất chất đầy mỗi nhà .
</s>
<s> Trong các con hẻm dài ngoằn_ngoèo , gần_như nhà nào cũng làm nghề này .
</s>
<s> Được biết từ lâu_nay , người dân vùng này mua vỏ bao xi-măng về đập sạch , rồi cắt dán thành nhiều loại bao lớn_nhỏ bỏ_mối cho các quầy hàng tạp_hóa ở Chợ_Lớn để đựng đường , đậu , ớt ...
</s>
<s> Ban_đầu chỉ có vài hộ làm bao .
</s>
<s> Cho đến nay , riêng phường 15 , quận 8 đã có khoảng trên 300 hộ theo nghề .
</s>
<s> Nghề làm bao được chia làm nhiều công_đoạn : rút chỉ , cắt dán , tiền công khoảng 15_._000 - 20_._000 đồng / ngày .
</s>
<s> Khâu đập bao mất_sức và phải sống chung với bụi nên thu_nhập cao hơn , khoảng 25_._000 đồng / ngày .
</s>
<s> Người khỏe , trai_tráng , người già , trẻ_em , phụ_nữ đều có_thể tham_gia .
</s>
<s> Cụ bà Phan_Thị_Ba , năm nay đã tám mươi tuổi vẫn ngồi dán bao , kể : " Hồi trẻ làm được nhiều chứ giờ thì cao lắm một ngày cũng chỉ được 8_._000 đồng , dẫu ít nhưng dồn chung tiền công với bốn đứa con cũng đủ sống qua_ngày " .
</s>
<s> Sống chung với ... bụi .
</s>
<s> Đường Lưu_Hữu_Phước có một con hẻm chỉ vừa đủ một người lách đi giữa những căn nhà san_sát nhau .
</s>
<s> Cuối con hẻm là một khoảnh đất trống , người dân ở đây gọi là khu Gò_Mả .
</s>
<s> Trong khoảnh đất khoảng 100 m2 che mưa che nắng bằng nhiều tấm bạt chắp_vá ấy bụi mù_mịt .
</s>
<s> Căng mắt tôi cũng chỉ nhìn thấy được những người đứng gần ngay trước mặt đang huơ tay lên xuống để đập bao , người đứng xa khoảng 15 bước chân thì chỉ thấy loáng_thoáng bóng đen .
</s>
<s> Không_gian ở đây đặc quánh những làn bụi màu xám mù_mịt .
</s>
<s> Ông Trương_Hồng_Sơn , Chủ_tịch UBND phường 15 , quận 8 : Chưa tìm được cách giải_quyết .
</s>
<s> Nghề làm bao là nghề truyền_thống có từ lâu , tạo công_ăn_việc_làm cho người dân nhưng lại gây ô_nhiễm môi_trường rất nặng .
</s>
<s> Trước đây chúng_tôi có một giải_pháp là yêu_cầu người đập bao đến những vùng_đất trống như rạch Làu để làm .
</s>
<s> Khi rạch Làu quy_hoạch thành khu chung_cư , không còn chỗ , họ đành đưa ra đường_phố đập vào ban_đêm .
</s>
<s> Sáng ra , đường_phố trắng_bóc bởi vôi , xi-măng ...
</s>
<s> Chúng_tôi dự_tính là sẽ yêu_cầu nhà nào đập bao phải xây bít_bùng lại , anh muốn đập thì vào trong đó mà đập .
</s>
<s> Nói thì nói vậy nhưng chúng_tôi cũng chưa tìm được cách nào để giải_quyết .
</s>
<s> Nếu mình dẹp nghề này thì khác_nào đổ nồi cơm của dân_nghèo ; kêu người_ta chuyển nghề thì không biết nghề gì để chuyển , mà để vậy thì không được vì ô_nhiễm môi_trường quá .
</s>
<s> Quẹt lớp mồ_hôi dính đầy bụi xi-măng trên trán , khạc nhổ nước_miếng liên_hồi , bà Nhiều nói với tôi : " Ở đây ai cũng bị viêm mũi , viêm họng cả ... " .
</s>
<s> Mọi người ở đây xem chuyện sống chung với bụi là bình_thường .
</s>
<s> Chị Linh , nhà gần đó , chỉ trông con nhưng mũi của chị cũng bị phủ trắng bởi bụi .
</s>
<s> Út_Em đập khoảng năm mươi bao là dừng tay , cầm miếng dưa_hấu ăn ngon_lành giữa làn bụi mù_mịt .
</s>
<s> Chỉ có vài người_lớn là đeo khẩu_trang , trẻ_em và những người còn lại thì vô_tư hả miệng cười nói .
</s>
<s> Xuyên giải_thích : " Đeo cũng như_không , bụi bay một_chút là lấp đầy khẩu_trang hà ! " .
</s>
<s> Có_lẽ vì_vậy mà Xuyên đang bị viêm họng nặng .
</s>
<s> Cách khu Gò_Mả mấy bước là nhà ông Võ_Thanh_Sơn , gia_đình đã có thâm_niên trên mười năm đập bao tại đây .
</s>
<s> Hiện ông đang bị xuất_huyết não , nằm bất_động một chỗ .
</s>
<s> Bé Luận , cháu ngoại ông , ba tuổi , cũng chỉ ngồi một chỗ vì bị mù .
</s>
<s> Mẹ em kể : " Lúc mới sinh ra , mắt con tôi bị đổ ghèn suốt .
</s>
<s> Đến tháng thứ sáu mới biết nó không thấy đường .
</s>
<s> Đi khám thì bác_sĩ bảo vô_phương cứu_chữa " .
</s>
<s> Anh của Luận là An , đang đập bao ở một căn chòi khác , thường_xuyên bị đau rát nơi bộ_phận sinh_dục .
</s>
<s> Tôi không biết đôi mắt của Luận , bộ_phận sinh_dục của An và tình_trạng ô_nhiễm môi_trường ở đây có liên_quan gì với nhau hay không , tôi chỉ dám chắc rằng tôi chưa thấy nơi nào bụi bay đặc quánh như nơi đây .
</s>
<s> Con chữ xa tầm tay .
</s>
<s> Các gia_đình đập bao hầu_hết đều nghèo .
</s>
<s> Trừ chi_phí thuê đất đập LBKT mỗi tháng khoảng 100_._000 đồng RBKT và tiền thuê nhà , những người ở khu Gò_Mả chỉ còn lo đủ cho cái ăn .
</s>
<s> Đó là chưa kể đến những ngày trời mưa , những tháng sau Tết , cả xóm phải ngồi_không .
</s>
<s> Khoảng thời_gian ấy họ lo nhất trong năm .
</s>
<s> Cái nghèo là một trong những nguyên_nhân khiến thế_hệ này đến thế_hệ khác mù_chữ .
</s>
<s> Hai vợ_chồng và sáu đứa con ông Mười đều không biết chữ .
</s>
<s> Hai người con lớn đã đi lấy chồng và cũng theo nghề đập bao .
</s>
<s> Bốn đứa còn lại tuổi từ 11 đến 20 , đến lớp_học tình_thương được vài tuần rồi nghỉ vì không đủ sức ngồi học ban_đêm .
</s>
<s> Ông Mười nói : " Trẻ ở đây bảy tuổi là cho đi rút chỉ , chín tuổi là bắt_đầu đập bao , không biết bao_giờ mới bỏ đuợc cái cây đập đây ... " .
</s>
<s> Ông Mười quê ở Trà_Vinh , bị cụt một chân trong thời chiến_tranh .
</s>
<s> Không làm_ruộng được , ông mang vợ_con lên thành_phố sống bằng nghề thợ_hồ .
</s>
<s> Cái chân khập_khiễng của ông khiến thu_nhập không đủ ăn nên cả gia_đình chuyển sang nghề đập bao từ mấy chực năm nay .
</s>
<s> Đen , Đỏ chưa hề được đến trường ; Quốc , An , Út_Em ... và nhiều em nữa học chưa hết bậc tiểu_học đã phải bỏ ngang , ở nhà đập bao kiếm tiền phụ gia_đình .
</s>
<s> Cu Đen nói : " Em muốn đi học lắm nhưng học phổ_thông ban_ngày thì không kiếm tiền giúp mẹ được , còn học lớp tình_thương ban_đêm thì đến lớp là mắt cứ díp lại vì mệt quá " .
</s>
<s> Nhìn lũ trẻ ngụp_lặn giữa đống bụi xám_xịt , tôi chợt lo cho tương_lai của các em khi cứ phải chung_sống bụi và tình_trạng thất_học .
</s>
<s> Nhúm ruột Việt trên đất Isan ... LBKT kỳ 5 RBKT : Quốc_tịch và giấc mơ cố_hương ...
</s>
<s> Một buổi tối ở Khonkaen , đang ngồi ăn tối cùng mấy anh_em Việt_kiều ở đấy bỗng chuông điện_thoại_di_động của anh Hải ngồi trong bàn réo vang , đang nghe , gương_mặt anh chợt rạng_rỡ hẳn lên .
</s>
<s> Anh thông_báo : " Bà_con dưới Mukdahan vừa gọi lên bảo rằng đợt này Muk có thêm hơn 100 người được nhập_tịch , chưa biết tất_cả tỉnh trong vùng có bao_nhiêu người được cấp ... " .
</s>
<s> Anh Chiến - phụ_trách công_tác Việt_kiều ở tòa Tổng_lãnh_sự Khonkaen - gọi về hỏi đại_sứ_quán ở Bangkok , rồi gọi sang Nakhon_Phanom , người gọi lên UdonThani , người gọi về Sakon_Nakhon .
</s>
<s> Không_khí chợt ồn_ào hẳn lên !
</s>
<s> Giấc mơ đời người ...
</s>
<s> Hỏi ra mới hay rất nhiều bà_con người Việt suốt một đời người sống trên đất Thái thế nhưng vẫn chưa được nhập quốc_tịch Thái .
</s>
<s> Không được nhập quốc_tịch nghĩa_là đối_mặt với cả một núi khó_khăn trong cuộc_sống .
</s>
<s> Không được đứng_tên mua_bán chuyển_nhượng đất_đai nhà_cửa , không có môn_bài kinh_doanh xuất_nhập_khẩu , và đáng lo nhất vẫn là chuyện con_cái không được vào đại_học hoặc nếu vào đại_học phải chịu một khoản học_phí như người nước_ngoài LBKT cao gấp năm lần so với người Thái RBKT và rất khó tìm được việc_làm tại các công_sở .
</s>
<s> Bác Hoàng_Minh_Tâm cho biết ngày trước , những năm chưa được thông_thoáng trong quan_hệ hai nước , muốn cho con_em mình thuận_lợi trong tương_lai , khi sinh con nhiều nhà phải gửi con mình cho những bà_con đã được nhập quốc_tịch , mỗi người nhận giúp một đứa , vậy mới sinh ra chuyện trong một gia_đình mà mấy anh_em ruột mỗi người phải mang một họ khác nhau .
</s>
<s> " Tôi được biết rằng trong thời_gian Bác_Hồ của chúng_ta sống ở đây đã dạy cho người Thái cách_thức đánh_cá nước_ngọt hữu_hiệu , nhắc_nhở những người Thái gốc Việt tại đây phải luôn nhớ đến công_ơn của mảnh đất mà ta đang sống , đồng_thời luôn dạy rằng tình_cảm của hai dân_tộc Thái_Lan - VN được gắn_bó bởi con sông Mekong .
</s>
<s> Sự đóng_góp và triết_lý của Bác_Hồ đã giúp mối quan_hệ hai nước Thái_Lan - VN ngày_càng phát_triển hơn " .
</s>
<s> LBKT Trích diễn_văn tại lễ khánh_thành làng hữu_nghị Việt - Thái ở bản Nachock của Thủ_tướng Thái_Lan Thaksin_Shinawatra RBKT .
</s>
<s> _Làm_sao nói hết được niềm ngóng_vọng khắc_khoải ấy ?
</s>
<s> Có một người Thái lại hiểu rõ tâm_nguyện , nỗi_lòng của những Việt_kiều , bà là tiến_sĩ Thăndzathip_Siphanar , công_tác tại Viện Giáo_dục châu Á thuộc Đại_học Chulalongkorn LBKT Bangkok RBKT .
</s>
<s> Bài báo viết : " Người VN tản_cư đều trông_ngóng mỏi_mòn với chính_phủ về những lá đơn của họ .
</s>
<s> Họ đệ đơn quá lâu , chính_phủ xem_xét quá chậm_trễ nên có người khi nhận được giấy_phép thì đã quá già_yếu , có người lâm trọng_bệnh sắp qua_đời và cũng có người đã chết .
</s>
<s> Việc được cấp phép trong hoàn_cảnh như vậy chỉ làm những người đang sống và con_cháu thêm đau_khổ .
</s>
<s> Chính vì_thế mà nhiều trường_hợp có giấy_phép nhưng không ai đến nhận .
</s>
<s> Điều này cũng nói lên sự xét_duyệt của cấp trên đã quá lâu đến thế_nào " .
</s>
<s> Tiến_sĩ Thăndzathip_Siphanar cũng nhấn_mạnh đến tiềm_năng của cộng_đồng người Việt ở đông bắc Thái : " Nếu chính_phủ nhập quốc_tịch Thái cho những người Việt này , không chỉ họ được lợi mà ngược_lại chính_phủ cũng sẽ nhận được từ họ những cống_hiến to_lớn cho đất_nước Thái_Lan bởi họ là những người có năng_lực .
</s>
<s> Phải thừa_nhận người Việt ở đây là những người cần_cù siêng_năng , chịu_khó và giàu lòng nhẫn_nại ...
</s>
<s> Ở vùng đông bắc Thái có nhiều mảnh đất khô_cằn đã được họ khai_phá và làm cho vùng_đất ấy trở_nên trù_phú xanh_tươi .
</s>
<s> Nếu không tin cứ thử đến xem trang_trại trồng cam ở UdonThani LBKT trang_trại này của anh Nguyễn_Văn_Tấn , một Việt_kiều ở Udon - NV RBKT rộng cả ngàn hecta .
</s>
<s> Không chỉ là nơi trồng_trọt mà đây còn là nơi nghiên_cứu , thực_tập cho các nhà_nông và không ít người là kỹ_sư nông_nghiệp " .
</s>
<s> Nhiều người ở Thái không hiểu hết ý_nghĩa và giá_trị của việc nhập quốc_tịch quan_trọng đến mức nào đối_với các Việt_kiều , nhất_là những người có độ tuổi 60 - 70 .
</s>
<s> Nó quan_trọng ở chỗ : khi có được quốc_tịch thì người Việt ở Thái mới có quyền làm hộ_chiếu để được về thăm Tổ_quốc , quê_hương , thăm ông_bà tổ_tiên .
</s>
<s> Về thăm cố_hương chính là giấc mơ một đời người của rất nhiều người Việt ở miền đông bắc Thái_Lan !
</s>
<s> Người Việt sinh_sống ở 17 / 19 tỉnh vùng này , có thời_điểm lên đến 10 vạn người LBKT những năm 1946 - 1953 RBKT .
</s>
<s> Từ năm 1960 - 1964 đã có nhiều chuyến hồi_hương của Việt_kiều với cả vạn người .
</s>
<s> Hiện_nay cộng_đồng người Việt tại đông bắc Thái có khoảng 5 vạn người , tập_trung nhiều nhất ở các tỉnh Nakhon_Phanom , Mukdahan , Khonkaen , Noong_Khai , SakonNakhon , Udonthani , Phichit , Kalaxin ...
</s>
<s> Tỉnh đông nhất có đến 6_._000 - 7_._000 người , tỉnh ít cũng 1_._000 người .
</s>
<s> Khác với các cộng_đồng người Hoa , người Lào ... , Việt_kiều ở đây , ngoài nghề nông thường là chủ các tiệm cơ_khí , điện_máy ... bởi tay_nghề cao .
</s>
<s> Hôm dự đám_tang một Việt_kiều ở Mukdahan , thật bất_ngờ khi chúng_tôi thấy một chiếc xe pick-up với hệ_thống loa trên nóc xe chạy đến đậu trước cổng chùa Diệu_Giác .
</s>
<s> Một người phụ_nữ dáng hoạt_bát vào gặp mấy anh_em ở Hội Việt_kiều Muk , sau đấy anh Vinh và anh Hải nói cho tôi biết người phụ_nữ ấy là bà Vosabuly_Sausirileun , người của Đảng XatThai , đang là ứng_viên đại_biểu Quốc_hội Thái_Lan nhiệm_kỳ tới .
</s>
<s> Bà biết hôm_nay ở đây tập_trung đông người Việt nên tranh_thủ đến vận_động tranh_cử .
</s>
<s> Vậy_là nhân buổi lễ tang của người Việt , bà Vosabuly đã có một buổi vận_động cử_tri thật ấn_tượng mà theo anh Hải dịch lại cho chúng_tôi nghe mục_tiêu , chương_trình mà bà đưa ra vẫn là sẽ vận_động việc cấp quốc_tịch cho Việt_kiều .
</s>
<s> Bây_giờ quốc_tịch đang là vấn_đề rất dễ chiếm cảm_tình LBKT và lá phiếu RBKT của cộng_đồng Việt_kiều ở đây .
</s>
<s> Hôm khánh_thành làng Hữu_nghị Việt - Thái ở bản Nachock , Thủ_tướng Thái_Lan , ngài Thaksin_Shinawatra , cũng đã nhấn_mạnh trong bài diễn_văn rằng : " Tôi đã được nghe ngài Thủ_tướng Phan_Văn_Khải nói rằng nhiều người Thái gốc Việt lớn_tuổi sinh_sống tại đây qua nhiều thế_hệ , đã có con_cháu nhưng vẫn chưa có giấy_tờ hợp_pháp , tôi hứa sẽ chỉ_thị và thúc_đẩy Bộ Nội_vụ và chính_quyền địa_phương sớm cấp giấy_tờ cho những người dân này để họ có dịp được về thăm quê_hương " .
</s>
<s> Ngay sau đó một cuộc họp về việc cấp quốc_tịch cho Việt_kiều đã được khẩn_trương tiến_hành với sự có_mặt của các tỉnh_trưởng trong vùng đông bắc Thái .
</s>
<s> Chưa đầy ba tuần sau , ngày 12 - 3 - 2004 tại hội_trường Trường Đại_học Sư_phạm tỉnh Nakhon_Phanom , đại_diện chính_quyền Thái_Lan , Thứ_trưởng Bộ Nội_vụ Pramuan_Ruchanaserre đã trao quốc_tịch cho 572 người Việt thuộc thế_hệ sinh_trưởng ở Thái hiện đang cư_trú tại các tỉnh vùng đông bắc Thái .
</s>
<s> Tại buổi lễ này đại_diện chính_quyền cũng cho biết sẽ có những đợt trao quốc_tịch tiếp để giải_quyết dứt_điểm hàng ngàn hồ_sơ xin cấp quốc_tịch Thái_Lan của người Việt đã nộp cơ_quan_chức_năng .
</s>
<s> Khi chúng_tôi đến thăm làng Hữu_nghị Việt - Thái ở bản Nachock , nhiều người dân vẫn còn náo_nức nhớ lại phút_giây hạnh_phúc khi thấy cờ Tổ_quốc và cờ Thái_Lan treo rợp đường Nakhon_Phanom , chưa bao_giờ họ tự_hào và hãnh_diện như thế khi thủ_tướng hai nước cắt băng khánh_thành ngôi làng hữu_nghị .
</s>
<s> Từ giờ_phút ấy , nhất_là sau lời hứa của Thủ_tướng Thaksin_Shinawatra với vấn_đề cấp quốc_tịch , đường về thăm cố_hương của những người Việt cao_niên không còn quá xa_vời .
</s>
<s> Mưu_sinh dưới đáy biển .
</s>
<s> Đối_với họ đáy biển là một nguồn sống thiết_thân .
</s>
<s> Nay biển cửa Sót cạn " hàng " , họ rủ nhau sang lặn ở biển cửa Lò , Quỳnh_Lưu LBKT Nghệ_An RBKT , biển Thanh_Hóa , Quảng_Ninh , đảo Thanh_Lân thuộc vùng đảo Cô_Tô .
</s>
<s> Khi biển phía Bắc hết mùa nắng ấm , họ di_chuyển vào biển Phan_Thiết LBKT Bình_Thuận RBKT , Ninh_Thuận , Bình_Tuy , đảo Phú_Quốc lặn thuê kiếm sống .
</s>
<s> Xưa lặn bộ nay lặn máy .
</s>
<s> Trong hơn 100 thợ lặn , chiếm quá nửa tổng_số thanh_niên trai_tráng của làng Xuân_Hòa , xã Thạch_Bằng LBKT Hà_Tĩnh RBKT có đến 40 người lặn có " bằng " .
</s>
<s> Họ tự_hào " con_trai Xuân_Hòa đẻ ra là biết lặn , biết bơi " .
</s>
<s> Tự_hào hơn khi họ kể chuyện ông Thú_Đỉnh - sư_phụ nghề lặn của làng - từng lặn bộ dưới biển cửa Sót sâu hàng chục mét để tháo cái chân_vịt của tàu_chiến Pháp đem về làm kỷ_niệm hồi năm_1953 .
</s>
<s> Có lần tàu biệt_kích Pháp chở súng_đạn định đổ_bộ lên vùng_biển Thạch_Bằng do va phải đá ngầm bị chìm ngoài cửa Sót , ông Đỉnh lại được dân_quân xã cử đi lặn lấy mấy chục khẩu súng_cối trong đêm khuya .
</s>
<s> Năm nay đã gần 80 tuổi , tai có hơi lãng đôi_chút nhưng ông Đỉnh vẫn chưa quên chuyện lặn .
</s>
<s> Ông nói : " Ngày_xưa chúng_tôi lặn bộ bắt con vẹm , hến cơm là hết .
</s>
<s> Lặn quanh_năm_suốt_tháng nhưng nhà vẫn nghèo vì lặn bộ không hết khả_năng của mình , với_lại hồi đó chưa có phong_trào ăn hải_sản như bây_giờ .
</s>
<s> Nay thanh_niên toàn lặn máy nên họ giàu lên là phải " .
</s>
<s> Kể chuyện lặn máy , hội thợ lặn gồm những con " rái_cá " nổi_tiếng như Khắc_Hùng , Công_Hòa , Khắc_Chiêng , Hữu_Huấn , Văn_Tưởng , Ngọc_Bích đều nhắc đến ông thầy Khánh từ Quảng_Ngãi ra bày nghề .
</s>
<s> Khi từ Quảng_Ngãi vượt biển đến Thạch_Bằng mua hàng , những thương_gia hải_sản đã phát_hiện Xuân_Hòa là một làng có truyền_thống lặn bộ nổi_tiếng .
</s>
<s> Thế_là họ tính bài truyền nghề lặn máy cho thanh_niên trong làng và tạo_lập " vệ_tinh " để khi cần họ thuê đi lặn .
</s>
<s> Vì_thế suốt dọc dài vùng_biển phía bắc miền Trung có bao_nhiêu làng biển , nhưng chỉ có mỗi làng Xuân_Hòa thạo nghề và trở_thành " đội quân thiện_chiến " .
</s>
<s> Nơi đây tóc của thợ lặn nào cũng vàng_hoe như tóc nhuộm và mắt của họ thì vàng lơ như mắt tây .
</s>
<s> Dưới đáy biển .
</s>
<s> Ngày 18 - 10 , sau một cuộc rượu trưa tôi theo hội Văn , Tưởng đi lặn ngoài đảo Mắt .
</s>
<s> Ngư_trường cách bờ 15 hải_lý , sâu chừng 20 sải LBKT tương_đương 30 m RBKT .
</s>
<s> Khi lặn , mỗi người ngậm phía đầu một cái vòi có chiều dài 100 - 150 m .
</s>
<s> Vòi này được nối qua cái đai chì đeo quanh người LBKT trước_đây lặn bộ thì đeo đá để có đủ độ nặng giữ người dưới biển RBKT và nối_liền với bình dưỡng_khí được vận_hành nhờ máy thủy LBKT máy_nổ vừa đưa thuyền đi vừa cung_cấp hơi cho máy nén khí đưa hơi vào bình dưỡng_khí RBKT .
</s>
<s> Thoáng chốc cả sáu thợ lặn đã chìm vào đáy biển .
</s>
<s> Trên con thuyền tròng_trành sóng liên_hồi đập_đi_đập_lại chỉ còn chú lơ thuyền và tôi .
</s>
<s> Chú lơ tên Hải đứng gác thuyền , gác máy .
</s>
<s> Nhiệm_vụ quan_trọng nhất của chú là không để thuyền người khác đi qua vùng lặn kéo theo những dây nhựa đang nổi bồng_bềnh trên mặt_biển đang nối_liền với miệng của thợ lặn để cung_cấp khí thở ; gỡ các dây khi sóng biển làm rối vào nhau và đổ nước mát cho các máy trên thuyền đủ sức chạy trong nhiều giờ liền .
</s>
<s> Là một thợ lặn trẻ biết hết mọi chuyện mưu_sinh dưới biển , Hải kể : " Dưới đáy biển , thợ lặn phai dùng một cái dùi bằng sắt hoặc con dao nhọn để cạy những con ngao , con sò bám rất chắc vào hang đá .
</s>
<s> Nơi không có bãi đá , thợ phải có đôi mắt thật tinh để có_thể phát_hiện những " mánh " của con hàng .
</s>
<s> Đó là khi làn cát tự_nhiên bị sụt xuống do ngao , sò đang di_chuyển dưới cát .
</s>
<s> Khi ấy chỉ cần dùng bàn_tay cào cát hoặc luồn sâu vào cát là bắt được " .
</s>
<s> Có khi nào gặp rắn biển không ? - tôi hỏi .
</s>
<s> Gặp thường .
</s>
<s> Nhưng gặp rắn thì bắt rắn .
</s>
<s> Nhiều chuyến thợ lặn còn lừa tôm_hùm , mực nang vào hang và quần cả những con cá_mú nặng 30 kg cho mệt_lử rồi vây lưới bắt ngon_ơ nữa kìa ...
</s>
<s> Sá gì , mặc cho giữa biển lạnh buốt .
</s>
<s> Tất_nhiên những lúc ấy họ chỉ lặn khoảng một giờ rồi lên nghỉ một chặp , sau đó lặn tiếp .
</s>
<s> Thợ lặn không sợ lạnh , chỉ sợ nhất đang lặn thì gặp biển nổi bão , dông , gió .
</s>
<s> Bước nhảy từ lặn bộ sang lặn máy đã giúp những hội thợ lặn làng Xuân_Hòa có điều_kiện chinh_phục những vùng_biển xa , rộng_lớn hơn .
</s>
<s> Nhưng công_cuộc mưu_sinh dưới đáy biển không phải lúc_nào cũng thuận_buồm_xuôi_gió .
</s>
<s> Trong làng lặn , anh_em đã phải lặng_lẽ mang những cái tang ...
</s>
<s> Đầu_tiên là Cường - một thợ trẻ .
</s>
<s> Cường chết trong tư_thế đang đeo đá vào người để tập lặn .
</s>
<s> Khi nhảy xuống , vòi nối miệng với máy dưỡng_khí bị bật ra .
</s>
<s> Sau 30 phút không thấy động_tĩnh , người trên thuyền kéo vòi lên thì Cường đã chết .
</s>
<s> Kế đến là anh Hồ , 37 tuổi , cùng bảy người khác đi lặn thuê trong biển Phan_Thiết .
</s>
<s> Đang lặn thì máy nén khí bị hỏng .
</s>
<s> Năm phút sau thấy bay thợ nổi lên nhưng anh Hồ lặn sâu quá 30 m , không ai thấy .
</s>
<s> Anh_em lại lặn xuống tìm , nhưng ...
</s>
<s> Ba hôm sau xác anh Hồ nổi lên trong bộ_đồ nhái .
</s>
<s> Mới_đây biển Thanh_Hóa rộ sò , có thợ lặn được hơn 1_triệu đồng / ngày .
</s>
<s> Thấy thế mấy người xã Thịnh_Lộc , huyện Can_Lộc sang mượn thuyền người Xuân_Hòa đi lặn .
</s>
<s> Do lặn không quen , gặp máy bị trục_trặc người trên thuyền không kịp sửa nên hai thợ lặn chết chìm dưới biển .
</s>
<s> Tôi bấm đồng_hồ đến giờ thứ ba rồi mà vẫn chưa thấy thợ lặn nào ngoi lên .
</s>
<s> Hải bảo còn đúng một giờ nữa .
</s>
<s> Dân thợ lặn tuy không có ai đeo đồng_hồ nhưng đến giờ là họ biết , nếu_không làm_sao đi lặn thuê được .
</s>
<s> Đúng tầm đủ bốn giờ Hải đứng dậy thông_báo : " Họ đang lên đấy " .
</s>
<s> Quả_thật , cả sáu người thợ lần_lượt hiện lên như những con nhái biển .
</s>
<s> Người nào cũng mang một túi lưới đầy chặt những ngao , sò_huyết , hến đỏ , cua_đá , tôm_hùm .
</s>
<s> Lên thuyền vừa_mới cất kính bảo_hiểm mắt đã thè lưỡi cười hả_hê .
</s>
<s> Tôi hỏi : " Có lặn tiếp được không ? " .
</s>
